# math.OA [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Quantum Graph Theory by Example](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23651)
*Gian Luca Spitzer,Ion Nechita*

Main category: math.OA

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个参数化量子图（quantum graphs）家族，通过矩阵三元组(A, B, C)描述，揭示了量子图结构可分解为经典成分（由"奇怪图"表示）和纯量子成分。基于此模型，作者为量子图参数（如连通分量数、色数等）提供了精确公式或界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子图理论面临的主要挑战在于量子图不再是离散对象，这导致难以构建具有启发性的非平凡示例。现有研究缺乏能够解析计算标准图参数的大型参数化量子图家族。

Method: 作者构建了一类可离散化思考的量子图，采用Musto、Reutter和Verdon引入的图形式化表示。这些示例源于经典矩阵群作用下的量子图，通过矩阵三元组(A, B, C)参数化，其中A和C由称为"奇怪图"的经典加权图描述，B提供纯量子贡献。

Result: 该参数化揭示了量子图结构的清晰分解：经典成分（奇怪图）和纯量子成分（无经典对应物）。基于此模型，作者为量子图参数（如连通分量数、色数、独立数和团数）提供了精确公式或建立了界限。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了首个能够解析计算标准图参数的大型参数化量子图家族，为量子图理论的发展提供了重要的示例资源和分析工具。

Abstract: Quantum graphs have been introduced by Duan, Severini, and Winter to describe the zero-error behaviour of quantum channels. Since then, quantum graph theory has become a field of study in its own right. A substantial source of difficulty in working with quantum graphs compared to classical graphs stems from the fact that they are no longer discrete objects. This makes it generally difficult to construct insightful, non-trivial examples. We present a collection of non-trivial quantum graphs that can be thought of in discrete terms, and that can be expressed in the diagrammatic formalism introduced by Musto, Reutter, and Verdon. The examples arise as the quantum graphs acted on by increasingly smaller classical matrix groups, and are parametrised by triples of matrices $(A, B, C)$. The parametrisation reveals a clean decomposition of quantum graph structure into classical and genuinely quantum components: $A$ and $C$ are described by a classical weighted graph called the strange graph, while $B$ provides a purely quantum contribution with no classical analogue. Based on this model, we give exact formulas or establish bounds for quantum graph parameters, such as the number of connected components, the chromatic number, the independence number, and the clique number. Our results provide the first large, parametric families of quantum graphs for which standard graph parameters can be computed analytically.

</details>

# math.DG [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Comparison theory for Lipschitz spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24195)
*Mathias Braun,Marta Sálamo Candal*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文证明了具有局部Lipschitz连续度量和类时分布Ricci曲率下界的全局双曲时空满足类时测度收缩性质，并推导出一系列几何比较定理和不等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究低正则性时空的几何性质，特别是处理具有局部Lipschitz连续度量和分布曲率的时空，这类时空包括脉冲引力波、薄壳和匹配时空等重要物理模型。

Method: 采用测度收缩性质（measure contraction property）的框架，结合凸几何中的定位技术，将黎曼几何中的比较定理推广到洛伦兹几何（Lorentzian geometry）中。

Result: 证明了全局双曲时空在给定条件下满足类时测度收缩性质，并获得了d'Alembert比较定理、类时Brunn-Minkowski不等式、类时Bishop-Gromov不等式等一系列尖锐形式的比较结果。

Conclusion: 该研究为低正则性时空建立了系统的几何比较理论，将黎曼几何中的经典结果成功推广到洛伦兹几何框架，解决了Petersen-Sprouse和Aubry近30年前预期的理论过渡问题。

Abstract: We prove a globally hyperbolic spacetime with locally Lipschitz continuous metric and timelike distributional Ricci curvature bounded from below obeys the timelike measure contraction property. The remarkable class of examples of spacetimes that are covered by this result includes impulsive gravity waves, thin shells, and matched spacetimes.
  As applications, we get new comparison theorems for Lipschitz spacetimes in sharp form: d'Alembert, timelike Brunn-Minkowski, and timelike Bishop-Gromov. Under appropriate nonbranching assumptions (conjectured to hold in even lower regularity), our results also yield the timelike curvature-dimension condition, a volume incompleteness theorem, as well as exact representation formulas and sharp comparison estimates for d'Alembertians of Lorentz distance functions from general spacelike submanifolds.
  Moreover, we establish the sharp timelike Bonnet--Myers inequality ad hoc using the localization technique from convex geometry. Alongside, we prove a timelike diameter estimate for spacetimes whose timelike Ricci curvature is positive up to a "small" deviation (in an $L^p$-sense). This adapts prior theorems for Riemannian manifolds by Petersen-Sprouse and Aubry to Lorentzian geometry, a transition the former two anticipated almost 30 years ago.

</details>


### [3] [Regularization of singular time-dependent Lagrangian systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24308)
*Manuel De León,Rubén Izquierdo-López,Luca Schiavone,Pablo Soto*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了奇异拉格朗日系统（singular Lagrangian system）的正则化方法，基于余迷向嵌入定理（coisotropic embedding theorem），利用Tulczyjew同构和几乎积结构（almost product structures）提供了替代方法，并证明了拉格朗日正则化的一阶唯一性，同时将方法扩展到时间依赖的奇异拉格朗日系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究奇异拉格朗日系统动力学的一种方法是尝试将其正则化（regularize），即找到一个等价的正则系统。对于时间无关的奇异拉格朗日系统，已有基于余迷向嵌入定理的方法，本文旨在重新审视这些结果并提供替代方法。

Method: 本文基于余迷向嵌入定理，采用Tulczyjew同构和几乎积结构（almost product structures）来构建替代的正则化方法。这种方法允许对原有构造进行轻微推广，并扩展到时间依赖的奇异拉格朗日系统。

Result: 证明了拉格朗日正则化的一阶唯一性（uniqueness of the Lagrangian regularization to first order）。同时，成功将方法论扩展到时间依赖的奇异拉格朗日系统（time-dependent singular Lagrangians）情况。

Conclusion: 本文提供了基于余迷向嵌入定理、Tulczyjew同构和几乎积结构的替代正则化方法，该方法不仅推广了原有构造，证明了正则化的一阶唯一性，还成功扩展到时间依赖的奇异拉格朗日系统。

Abstract: One approach to studying the dynamics of a singular Lagrangian system is to attempt to regularize it, that is, to find an equivalent and regular system. In the case of time-independent singular Lagrangians, an approach due to \textit{A. Ibort} and \textit{J. Marín-Solano} is to use the coisotropic embedding theorem proved by \textit{M.J. Gotay} which states that any pre-symplectic manifold can be coisotropically embedded in a symplectic manifold. In this paper, we revisit these results and provide an alternative approach, also based on the coisotropic embedding theorem, that employs the Tulczyjew isomorphism and almost product structures, and allows for a slight generalization of the construction. In this revision, we also prove uniqueness of the Lagrangian regularization to first order. Furthermore, we extend our methodology to the case of time-dependent singular Lagrangians.

</details>

# cond-mat.mtrl-sci [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Proton-Transfer Ferroelectrics with Exceptional Switching Endurance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23764)
*Bibek Tiwari,Yuanyuan Ni,Xiaoshan Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究展示了通过低温沉积约束结晶（LDRC）技术制备的2-甲基苯并咪唑（MBI）薄膜在铁电存储器应用中具有卓越的抗疲劳性能，在10^8次循环后仍保持稳定的剩余极化，为无氟有机铁电器件提供了简单可靠的平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可靠的有机铁电材料在存储器应用中需要承受重复电学开关操作下的极端耐久性。当前聚合物铁电材料如P(VDF-TrFE)通常需要界面工程才能获得可比性能，因此需要寻找更简单、无需工程化结构的解决方案。

Method: 采用低温沉积后约束结晶（low-temperature deposition followed by restrained crystallization, LDRC）方法制备高度结晶的2-甲基苯并咪唑（2-methylbenzimidazole, MBI）薄膜，构建简单的Pt/MBI/Pt电容器结构。使用Kolmogorov-Avrami-Ishibashi（KAI）模型分析开关动力学，并设计了严格的疲劳测试协议，包括在约2倍矫顽场（2Ec）下使用5毫秒脉冲进行双极开关操作。

Result: MBI薄膜表现出毫秒级特征开关时间和沿氢键链的质子转移相关的准一维畴生长。在连续运行约2周的疲劳测试中，剩余极化仅在前10^4次循环中表现出轻微唤醒效应（+10%），在10^8次循环后最终恢复到接近初始值，测试受限于实验持续时间而非器件失效。

Conclusion: LDRC实现的高结晶度与局域质子转移开关机制相结合，在极化反转期间引入最小的结构扰动，从而实现了出色的抗疲劳耐受性。MBI作为一种简单、无氟的平台，为耐用的有机铁电器件提供了有前景的解决方案。

Abstract: Reliable organic ferroelectrics for memory applications require extreme endurance under repeated electrical switching. Here we demonstrate exceptional fatigue resistance in highly crystalline 2-methylbenzimidazole (MBI) films grown by low-temperature deposition followed by restrained crystallization (LDRC) in a simple Pt/MBI/Pt capacitor geometry. Switching kinetics analyzed using the Kolmogorov-Avrami-Ishibashi (KAI) model reveal characteristic millisecond switching times and quasi-one-dimensional domain growth associated with proton transfer along hydrogen-bond chains. Guided by these kinetics, we implemented a stringent fatigue protocol designed to maximize switching stress, involving bipolar switching at approximately 2Ec with 5 ms pulses, well beyond the characteristic switching time, for continuous operation over approximately 2 weeks. The remanent polarization exhibits only a minor wake-up (+10% within the first 10^4 cycles) and ultimately returns to approximately its initial value after 10^8 cycles, with testing limited by experimental duration rather than device failure. This robust endurance is achieved in an unengineered structure and contrasts with polymer ferroelectrics such as P(VDF-TrFE), where comparable performance typically relies on interfacial engineering. The combination of LDRC-enabled high crystallinity and localized proton-transfer switching, which introduces minimal structural perturbation during polarization reversal, enables this outstanding fatigue tolerance and highlights MBI as a simple, fluorine-free platform for durable organic ferroelectric devices.

</details>


### [5] [Coupling of phase transition, anharmonicity, and thermal transport in CaSnF$_6$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23851)
*Daxue Hao,Hao Huang,Geng Li,Yu Wu,Shuming Zeng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究结合第一性原理计算与机器学习神经进化势能，揭示了CaSnF₆中结构相变与热输运的耦合机制，发现负热膨胀源于低能刚性单元模式，而强非谐性主导的热导率在相变附近呈现非单调异常行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解结构相变与热输运之间的耦合对于设计具有可调性质的功能材料至关重要。本研究旨在探索这种相互作用在CaSnF₆中的具体表现。

Method: 研究结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）与机器学习神经进化势能（machine-learned neuroevolution potential），实现了大尺度分子动力学模拟（large-scale molecular dynamics simulations）跨越宽温度范围。非平衡模拟（non-equilibrium simulations）用于揭示热导率异常。

Result: 模拟准确捕捉到一级结构相变（first-order structural phase transition）及相关晶格动力学。负热膨胀（negative thermal expansion）源于涉及角共享[CaF₆]⁴⁻八面体协同旋转的低能刚性单元模式（rigid unit modes）。强非谐性（strong anharmonicity）主要由四声子散射（four-phonon scattering）主导，抑制晶格热导率（κ_L）。相变附近κ_L呈现显著非单调异常，偏离传统的∼1/T^α行为。

Conclusion: 研究建立了连接晶格几何、非谐振动动力学与热输运的统一机制，并突显了机器学习势能在桥接原子尺度相变与宏观输运性质方面的潜力。

Abstract: Understanding the coupling between structural phase transitions and thermal transport is essential for designing functional materials with tunable properties. Here, we investigate this interplay in CaSnF$_6$ by combining first-principles calculations with a machine-learned neuroevolution potential that enables large-scale molecular dynamics simulations across a wide temperature range. The simulations accurately capture the first-order structural phase transition and associated lattice dynamics. We show that the negative thermal expansion originates from low-energy rigid unit modes involving cooperative rotations of corner-sharing [CaF$_6$]$^{4-}$ octahedra, which induce bond-angle bending and volume contraction. At the same time, strong anharmonicity, dominated by four-phonon scattering, plays a central role in suppressing lattice thermal conductivity ($κ_L$). Crucially, non-equilibrium simulations reveal a pronounced non-monotonic anomaly in $κ_L$ near the phase transition, deviating from the conventional $\sim 1/T^α$ behavior and providing direct transport evidence of lattice reconstruction. These results establish a unified mechanism linking lattice geometry, anharmonic vibrational dynamics, and thermal transport, and highlight the potential of machine-learned potentials for bridging atomic-scale phase transitions with macroscopic transport properties.

</details>


### [6] [An Efficient High-Degree, High-Order Equivariant Graph Neural Network for Direct Crystal Structure Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23941)
*Ziduo Yang,Wei Zhuo,Huiqiang Xie,Xiaoqing Liu,Lei Shen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: E³Relax-H²是一种端到端的高阶高次等变图神经网络，将初始晶体直接映射到其弛豫结构，通过将原子和晶格向量统一表示为图节点，解决了现有机器学习方法在晶体结构优化中的三个关键限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密度泛函理论（DFT）进行晶体结构优化计算成本高昂，现有机器学习方法面临三个关键限制：大多数模型仅处理原子而隐含处理晶格向量；缺乏同时捕获高阶角信息和高阶几何关联的有效机制；许多流程是多阶段而非真正端到端，容易导致误差累积。

Method: 提出E³Relax-H²模型，将原子和晶格向量都提升为图节点，实现结构自由度的统一对称一致表示。引入两个消息传递机制：高阶高次消息传递模块捕获高阶角表示和高阶多体关联；晶格-原子消息传递模块显式建模晶格变形与原子位移的双向耦合。还提出了针对周期性边界条件下单次结构预测的可微周期性感知笛卡尔位移损失函数。

Result: 该方法实现了端到端的高阶高次等变图神经网络，能够将初始晶体结构直接映射到其弛豫结构，通过统一表示原子和晶格向量，同时捕获高阶几何信息，避免了多阶段流程的误差累积问题。

Conclusion: E³Relax-H²通过将原子和晶格向量统一表示为图节点，结合高阶高次消息传递机制，提供了一种真正端到端的晶体结构优化方法，克服了现有机器学习方法在晶格处理、高阶信息捕获和流程集成方面的局限性。

Abstract: Crystal structure optimization is fundamental to materials modeling but remains computationally expensive when performed with density-functional theory (DFT). Machine-learning (ML) approaches offer substantial acceleration, yet existing methods face three key limitations: (i) most models operate solely on atoms and treat lattice vectors implicitly, despite their central role in structural optimization; (ii) they lack efficient mechanisms to capture high-degree angular information and higher-order geometric correlations simultaneously, which are essential for distinguishing subtle structural differences; and (iii) many pipelines are multi-stage or iterative rather than truly end-to-end, making them prone to error accumulation and limiting scalability. Here we present E$^{3}$Relax-H$^{2}$, an end-to-end high-degree, high-order equivariant graph neural network that maps an initial crystal directly to its relaxed structure. The key idea is to promote both atoms and lattice vectors to graph nodes, enabling a unified and symmetry-consistent representation of structural degrees of freedom. Building on this formulation, E$^{3}$Relax-H$^{2}$ introduces two message-passing mechanisms: (i) a high-degree, high-order message-passing module that efficiently captures high-degree angular representations and high-order many-body correlations; and (ii) a lattice-atom message-passing module that explicitly models the bidirectional coupling between lattice deformation and atomic displacement. In addition, we propose a differentiable periodicity-aware Cartesian displacement loss tailored for one-shot structure prediction under periodic boundary conditions.

</details>


### [7] [ChargeFlow: Flow-Matching Refinement of Charge-Conditioned Electron Densities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23943)
*Tri Minh Nguyen,Sherif Abdulkader Tawfik,Truyen Tran,Svetha Venkatesh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: ChargeFlow是一种基于流匹配（flow matching）的电荷密度精炼模型，通过3D U-Net速度场将原子密度叠加转换为DFT电子密度，显著提高了非局域电荷重分布和电荷态外推问题的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确计算电荷密度是电子结构理论的核心，但使用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算电荷态依赖的密度对于大规模筛选和缺陷工作流程仍然过于昂贵。需要开发更高效的方法来预测带电材料的电子密度。

Method: 提出ChargeFlow模型，采用流匹配（flow matching）精炼方法，通过3D U-Net速度场将电荷条件化的原子密度叠加转换为对应的DFT电子密度。模型在9,502个带电Materials Project计算数据上进行训练。

Result: 在包含钙钛矿、带电缺陷、金刚石缺陷、金属有机框架和有机晶体的1,671个外部基准结构上评估，ChargeFlow在非局域电荷重分布和电荷态外推问题上表现最强。变形密度误差从3.62%降至3.21%，电荷响应余弦相似度从0.571提升至0.655（相对于ResNet基线）。

Conclusion: 预测的密度在下游分析中保持化学实用性，成功在所有1,671个基准结构上实现Bader分割，并产生高保真静电势。流匹配被定位为带电材料密度精炼的实用策略。

Abstract: Accurate charge densities are central to electronic-structure theory, but computing charge-state-dependent densities with density functional theory remains too expensive for large-scale screening and defect workflows. We present ChargeFlow, a flow-matching refinement model that transforms a charge-conditioned superposition of atomic densities into the corresponding DFT electron density on the native periodic real-space grid using a 3D U-Net velocity field. Trained on 9,502 charged Materials Project-derived calculations and evaluated on an external 1,671-structure benchmark spanning perovskites, charged defects, diamond defects, metal-organic frameworks, and organic crystals, ChargeFlow is not uniformly best on every in-distribution class but is strongest on problems dominated by nonlocal charge redistribution and charge-state extrapolation, improving deformation-density error from 3.62% to 3.21% and charge- response cosine similarity from 0.571 to 0.655 relative to a ResNet baseline. The predicted densities remain chemically useful under downstream analysis, yielding successful Bader partitioning on all 1,671 benchmark structures and high-fidelity electrostatic potentials, which positions flow matching as a practical density-refinement strategy for charged materials.

</details>


### [8] [Fundamentals and applications of aberration corrected high resolution transmission electron microscopy in materials science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23958)
*Ranjan Datta,Sneha Kobri M.,Sudip Mahato*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文综述了像差校正相位衬度透射电子显微镜（aberration-corrected phase contrast TEM）在原子尺度材料结构表征中的基本原理和应用，涵盖像差校正技术、直接图像解释方法，并与竞争性原子分辨率相位衬度技术进行比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在系统介绍像差校正相位衬度透射电子显微镜的基本原理，该技术能够在原子长度尺度上表征材料的原子排列和电子结构信息，为材料科学研究提供关键的结构表征工具。

Conclusion: 随着仪器设备和记录装置的巨大进步，这些工具和方法在解决具有挑战性的材料科学问题方面具有广阔的未来前景，为原子尺度材料表征提供了强大的技术平台。

Abstract: In this review article fundamentals of aberration corrected phase contrast transmission electron microscopy for the structural characterization of materials at atomic length scale is presented. The word structure entails atomic arrangement as well as electronic structure information of the materials. The article summarily covers a range of topics on the basics of aberrations, aberration correctors, direct image interpretation with negative Cs phase contrast microscopy, a discussion in comparison with the competitive atomic resolution phase contrast methods for example, off-axis electron holography, electron ptychography, differential phase contrast microscopy. With the tremendous advancement in instrumentation and recording devices, potential future perspective of such tools and methods in solving challenging materials science problems are outlined.

Abstract: Epitaxial heterostructures of two-dimensional van der Waals magnets and topological insulators offer a powerful platform for probing interfacial spin interactions that govern magnetic textures in low-dimensional quantum systems, while simultaneously enabling highly efficient, atomically thin spin-orbit-torque memory and computing architectures. Together, our results offer a new strategy for phase-selective control of magnetic domains through interfacial engineering.

  <summary>Details</summary>

As the model was trained exclusively under constant thermal conditions, it cannot account for the thermal history dependence of grain boundary kinetics, fundamentally limiting its applicability to the time-varying thermal profiles characteristic of industrial heat treatment processes. This study extends the previous framework by incorporating Feature-wise Linear Modulation (FiLM) for thermal conditioning to predict grain growth under complex, time-varying thermal profiles. The model was trained on a large dataset of grain growth evolution under thermal profiles with heating and cooling rates ranging from 0.01 kelvin per second to 10 kelvin per second. The results demonstrate that the proposed thermal conditioning mechanism enables the model to capture the influence of variable thermal profiles on grain boundary migration kinetics.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Quantum-electrodynamical density-functional theory (QEDFT) provides a first-principles framework for describing materials coupled to quantized electromagnetic fields. While QEDFT has successfully captured cavity-induced modifications of electronic structures in atoms and molecules, a fully self-consistent and accurate framework to simulate and predict the structural, phonon-related, polarization and optical response of periodic solids in optical cavities has remained elusive. Here, we introduce a unified QEDFT approach that incorporates collective light-matter coupling in the electronic ground state, density functional perturbation theory for phonons, and real-time time-dependent QEDFT for optical excitations. This framework enables \textit{ab initio} calculations of cavity-modified electronic and phononic dispersions, Born effective charges, dielectric tensors, and both resonant and non-resonant optical absorption spectra. Using wurtzite \ac{GaN} in an optical cavity as a case study, we demonstrate that the quantized vacuum field reshapes electronic, phononic and polarization properties, producing experimentally accessible signatures in the transmission and absorption spectra. These results establish QEDFT as a general first-principles platform for predicting and exploring cavity-modified quantum materials.

### [13] [On the configurational force associated with blocked slip bands at grain boundaries in α-Ti](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24129)
*Abdalrhaman Koko*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶界（grain boundaries）能够阻碍滑移带传播并产生强烈的局部应力和应变场，影响多晶金属的后续变形和损伤起始。传统几何判据（如施密德因子和滑移传递参数）仅描述晶体学相容性，无法量化受阻滑移事件的能量严重性。

Method: 应用构型力（configurational force）框架于商业纯钛中受阻滑移带的高角分辨率电子背散射衍射（HR-EBSD）测量数据。通过从测量的弹性场评估J型等效域积分（J-type equivalent domain integral），量化与应力局部化相关的局部能量驱动力的强度和方向依赖性。

Result: 结果显示传统几何度量与构型力响应之间存在显著解耦，表明局部应力集中几何形状强烈影响相邻晶粒中哪些晶体学上允许的扩展方向在能量上更有利。该框架提供了量化受阻滑移严重性的物理基础。

Conclusion: 构型力框架为量化受阻滑移严重性提供了物理基础，并激励未来原位研究以定义滑移传递或开裂的临界传递阈值（critical transfer threshold）。该方法能够评估变形向相邻晶粒扩展的能量倾向。

Abstract: Grain boundaries can block slip-band propagation and generate intense local stress and strain fields that influence subsequent deformation and damage initiation in polycrystalline metals. Conventional geometric criteria, such as Schmid factor and slip-transfer parameters, describe crystallographic compatibility but do not quantify the energetic severity of a blocked slip event. Here, we apply a configurational force framework to high-angular-resolution electron backscatter diffraction (HR-EBSD) measurements obtained from a blocked slip band in commercially pure titanium. By evaluating a J-type equivalent domain integral from the measured elastic field, we quantify both the magnitude and directional dependence of the local energetic driving force associated with the stress localisation; thus, providing an energetic descriptor of the tendency for deformation to extend into the neighbouring grain. The results show a marked decoupling between conventional geometric metrics and the configurational force response, indicating that the local stress-localisation geometry strongly influences which crystallographically admissible extension directions in the neighbouring grain are energetically favoured. The framework provides a physically grounded basis for quantifying blocked-slip severity and for motivating future in situ studies aimed at defining a critical transfer threshold for transfer or cracking.

### [14] [When Trace Water Dominates: Hydration-Mediated Dielectric and Transport Behaviour in BiFeO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24145)
*Subir Majumder,Gilad Orr,Paul Ben-Ishai*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 微量水（<1 wt%）可显著改变多孔BiFeO₃陶瓷的介电响应，导致异常大的介电强度（Δε≈10⁴-10⁵）和非阿伦尼乌斯（non-Arrhenius）弛豫行为，这些效应在脱水后消失，表明受限水对介电异常有重要外源贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管微量水能深刻改变功能氧化物的介电响应，但在广泛报道巨介电行为的体系中，这种效应尚未得到充分认识。本研究旨在探究亚百分比水合（<1 wt%）对多孔BiFeO₃陶瓷的介电弛豫、电荷传输和界面极化特性的影响。

Method: 采用宽频介电谱（broadband dielectric spectroscopy）分析水合与脱水状态下多孔BiFeO₃陶瓷的介电行为。通过与层状粘土矿物的水合控制介电响应进行比较，评估受限水在晶界、孔表面和内部界面的有效性。

Result: 水合状态下观察到主导弛豫过程，其特征为异常大的介电强度（Δε≈10⁴-10⁵）和明显的鞍点偏离阿伦尼乌斯（Arrhenius）动力学，表明多孔氧化物系统中存在非阿伦尼乌斯弛豫行为。这些特征仅在水合状态出现，脱水后消失，而控制热激活弛豫时间尺度的本征激活势垒保持可比性。

Conclusion: 微量受限水对多孔氧化物陶瓷的介电和传输异常有重要外源贡献。脱水控制介电循环为重新评估功能氧化物材料中的巨介电响应、麦克斯韦-瓦格纳型（Maxwell-Wagner-type）效应和水合诱导现象提供了实用的诊断框架。

Abstract: Traces of water can profoundly alter the dielectric response of functional oxides, yet such effects have remained largely unrecognized in systems where colossal dielectric behaviour has been widely reported. Here, we investigate the impact of sub-percent hydration ($<$1 wt\%) on the dielectric relaxation, charge transport, and interfacial polarization properties of porous BiFeO$_3$ ceramics. Broadband dielectric spectroscopy reveals, in the hydrated state, a dominant relaxation process characterized by an anomalously large dielectric strength ($Δ\varepsilon \approx$ 10$^4$-10$^5$) and a pronounced saddle-point deviation from Arrhenius dynamics, indicative of non-Arrhenius relaxation behaviour in a porous oxide system. These features appear only in the hydrated state and vanish upon dehydration, while the intrinsic activation barriers governing the thermally activated relaxation timescale remain comparable. Comparison with hydration-controlled dielectric responses in layered clay minerals shows that similar qualitative deviations can emerge in BiFeO$_3$ with nearly fifteen-fold lower water content, underscoring the effectiveness of confined water at grain boundaries, pore surfaces, and internal interfaces. Together, these results demonstrate that trace, confined water can make a major extrinsic contribution to dielectric and transport anomalies in porous oxide ceramics. The use of dehydration-controlled dielectric cycling provides a practical diagnostic framework for reassessing colossal dielectric responses, Maxwell-Wagner-type effects, and hydration-induced phenomena in functional oxide materials.

### [15] [The domain-wall/metal-electrode injection barrier in lithium niobate: Which electrical transport model fits best?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24178)
*Manuel Zahn,Elke Beyreuther,Iuliia Kiseleva,Julius Ratzenberger,Michael Rüsing,Lukas M. Eng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究重新审视了铌酸锂晶体中导电畴壁与金属电极界面的电学行为，将原有的"R2D2"等效电路模型推广为"R2X2"模型，并通过交流电流谐波分析确定福勒-诺德海姆隧穿机制最能解释界面特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全面描述铌酸锂单晶中导电畴壁的电输运特性及金属电极界面的电荷注入行为是一个复杂挑战。先前提出的"R2D2"等效电路模型虽能匹配直流I-V特性，但界面可能存在多种超越二极管相关电子跳跃传输的并发过程。

Method: 研究将"R2D2"模型推广为"R2X2"电路模型（X代表HT、TE、FNT、SCLC等不同传输机制）。同时采用高阶谐波畴壁电流贡献分析（HHCC），即交流I-V检测，以比纯直流I-V曲线拟合更高的精度区分不同理论模型。

Result: 交流与直流分析结果高度一致，最终发现福勒-诺德海姆隧穿（Fowler-Nordheim tunneling, FNT）模型最能解释所研究的畴壁/电极结特性。该方法成功区分了电子跳跃传输、热电子发射、福勒-诺德海姆隧穿和空间电荷限制传导等多种可能机制。

Conclusion: 通过推广等效电路模型并引入交流谐波分析技术，研究精确确定了铌酸锂导电畴壁界面电荷注入的主导机制为福勒-诺德海姆隧穿，为理解此类复杂界面电学行为提供了更精确的分析框架。

Abstract: The comprehensive description of both the electrical transport along conductive domain walls (CDWs) in lithium niobate (LNO) single crystals and the charge injection at the interfacing metal electrodes, emerged to be a complex challenge. Recently, a heuristic evaluation allowed to postulate the "R2D2" equivalent-circuit model (consisting of two parallel resistor-diode pairs) to appropriately match the DC current-voltage (I-V) characteristics. Here, we carefully revisit the interfacial electrical behavior, i.e., the diode part of the equivalent circuit model, since many more processes beyond the diode-related electron hopping transport (HT) assumed so far, may concurrently occur, such as thermionic emission (TE), Fowler-Nordheim tunneling (FNT), space-charge limited conduction (SCLC), and others more. The "R2D2" model thus needs to be generalized into an "R2X2" circuit model (with X = HT, TE, FNT, and others) to fit to the experimental data. Moreover, to double check for the best I-V curve fitting to the different theories, we apply a higher-harmonic DW current-contribution (HHCC) analysis, i.e., an AC I-V inspection, that allows us to discriminate between all these possible models with much higher precision than from pure DC I-V curve fitting. Both the AC and DC analysis reveal well consistent results, finally finding that the FNT model accounts best for the domain-wall/electrode junctions investigated here.

### [16] [Tunable intersublattice exchange coupling drives magnetic evolution in Mn$_{3+x}$Ga$_{1-x}$C ($0 \le x \le 0.60$)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24185)
*Dong-Hui Xu,Cong-Mian Zhen,Deng-Lu Hou,Li Ma,De-Wei Zhao,Guo-ke Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过Mn掺杂调控Mn₃GaC反钙钛矿的磁性和输运性质，发现随着Mn含量增加，系统经历从反铁磁态到倾斜铁磁态再到强铁磁态的连续转变，同时磁有序温度显著提升，拓扑霍尔电阻率在特定掺杂浓度达到峰值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Mn₃₊ₓGa₁₋ₓC反钙钛矿（antiperovskite）中Mn替代Ga位点对磁性和输运性质的影响，旨在理解晶格收缩如何抑制Mn₃GaC的反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）序，并探索磁态转变的微观机制。

Method: 通过实验合成Mn₃₊ₓGa₁₋ₓC（0 ≤ x ≤ 0.60）系列样品，测量其磁性和输运性质演化；结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析不同掺杂浓度下的磁矩排列和自旋构型。

Result: 随着x增加，系统磁基态经历从反铁磁态→倾斜铁磁态（canted ferrimagnetic state）→强铁磁态（robust ferrimagnetic state）的连续转变，磁有序温度显著提升。饱和磁矩在x=0.10时达到最大值3.63μ_B/f.u.，拓扑霍尔电阻率（topological Hall resistivity）在x=0.20时达到峰值1.47μΩ·cm。计算显示x=0.20时面心Mn磁矩倾斜约40°，表明存在自旋阻挫（spin frustration）。

Conclusion: 亚晶格间反铁磁耦合（intersublattice antferromagnetic coupling）主导了磁转变和涌现的输运现象，这为设计高有序温度反钙钛矿材料提供了微观基础。

Abstract: We investigate the magnetic and transport evolution in Mn$_{3+x}$Ga$_{1-x}$C ($0 \le x \le 0.60$), where Mn substitution at corner Ga sites induces lattice contraction and suppresses the antiferromagnetic order of Mn$_3$GaC. As $x$ increases, the magnetic ground state of the system undergoes a sequential transition from an antiferromagnetic state, via a canted ferrimagnetic state, to a robust ferrimagnetic state, accompanied by a surge in the magnetic ordering temperature. Saturation magnetic moments reaches a maximum of 3.63~$μ_{\mathrm{B}}$/f.u. at $x = 0.10$, whereas the topological Hall resistivity peaks at 1.47~$μΩ\cdot$cm for $x = 0.20$ before decreasing with further doping. First-principles calculations demonstrate a $\sim\!40^{\circ}$ canting of face-centered Mn moments at $x = 0.20$, signifying spin frustration, and an eventual antiparallel alignment of face-centered and corner-site Mn moments at higher $x$. These results reveal that intersublattice antiferromagnetic coupling governs the magnetic transformation and emergent transport phenomena, thus providing a microscopic foundation for designing high-ordering-temperature antiperovskites.

### [17] [First-principles high-throughput screening of ruthenium compounds for advanced interconnects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24194)

Method: 研究采用高通量筛选（high-throughput screening）方法，系统性地研究了包括二元、三元和四元系统在内的2106种钌基化合物。形成化合物提供了一种有效策略来设计新颖特性，扩展了纯金属约束之外的材料设计空间。

Conclusion: 钌基化合物作为铜的可行替代品，能够有效应对互连尺寸缩小带来的电阻率挑战，为下一代互连技术提供了有前景的材料解决方案。

Abstract: As interconnect dimensions continue to shrink, the industry-standard copper faces a critical increase in resistivity, presenting a significant hurdle to overall device performance. To overcome this limitation, this work investigates the potential of ruthenium (Ru)-based compounds, encompassing binary, ternary, and quaternary systems, as viable alternatives to copper (Cu). Ruthenium is regarded as a strong candidate, owing to its inherent advantages in reliability and more favorable resistivity scaling at reduced dimensions. Moreover, forming compounds offers an effective strategy to engineer novel properties, expanding the material design space beyond the constraints of pure metals. Utilizing a high-throughput screening methodology, we systematically investigated a broad spectrum of 2,106 Ru-based compounds to identify candidates with superior electronic transport and reliability characteristics. Consequently, we successfully identified a total of 61 promising candidates that exhibit excellent resistivity scaling behavior and enhanced reliability. These findings demonstrate that Ru-based compounds offer a viable pathway to overcome the scaling limitations of next-generation interconnects.

### [18] [Diffusion coefficients of multi-principal element alloys from first principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24228)
*Damien K. J. Lee,Anirudh Raju Natarajan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了嵌入局部簇展开（eLCE）方法，用于计算多主元合金（MPEAs）中的空位介导扩散系数，揭示了局部动力学势垒而非热力学因素主导扩散过程，并识别出具有反迟滞扩散特性的合金成分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多主元合金（multi-principal element alloys, MPEAs）中的空位介导扩散机制尚未被充分理解。现有计算方法因化学元素数量众多，难以将电子结构与宏观输运系数联系起来。

Method: 本文引入了嵌入局部簇展开（embedded local cluster expansion, eLCE）方法，该方法桥接了第一性原理计算与动力学蒙特卡洛模拟，用于计算多组分扩散系数矩阵。将该方法应用于V-Cr-Nb-Mo-Ta-W体系的难熔多主元合金。

Result: 研究发现，局部动力学势垒（local kinetic barriers）而非热力学或空位关联因子主要控制这些材料中的扩散过程。扩散是迟滞（sluggish）还是反迟滞（anti-sluggish）取决于平均空位迁移势垒相对于混合规则估计值以及快速扩散物种的渗透路径可用性。通过筛选六元成分空间，识别出具有反迟滞扩散特性的成分。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种预测性的第一性原理方法，用于计算非稀薄输运系数并设计具有目标输运特性的多主元合金。该方法为理解多主元合金中的扩散机制提供了新见解。

Abstract: Vacancy-mediated diffusion in multi-principal element alloys (MPEAs) remains poorly understood. Existing computational methods face challenges in connecting electronic structure to macroscopic transport coefficients due to the large number of chemical elements. To address this, we introduce the embedded local cluster expansion (eLCE), which bridges first-principles calculations with kinetic Monte Carlo simulations to compute the matrix of multicomponent diffusion coefficients. Applying this approach to refractory MPEAs in the V-Cr-Nb-Mo-Ta-W system, we evaluate the complete mobility and diffusion tensors of a six-component alloy at finite temperatures. We find that local kinetic barriers, rather than thermodynamics or vacancy correlation factors, primarily control diffusion in these materials. Whether diffusion is sluggish or anti-sluggish depends on the mean vacancy migration barrier relative to the rule-of-mixtures estimate and on the availability of percolating pathways of fast-diffusing species. We use this insight to screen the senary composition space and identify compositions with anti-sluggish diffusion. This study presents a predictive, first-principles approach for computing non-dilute transport coefficients and designing MPEAs with targeted transport properties.

### [19] [Mn substitution induced a ferrimagnetic to ferromagnetic transition in trigonal $\text{Cr}_5\text{Te}_8$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24261)
*Ze-Xin Liu,Guang-Yu Wen,Cong-Mian Zhen,Deng-Lu Hou,Li Ma,De-Wei Zhao,Guo-ke Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究合成了原始和Mn掺杂的三方（trigonal）Cr₅Te₈单晶，并进行对比表征。实验测量包括磁性参数如居里温度（T_C）和饱和磁矩（m_S）。同时采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）进行理论模拟，分析磁结构和掺杂效应。

Result: 原始三方Cr₅Te₈的T_C为226 K，m_S为1.86 μ_B/Cr；Mn掺杂后T_C提升至249 K，m_S增至2.72 μ_B/离子。m_S的显著增加远超Mn本身的贡献，表明原始晶体中存在反平行自旋排列（antiparallel spin alignment）。计算确认原始Cr₅Te₈为亚铁磁体（ferrimagnet，m_S≈1.60 μ_B），而掺杂Mn原子优先占据范德华间隙（vdW gaps），诱导体系转变为铁磁态（ferromagnetic state），计算m_S为2.92 μ_B，与实验结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 本研究澄清了三方Cr₅Te₈的磁基态模糊性，确认其为亚铁磁体而非铁磁体。过渡金属掺杂（特别是Mn）通过占据范德华间隙并诱导磁态转变，为调控和优化CrₓTeᵧ化合物的磁性能提供了有效途径。

Abstract: The critical role of transition-metal doping in optimizing the performance of 2D vdW $\text{Cr}_x\text{Te}_y$ ferromagnets remains largely unexplored. Here, we report the synthesis and comparative characterization of pristine and Mn-doped trigonal $\text{Cr}_5\text{Te}_8$ single crystals. Trigonal $\text{Cr}_5\text{Te}_8$ exhibits a magnetic ordering temperature ($T_C$) of 226 K and a saturation moment ($m_S$) of 1.86 $μ_B$/Cr at 5 K. In comparison, Mn substitution enhances $T_C$ to 249 K and $m_S$ to 2.72 $μ_B$/ion. This substantial increase in $m_S$ far exceeds the nominal contribution of Mn alone, providing compelling evidence for antiparallel spin alignment in trigonal $\text{Cr}_5\text{Te}_8$. Complementing these experimental findings, first-principles calculations identify trigonal $\text{Cr}_5\text{Te}_8$ as a ferrimagnet ($m_S \approx 1.60~μ_B$) rather than a ferromagnet. Furthermore, simulations reveal that doped Mn atoms preferentially occupy the vdW gaps and drive a transition to a ferromagnetic state with a calculated $m_S$ of 2.92 $μ_B$, in excellent agreement with experimental results. This work resolves the ambiguity regarding the magnetic ground state of trigonal $\text{Cr}_5\text{Te}_8$ and demonstrates that transition metal substitution provides an effective route to modulate and optimize the magnetic properties of $\text{Cr}_x\text{Te}_y$ compounds.

### [21] [Lattice-Expansion-Driven Stabilization of Helical Magnetic Order in Ru-Doped MnP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24281)
*Xin-Wei Wu,Deng-lu Hou,Li Ma,Cong-mian Zhen,De-wei Zhao,Guoke Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MnP在自旋电子器件中的应用受限于其较低的螺旋有序温度（TS），研究旨在通过化学掺杂提升TS以拓展其实际应用潜力。

Method: 在Mn1-xRuxP单晶中进行Ru替代掺杂，诱导高度各向异性的晶格膨胀，特别关注b轴参数变化；结合Mo和W掺杂类似物的数据，建立TS和TC与b轴的普适标度关系；通过第一性原理计算揭示晶格膨胀对磁耦合的选择性影响。

Result: Ru掺杂使TS从51K显著提升至215K，沿[010]方向的临界场从2.3kOe增至30.0kOe，同时TC从291K降至215K；发现TS和TC主要受b轴参数控制，呈现普适线性标度关系；第一性原理计算表明晶格膨胀选择性削弱铁磁耦合而保留反铁磁相互作用，增强磁阻挫并稳定螺旋磁性。

Conclusion: 通过定向b轴工程实现的化学压力是稳定MnP中螺旋磁性的稳健且可推广的范式，为设计高性能手性自旋电子器件提供了有效策略。

Abstract: The practical utilization of MnP in chiral spintronic devices is fundamentally constrained by its low helical ordering temperature ($T_{\rm S}$). Here, we demonstrate that Ru substitution in Mn$_{1-x}$Ru$_x$P single crystals drives a highly anisotropic lattice expansion, where the $b$-axis elongation is one-quarter that of the $a$- and $c$-axes ($\sim$ 0.04 Å). This structural distortion profoundly stabilizes the helical ground state, elevating $T_{\rm S}$ from 51~K to 215~K and the critical field along the [010] direction at 5~K from 2.3 to 30.0~kOe, while suppressing the Curie temperature ($T_{\rm C}$) from 291~K to 215~K. Synthesizing these results with reported data on Mo- and W-doped analogues reveals that $T_{\rm S}$ and $T_{\rm C}$ are governed primarily by the $b$-axis parameter, exhibiting universal linear scaling relationships ($dT_{\rm S}/db = 1.59 \times 10^4\ \text{KÅ}^{-1}$, $dT_{\rm C}/db = 0.69 \times 10^4\ \text{KÅ}^{-1}$) far greater than those associated with the $a$- or $c$-axes. First-principles calculations reveal that the lattice expansion selectively attenuates ferromagnetic coupling while preserving antiferromagnetic interactions between nearest-neighbor Mn atoms, thereby enhancing magnetic frustration and stabilizing helimagnetism. These findings establish chemical pressure via directed $b$-axis engineering as a robust, generalizable paradigm for stabilizing helimagnetism in MnP.

In this work, this LbL-LPE spin-coating is established as a robust, high-throughput fabrication protocol suitable for application-ready materials. The protocol incorporates correlative characterization combining grazing-incidence wide-angle X-ray scattering (GIWAXS), infrared and UV-Vis spectroscopy, scanning electron microscopy (SEM), and time-of-flight secondary ion mass spectrometry (ToF-SIMS) to ensure control over surface chemistry, reactant delivery, and film growth. Determination of the degree of orientation and the Hermans orientation parameters provides a key quality metrics for assessing crystal alignment and reproducibility. Motivation: 多巴胺水平与帕金森病（Parkinson's）和阿尔茨海默病（Alzheimer's）等神经系统疾病密切相关。因此，可靠且灵敏的多巴胺检测对于神经退行性疾病（neurodegenerative diseases）的早期诊断和监测至关重要。

Method: 本研究提出了一种基于空间自相位调制（spatial self-phase modulation, SSPM）的简单、无标记（label-free）液体传感方法。该方法利用由Al70Co10Fe5Ni10Cu5五种元素组成的二维准晶（2D quasicrystal）纳米结构，该结构因其高表面积体积比（surface-to-volume ratio）而提供活性位点。通过分析不同浓度多巴胺溶液（1100 ppb）混合时衍射图案的时间演化（time evolution），检测非线性折射率（nonlinear refractive index）的变化。

Result: 实验显示，1100 ppb多巴胺溶液在活性二维Al准晶溶液中引起衍射图案的偏移，表现出明显的数值变化，表明非线性折射率发生了改变。通过时间演化分析计算了非线性折射率变化和时间常数（time constant）的灵敏度。该SSPM传感方法进一步与拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）、紫外-可见光谱（UV-Vis spectroscopy）和傅里叶变换红外光谱（FTIR spectroscopy）等其他光学传感方法进行了比较。

Conclusion: 基于表面等离子体共振（SPR）激活的二维Al准晶纳米结构成功展示了多巴胺传感能力，并进行了定性和定量评估。实验观测结果通过基于密度泛函理论（DFT-based simulations）的模拟得到解释。当前的SSPM方法可用于快速、大规模的医学诊断。

Abstract: Dopamine levels are linked to neurological illnesses like Parkinson's and Alzheimer's. Thus, reliable and sensitive detection of dopamine is crucial for early diagnosis and surveillance of neurodegenerative diseases. Non-noble-metal-based nanomaterials are ideal for light-mediated sensing of organic molecules. Among these, 2D quasicrystal structures consisting of five elements, namely Al70Co10Fe5Ni10Cu5, provide active sites due to their high surface-to-volume ratio, making them excellent for organic chemical sensing. Here, we propose a simple, label-free, spatial self-phase-modulation (SSPM)-based sensing method in liquid form. SSPM-based time evolution of the diffraction pattern for varied mixing levels of a 1100 ppb dopamine solution shows a shift in the active 2D Al QC solution. The 1100 ppb solution shows a distinct value, indicating a change in the nonlinear refractive index. Time-evolution analysis is used to calculate sensitivities to changes in the nonlinear refractive index and time constant. The SPR-activated 2D Al QC nanostructure is used to demonstrate dopamine sensing and to perform qualitative and quantitative evaluations. The SSPM-based sensing has been further compared with other optical-based sensing methods such as Raman spectroscopy, UV-Vis spectroscopy, and FTIR spectroscopy. The experimental observations are also explained using DFT-based simulations. The current SSPM method can be used for rapid, large-scale medical diagnostics.

</details>


### [24] [Substrate-dependent pore formation in molybdenum disulfide monolayers under ion irradiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24416)
*Y. Liebsch,U. Javed,L. Skopinski,L. Daniel,F. Appel,R. Rahali,C. Grygiel,H. Lebius,C. Frank,L. Breuer,L. Kirsch,F. Koch,J. Kotakoski,M. Schleberger*

TL;DR: 该研究通过高电荷离子和快重离子辐照，探究了不同基底上单层MoS₂纳米孔形成的机制，发现基底类型显著影响孔尺寸和形成效率，表明基底依赖的电子耗散途径是关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离子辐照是纳米结构表面加工的重要工具，但能量在表面和超薄材料中的沉积与耗散机制尚不明确。本研究旨在探究不同基底上单层MoS₂在两种离子辐照下的纳米孔形成过程。

Method: 使用高电荷离子（highly charged ions, HCIs）和快重离子（swift heavy ions, SHIs）辐照不同基底上的单层MoS₂，包括悬浮MoS₂、SiO₂基底上的MoS₂、双层MoS₂以及金基底上的MoS₂。通过扫描透射电子显微镜（scanning transmission electron microscopy）量化孔半径和孔形成效率。

Result: 孔尺寸和孔形成效率对基底类型表现出显著依赖性：SiO₂基底上的MoS₂形成的孔最大且最频繁，而金基底则强烈抑制孔的形成。两种离子辐照下的孔尺寸观测结果一致，表明基底和界面依赖的电子耗散途径起核心作用。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，基底类型通过影响电子耗散途径，在纳米孔形成过程中发挥关键作用。这一发现为理解离子辐照在超薄材料中的能量沉积与耗散机制提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Ion irradiation is a versatile tool for nanostructuring surfaces, yet the roles of energy deposition and dissipation at the surface and in ultrathin materials remain poorly understood. In this study, we investigate nanopore formation in monolayer MoS$_2$ on different substrates under irradiation of highly charged ions (HCIs) and swift heavy ions (SHIs): two types of ions that, despite having vastly different kinetic energies, interact primarily with the electronic system of the target. Using scanning transmission electron microscopy, we quantify pore radii and pore formation efficiencies for suspended MoS$_2$, MoS$_2$ on SiO$_2$, bilayer MoS$_2$ and MoS$_2$ on gold. Both pore size and pore formation efficiency exhibit a pronounced dependence on the type of substrate. Pores are largest and most frequent in MoS$_2$ on SiO$_2$, while the gold substrate massively quenches pore formation. The results indicate that the observed pore dimensions under both HCI and SHI irradiation are consistent with a central role of substrate and interface-dependent electronic dissipation pathways.

### [25] [Fine-tuning universal machine learning potentials for transition state search in surface catalysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24482)
*Raffaele Cheula,Mie Andersen,John R. Kitchin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定表面反应的过渡态对于理解和设计异相催化剂至关重要，但使用密度泛函理论进行计算仍然成本高昂。虽然机器学习势函数提供了显著的加速，但任务特定模型在催化系统间的可迁移性有限，而通用机器学习势函数对反应构型的准确性不足。

Method: 研究基于主动学习的工作流程，迭代微调通用机器学习势函数用于DFT质量的过渡态搜索。首先使用来自金属和单原子合金表面CO2加氢反应网络的250个过渡态来基准测试过渡态搜索算法，识别出Sella算法最为稳健，并提出改进版本（Bond-Aware Sella）。然后探索了顺序和批量主动学习策略进行微调。

Result: 改进的Bond-Aware Sella算法显著提高了过渡态搜索的成功率。研究表明，通过微调的通用机器学习势函数，平均每个结构仅需8次DFT单点计算即可找到DFT质量的过渡态结构。

Conclusion: 这证明了微调的通用机器学习势函数用于高通量催化剂筛选的可行性，为解决传统DFT计算成本高昂的问题提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Determining transition states (TSs) of surface reactions is central to understanding and designing heterogeneous catalysts but remains computationally prohibitive with density functional theory (DFT). While machine learning potentials (MLPs) offer significant speedups, task-specific models have limited transferability across catalytic systems, and universal MLPs (uMLPs) lack the accuracy needed for reactive configurations. Here, we present a workflow based on active learning to iteratively fine-tune uMLPs for DFT-quality TS search. Using 250 TSs from the CO2 hydrogenation reaction network on metal and single-atom alloy surfaces, we first benchmark TS search algorithms, identifying the Sella algorithm as most robust, and propose a modification (Bond-Aware Sella) that substantially improves its success rate. We then explore sequential and batch active-learning strategies for fine-tuning and show that DFT-quality TS structures can be found using only 8 DFT single-point calculations on average per structure. This demonstrates the viability of fine-tuned uMLPs for high-throughput catalyst screening.

Abstract: We present a comprehensive first-principles investigation of defects in 4$H_b$-TaS$_2$. Motivated by recent defect manipulation in 4$H_b$-TaS$_2$ via STM, we address their microscopic nature and impact on interlayer charge transfer. ### [27] [Multiple Topological States in LaAgAs2, a Failed Square-Net Semimetal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24513)
*Yang Liu,Tongrui Li,Xixi Yuan,Nour Maraytta,Alexei V. Fedorov,Asish K. Kundu,Turgut Yilmaz,Elio Vescovo,Xueliang Wu,Long Zhang,Mingquan He,Yisheng Chai,Xiaoyuan Zhou,Michael Merz,Zhe Sun,Huixia Fu,Tonica Valla,Aifeng Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过综合实验与理论方法，揭示了LaAgAs₂材料中cis-trans晶格畸变对电子结构的影响，发现该材料在费米能级附近存在多种拓扑态，为拓扑材料的有意设计提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索新材料的有意设计（rational design）作为发现拓扑材料的重要方向，需要深入理解晶体结构与电子结构之间的关联性。本研究旨在通过LaAgAs₂这一具体材料，阐明这种关联性。

Method: 采用综合实验与理论计算方法：单晶X射线衍射（XRD）用于晶体结构分析，量子振荡（quantum oscillation）和角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）用于电子结构表征，并结合密度泛函理论（DFT）计算进行理论验证。

Result: XRD显示LaAgAs₂结晶为HfCuSi₂衍生结构，其方形网络（square net）畸变为cis-trans链。ARPES揭示其电子结构与基于方形网络的半金属显著不同，费米面呈准二维特征，包含区中心的狄拉克型空穴口袋和区边界的准一维椭圆电子口袋。DFT计算表明cis-trans畸变将二维方形网络衍生的狄拉克带转变为准一维平庸带，并在区中心附近识别出多种拓扑态，包括非平庸Z₂拓扑表面态和体狄拉克态。

Conclusion: 本研究阐明了cis-trans畸变对电子结构的影响，确认LaAgAs₂为费米能级附近存在多种拓扑态的拓扑材料，为有意设计新型拓扑材料提供了指导原则。

Abstract: The rational design of new materials emerges as an important direction to explore new topological materials, which is based on the understanding of the correlation between crystal and electronic structures. In this paper, we perform a comprehensive study on the crystal and electronic structures in LaAgAs2 through a combination of single-crystal x-ray diffraction (XRD), quantum oscillation, and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) experimental measurements, and density functional theory (DFT) calculations. Single-crystal XRD measurements reveal that LaAgAs2 crystallizes into a HfCuSi2-derived structure with the square net distorted into cis-trans chains. Quantum oscillation measurements reveal two frequencies with small effective masses and quasi-two-dimensional (2D) characters. ARPES measurements reveal an electronic structure strikingly different from the square-net-based semimetals, such as LaAgAs2. The Fermi surface is quasi-two-dimensional (2D), with Dirac-like hole pockets at the zone center and a quasi-1D elliptical electron pocket at the zone boundary. Based on the DFT calculations, the measured electronic structure can be well understood regarding the cis-trans distortion, which transforms the two-dimensional square net-derived Dirac bands into quasi-1D trivial bands. Intriguingly, multiple topological states can be identified around the zone center, including a nontrivial Z2 topological surface state and a bulk Dirac state. Our study clarifies the impact of cis-trans distortion and identifies LaAgAs2 as a topological material with multiple topological states near the Fermi level, providing a guideline for intentionally designing new topological materials.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用磁透射X射线显微镜（Magnetic Transmission X-ray Microscopy）实验，将观察到的传播路径与局域磁构型相关联。通过施加纵向和横向磁场调控NdCo/NiFe可重构跑道中条纹畴（stripe domain）模式内的反涡旋传播。

Abstract: The controlled propagation of spin textures at bifurcations is a critical challenge for racetrack-based logic devices. Here, we investigate the effect of longitudinal and transverse magnetic fields on the propagation of magnetic antivortices at bifurcations within the stripe domain pattern of a reconfigurable NdCo/NiFe racetrack in order to control the preferred antivortex trajectory. Magnetic Transmission X-ray Microscopy experiments were employed to correlate the observed propagation path with the local magnetic configuration. We demonstrate that Zeeman coupling to the magnetization components at the bifurcation core enables switching of the preferred propagation branch using low-amplitude transverse magnetic fields, without modifying the global stripe domain configuration that defines the guiding racetrack landscape. In-plane magnetic anisotropy provides an additional mechanism to break the symmetry between the upper and lower bifurcation branches by tuning the relative orientation between the stripe domain pattern and the longitudinal magnetic fields.

Abstract: Chiral crystals exhibit useful handedness-dependent properties, including spin selectivity and circularly polarized light sensitivity, yet controlling which enantiomer forms during synthesis remains a central challenge. Existing approaches utilize molecules in solution to template crystal growth, which restricts processing conditions and introduces organic contaminants incompatible with device fabrication. Enantioselective growth of a chiral crystal on a chiral surface via vapor-phase synthesis (chiral epitaxy) has not yet been demonstrated. Here, we show chiral epitaxy of aligned tellurium nanowires on a low-symmetry two-dimensional material, ReSe2. In situ electron microscopies suggest a mechanism where handedness is determined at nucleation by the interface energy difference between Te enantiomers and the chiral substrate surface. ### [30] [optimade-maker: Automated generation of interoperable materials APIs from static data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23536)
*Kristjan Eimre,Matthew L. Evans,Bud Macaulay,Xing Wang,Jusong Yu,Nicola Marzari,Gian-Marco Rignanese,Giovanni Pizzi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了optimade-maker轻量级工具包，支持从原始原子结构和属性数据自动生成符合OPTIMADE标准的API。该工具包支持多种原始数据集，能够转换为标准化的OPTIMADE数据表示，并允许在本地和生产环境中快速部署API。

Result: 在Materials Cloud Archive上实现了自动化服务，自动创建和发布贡献数据集的OPTIMADE API，实现即时可发现性和互操作性。同时为剑桥结构数据库（CSD）和无机晶体结构数据库（ICSD）实现了数据转换管道，通过OPTIMADE框架提供统一访问。

Conclusion: 通过降低互操作数据发布的技术门槛，optimade-maker代表了向可扩展、FAIR（可查找、可访问、可互操作、可重用）材料数据生态系统迈出的重要一步，整合了社区贡献和精心管理的数据库。

Abstract: Atomistic structural data are central to materials science, condensed matter physics, and chemistry, and are increasingly digitised across diverse repositories and databases. Interoperable access to these heterogeneous data sources enables reusable clients and tools, and is essential for cross-database analyses and data-driven materials discovery. Toward this aim, the OPTIMADE (Open Databases Integration for Materials Design) specification defines a standard REST API for atomistic structures and related properties. However, deploying and maintaining compliant services remains technically demanding and poses a significant barrier for many data providers. Here, we present optimade-maker, a lightweight toolkit for the automated generation of OPTIMADE-compliant APIs directly from raw atomistic structure and property data. The toolkit supports a wide range of raw datasets, enables conversion to a standardised OPTIMADE data representation, and allows for rapid deployment of APIs in both local and production environments. We further demonstrate it through an automated service on the Materials Cloud Archive, which automatically creates and publishes OPTIMADE APIs for contributed datasets, enabling immediate discoverability and interoperability. In addition, we implement data transformation pipelines for the Cambridge Structural Database (CSD) and the Inorganic Crystal Structure Database (ICSD), enabling unified access to these curated resources through the OPTIMADE framework. By lowering the technical barriers to interoperable data publication, optimade-maker represents an important step toward a scalable, FAIR materials data ecosystem integrating both community-contributed and curated databases.

### [31] [On two Abelian Groups Related to the Galois Top](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23716)
*Helmut Ruhland*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文研究了Galois陀螺（Galois top）的数学物理性质，定义了与刚体Galois轴上点相关的阿贝尔半群（abelian semigroup）和阿贝尔群（abelian group），这些代数结构源于Huygens-Steiner定理在该系统中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Galois陀螺作为数学物理中的研究对象，具有独特的代数运动不变量和超越运动不变量。研究其刚体动力学性质，特别是Galois轴上的点与Huygens-Steiner定理的关联，需要建立相应的代数结构来描述这些物理特性。

Method: 通过应用Huygens-Steiner定理到刚体Galois轴上的点，定义了与这些物理性质相关的阿贝尔半群和阿贝尔群。这些代数结构旨在描述Galois陀螺系统中点的集合运算特性。

Result: 成功构建了与Galois陀螺系统相关的阿贝尔半群和阿贝尔群结构。这些代数结构能够描述刚体Galois轴上点的集合在Huygens-Steiner定理应用下的数学性质。

Conclusion: Galois陀螺的物理特性可以通过定义的阿贝尔半群和阿贝尔群进行代数描述，这些结构为理解该数学物理系统中的Huygens-Steiner定理应用提供了代数框架。

Abstract: In mathematical physics the Galois top, introduced by S. Adlaj, possesses a fixed point on one of two Galois axes through its center of mass. This heavy top has two algebraic motion invariants and an additional transcendental motion-invariant. This third invariant depends on an antiderivative of a variable in the canonical phase space. In this article an abelian semigroup and an abelian group are defined that are related to the application of the Huygens-Steiner theorem to points on the Galois axis of a rigid body.

### [32] [Deep Kinetic JKO schemes for Vlasov-Fokker-Planck Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23901)
*Wonjun Lee,Li Wang,Wuchen Li*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于深度神经网络的数值方法，用于求解包括线性和非线性情形的动力学福克-普朗克方程（kinetic Fokker-Planck equations）。该方法构建了动力学JKO（Jordan-Kinderlehrer-Otto）方案，通过粒子近似和神经网络参数化实现高维动力学模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发一种能够有效求解高维动力学福克-普朗克方程的数值方法。传统方法在处理高维问题时面临计算挑战，需要新的计算框架来保持方程的基本变分和结构特性。

Method: 基于Vlasov型方程的保守耗散结构，构建了一类广义最小化运动方案作为迭代约束最小化问题：保守部分确定约束集，耗散部分定义目标泛函。这形成了动力学JKO方案，通过粒子近似和深度神经网络参数化速度场来计算每一步迭代。

Result: 提出的动力学JKO-神经ODE框架能够有效表示高维动力学，同时保持底层偏微分方程的基本变分和结构特性。通过大量数值实验验证了该方法的有效性，证明其适用于高维数值模拟。

Conclusion: 该方法为求解高维动力学福克-普朗克方程提供了有效的数值框架，结合了变分结构保持和神经网络表示的优势，在高维数值模拟中展现出良好性能。

Abstract: We introduce a deep neural network-based numerical method for solving kinetic Fokker Planck equations, including both linear and nonlinear cases. Building upon the conservative dissipative structure of Vlasov-type equations, we formulate a class of generalized minimizing movement schemes as iterative constrained minimization problems: the conservative part determines the constraint set, while the dissipative part defines the objective functional. This leads to an analog of the classical Jordan-Kinderlehrer-Otto (JKO) scheme for Wasserstein gradient flows, and we refer to it as the kinetic JKO scheme. To compute each step of the kinetic JKO iteration, we introduce a particle-based approximation in which the velocity field is parameterized by deep neural networks. The resulting algorithm can be interpreted as a kinetic-oriented neural differential equation that enables the representation of high-dimensional kinetic dynamics while preserving the essential variational and structural properties of the underlying PDE. We validate the method with extensive numerical experiments and demonstrate that the proposed kinetic JKO-neural ODE framework is effective for high-dimensional numerical simulations.

</details>


### [33] [Volume Term Adaptivity for Discontinuous Galerkin Schemes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24189)
*Daniel Doehring,Jesse Chan,Hendrik Ranocha,Michael Schlottke-Lakemper,Manuel Torrilhon,Gregor Gassner*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于高阶间断伽辽金（DG）格式的体积项自适应（v-adaptivity）概念，通过基于合适指标在每个龙格-库塔阶段交换DG格式的体积贡献离散化，以提升鲁棒性、效率和近似质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对求解时间依赖偏微分方程的高阶间断伽辽金（discontinuous Galerkin, DG）格式，需要平衡鲁棒性与效率的需求。传统均匀体积项离散化方法难以同时优化这两个方面，因此需要一种自适应策略来动态调整离散化方式。

Method: 提出体积项自适应（v-adaptivity）方法，基于合适指标在每个龙格-库塔（Runge-Kutta）阶段交换DG格式的体积贡献离散化。根据关注重点（鲁棒性或效率）选择不同自适应策略：当弱形式体积项离散化比熵守恒通量差分体积积分产生更多熵时，使用前者以获得熵稳定（entropy-stable）格式；若以提高效率为主要目标，则在不超过特定熵阈值或不引发不稳定的条件下使用弱形式体积积分。

Result: v-自适应DG格式相比均匀体积项离散化方案，在鲁棒性、效率和近似质量方面均有提升。该方法在应用于二维和三维可压缩流动问题前，已对其精度、线性稳定性和熵可容许性（entropy-admissibility）进行了全面验证。

Conclusion: 体积项自适应（v-adaptivity）为高阶DG格式提供了一种通用方法，能够根据具体需求动态调整体积项离散化策略，从而在保持数值稳定性的同时优化计算效率，适用于多维可压缩流动问题的求解。

Abstract: We introduce the concept of volume term adaptivity for high-order discontinuous Galerkin (DG) schemes solving time-dependent partial differential equations. Termed v-adaptivity, we present a novel general approach that exchanges the discretization of the volume contribution of the DG scheme at every Runge-Kutta stage based on suitable indicators. Depending on whether robustness or efficiency is the main concern, different adaptation strategies can be chosen. Precisely, the weak form volume term discretization is used instead of the entropy-conserving flux-differencing volume integral whenever the former produces more entropy than the latter, resulting in an entropy-stable scheme. Conversely, if increasing the efficiency is the main objective, the weak form volume integral may be employed as long as it does not increase entropy beyond a certain threshold or cause instabilities. Thus, depending on the choice of the indicator, the v-adaptive DG scheme improves robustness, efficiency and approximation quality compared to schemes with a uniform volume term discretization. We thoroughly verify the accuracy, linear stability, and entropy-admissibility of the v-adaptive DG scheme before applying it to various compressible flow problems in two and three dimensions.

</details>

Result: 获得完整分类：此类相由 $φ\in\operatorname{End}(G)$ 参数化。对每个 $φ$ 识别了体材料 $\mathcal{Z}(\mathcal{H})\simeq\mathcal{D}_G^2$ 中相关的可凝聚代数（condensable algebra）$\mathcal{A}_φ$。通过修改的 Kitaev 模型实现了（可能扭曲的）基于群的团簇态（group-based cluster state）。

Conclusion: 该研究完整分类了具有 $\mathrm{Rep}(G)\times G$ 对称性的 $1+1$ 维玻色 SPT 相的内在混合相，建立了参数化方案与可凝聚代数的对应关系，并通过晶格模型提供了物理实现。

Abstract: We classify $1+1$d bosonic SPT phases with non-invertible symmetry $\mathrm{Rep}(G)\times G$, equivalently the fusion-category symmetry $\mathcal{H}=\mathrm{Rep}(G)\times\mathrm{Vec}_G$. Focusing on \emph{intrinsically mixed} phases (trivial under either factor alone), we use the correspondence between $\mathcal{H}$-SPTs, $\mathcal{H}$-modules over $\mathrm{Vec}$, and fiber functors $\mathcal{H}\to\mathrm{Vec}$ to obtain a complete classification: such phases are parametrized by $φ\in\operatorname{End}(G)$. For each $φ$ we identify the associated condensable (Lagrangian) algebra $\mathcal{A}_φ$ in the bulk $\mathcal{Z}(\mathcal{H})\simeq\mathcal{D}_G^2$. We further provide an explicit lattice realization by modifying Kitaev's quantum double model with a domain wall $\mathcal{B}_φ$ and smooth/rough boundaries, and then contracting to a 1D chain, yielding a (possibly twisted) group-based cluster state whose ribbon-generated symmetry operators encode the same $φ$.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限温度密度泛函理论常依赖零温近似，使用基态交换关联泛函配合热化密度。然而，这种方法忽略了交换关联自由能的显式温度依赖性——这在暖密物质等电子效应和热效应均显著的区域尤为关键。

Method: 本文引入熵修正的零温方法，利用广义热绝热连接公式提取交换关联熵，为标准零温近似构建热修正。采用均匀电子气体参数化，将该方法与有限温度绝热连接进行比较。

Result: 该方法在低密度区域表现最佳，为零温密度泛函近似提供了有用补充。研究进一步识别了绝热连接曲线间的密度依赖性交点，揭示了基态关联能和关联势的依赖性。

Abstract: Density functional theory at finite temperatures often relies on the zero-temperature approximation, which uses a ground-state exchange-correlation functional with thermalized densities. This approach, however, neglects the explicit temperature dependence of the exchange-correlation free energy -- a key factor in regimes such as warm dense matter, where both electronic and thermal effects are significant. In this work, we introduce the entropy-corrected zero-temperature approach, in which the exchange-correlation entropy is extracted using the generalized thermal adiabatic connection formula to construct a thermal correction to the standard zero-temperature approximation. Using a uniform electron gas parametrization, we compare this approach to the finite-temperature adiabatic connection and demonstrate that it performs best at lower densities. This provides a useful complement to zero-temperature density functional approximations, which generally perform better at moderate-to-large densities. We further identify a density-dependent intersection between the adiabatic connection curves, revealing a dependence on the ground state correlation energy and correlation potential. Additionally, extension of the entropy corrected approach applied as a local density approximation--like temperature correction to the zero temperature approximation is discussed.

Abstract: We study two-dimensional periodic metamaterials in which idealised cylindrical inclusions are modelled by boundary conditions. In the scalar time-harmonic setting, the background field satisfies the Helmholtz equation, and high-contrast inclusion limits reduce to Dirichlet or Neumann conditions, with direct analogues in dielectric and acoustic media. By switching the condition assigned to selected inclusions, we break point-group symmetries of the primitive cell and thereby lift symmetry-induced degeneracies in the Floquet--Bloch spectrum of hexagonal and square lattices, opening valley-type band gaps with Berry curvature localised near opposite valleys.
  To analyse infinite and finite structures within a unified framework, we derive matched-asymptotic point-scatterer approximations for mixed Dirichlet--Neumann arrays. For doubly periodic systems, this yields a finite-dimensional generalised eigenvalue problem for the Floquet--Bloch spectrum; for finite arrays, it yields a generalised Foldy multiple-scattering system. In both hexagonal and square lattices, geometrically identical crystals can realise distinct valley-Hall phases solely through boundary-condition assignment while retaining an overlapping bulk gap. Spatially varying this assignment therefore creates and relocates internal interfaces without altering the underlying geometry, enabling the associated valley-Hall interfacial modes to be repositioned within the same crystal.

Method: 开发了宽场二维电子光谱显微镜（2DESM），该技术整合了多维相干光谱（multidimensional coherent spectroscopy）与光学成像。系统具有宽带覆盖（1.4-1.8 eV），能够直接获取空间分辨的二维电子光谱（2DES）图，无需空间扫描即可同时捕获光谱和空间域信息。

Abstract: We present a widefield two-dimensional electronic spectroscopy microscope (2DESM) that integrates multidimensional coherent spectroscopy with optical imaging, enabling femtosecond temporal and micrometer spatial resolution. The broadband coverage (1.4-1.8 eV) allows the direct acquisition of spatially resolved two-dimensional electronic spectroscopy (2DES) maps of relevant near infrared excitations without the need for spatial scanning. By capturing both spectral and spatial domains simultaneously, 2DESM overcomes limitations of pump-probe microscopy and scanning 2DES, providing access to decoherence dynamics, inhomogeneous broadening, and coherent coupling in heterogeneous systems. As a proof-of-concept we performed 2DESM measurements on bilayer WSe2 encapsulated in hBN, revealing distinct spatial variations in excitonic dynamics. These results validate the ability of 2DESM to link local environments with ultrafast coherent processes and establish 2DESM as a versatile platform for probing quantum coherence, many-body interactions, and non-local energy transfer in two-dimensional materials, heterostructures, and micrometer-scale optoelectronic devices.

### [38] [Self-organised structures in mixed active-passive suspensions due to hydrodynamic interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23555)
*Alexander Chamolly,Takuji Ishikawa*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究采用三维斯托克斯动力学方法，探究了底部重心微泳体（bottom-heavy squirmers）与被动障碍球混合悬浮液的集体动力学，揭示了多种相分离结构及其对微泳体类型的依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合悬浮液中微泳体与被动颗粒的相分离现象已被认知，但由于多体流体动力学相互作用的精确处理困难，混合悬浮液中的自组织结构形成机制尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 研究采用三维斯托克斯动力学（Stokesian dynamics）方法，模拟了球形底部重心微泳体（bottom-heavy squirmers）与障碍球的混合致密悬浮液，并考虑了流体动力学相互作用。

Result: 结果显示：无外部定向机制时，被动球的存在会干扰取向有序的形成；中性或拉泳体（puller squirmers）在高堆积密度下，初始相分离态呈亚稳态；底部重心微泳体在某些条件下可发生动态相分离，包括中性微泳体和拉泳体在中等密度下的纤维状分离，以及高密度强底部重心拉泳体形成的新型层状相分离结构。

Abstract: Microswimmers in suspension exhibit collective swimming behaviour, forming various self-organised structures including ordered, aggregated, and turbulent-like structures. When mixed with passive particles phase-separation is known to occur, but due to the difficulty of accurately handling many-body hydrodynamic interactions, the formation of self-organised structures in mixed suspensions has remained unexplored so far. In this study, we investigate the dynamics of mixed dense suspensions of spherical bottom-heavy squirmers and obstacle spheres using Stokesian dynamics in three dimensions, taking hydrodynamic interactions into account. The results show that without an external orientating mechanism the formation of orientational order is in general disturbed by the presence of passive spheres. An initially phase-separated state is metastable for neutral or puller squirmers at high packing densities. When the squirmers are bottom-heavy, phase-separation can occur dynamically in some cases, notably a fibrillar kind of separation for neutral squirmers and pullers at medium densities. We also observed a novel form of lamellar phase-separation for pullers at high densities with strong bottom-heaviness, with a sandwich-like structure consisting of a layer of passive particles pushed by a layer of swimmers, followed by a gap. These results indicate that microstructure and particle transport undergo significant changes depending on the type of swimmer, highlighting the importance of hydrodynamic interactions. These insights allow for a deeper understanding of the behaviour of active particles in complex fluids and to control them using external torques.

### [39] [An Improved Paralyzable Detector Mod](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23540)
*Yueyun Chen,Matthew Mecklenburg*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 某些辐射探测器在高输入计数率下会出现"瘫痪"现象，当计数率接近事件鉴别器工作速率时，单参数死时间模型失效。需要更精确的模型来描述探测器在高计数率下的性能。

Method: 提出了修正的可瘫痪探测器模型，该双参数解析模型考虑了事件鉴别器的有限响应时间，相比传统单参数死时间模型增加了对鉴别器响应时间的描述。

Result: 与商用X射线探测器的实验数据对比显示，该模型能更好地描述输入和输出计数率关系，并能独立确定鉴别器响应时间和脉冲整形器死时间这两个关键性能参数。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了采集后堆积校正方法，显著减少高通量谱中的伪影。通过优化采集和校正流程，用户可在不损失精度的情况下将数据采集速度提高一个数量级。

Abstract: Certain radiation detectors are `paralyzed' with high input count rates. When applied to count rates close to the event discriminator working rate the one-parameter dead time model fails. Here we present a corrected paralyzable detector model accounting for the event discriminator's finite response time. This two-parameter analytical model, when compared to the experimental data from a commercial x-ray detector, gives an improved description of the input and output count rate relations. Furthermore, it can independently determine the discriminator response time and the pulse shaper dead time, critical parameters for understanding a detector's performance. Finally, this model also provides a post-acquisition pile-up correction that greatly reduces artifacts in high-throughput spectra. In some situations, applying this model to optimize the acquisition and post-acquisition correction allows a user to acquire data an order of magnitude faster without compromising accuracy.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双相时间投影室（dual-phase TPC）采用多吨级液态氙（LXe）靶质量，是暗物质搜索的前沿探测器技术。除了暗物质直接探测的优势外，天然氙靶还可用于搜索无中微子双贝塔衰变（0νββ）过程，该过程会违反轻子数守恒并表明中微子是马约拉纳粒子（Majorana particles）。然而，此类0νββ搜索受到探测器材料产生的伽马射线本底（gamma-ray backgrounds）的限制。

Method: 本研究设计了增强卷积神经网络（augmented convolutional neural network, A-CNN）模型，从探测器数据中提取额外的事件拓扑信息（event-topology information）。使用领先的液态氙时间投影室实验XENONnT的模拟和校准数据进行模型验证。

Abstract: Dual-phase time projection chamber (TPC) that employs a multi-ton-scale liquid xenon (LXe) target mass is a pioneering detector technology to search for dark matter. Beyond its advantage in dark matter direct detection efforts, the natural xenon target allows it to search for the neutrinoless double-beta decay ($0νββ$) process, which would violate lepton number conservation and indicate that neutrinos are Majorana particles. However, such $0νββ$ searches have been limited by gamma-ray backgrounds originating from the detector materials. In this work, we designed an augmented convolutional neural network (A-CNN) model to extract additional event-topology information from detector data. Using simulation and calibration data from XENONnT, a leading LXe TPC experiment, our model achieved over 60% background rejection while maintaining 90% signal acceptance. This rejection power improves XENONnT's projected sensitivity of the $^{136}$Xe $0νββ$ search by about 40%. Finally, we discuss two notable observations in MicroBooNE's data, both reported here for the first time: an approximately 50% decline in MicroBooNE's light yield over time, concentrated in the first two years of running; and a higher than expected O(200 kHz) rate of single photoelectron noise. ### [42] [The read-out electronics for the FLASH experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23846)
*Luigi Calligaris,Claudio Puglia,Gianluca Lamanna*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: FLASH 实验是一个暗物质（Dark Matter）和高频引力波（High-Frequency Gravitational Waves）探测项目，使用两个低温谐振腔扫描117-360 MHz频段，通过超导量子干涉放大器和软件定义无线电技术实现极弱信号（~10⁻²² W）的读取与处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在探测暗物质（DM）粒子和高频引力波（HFGWs），这些是目前物理学中尚未被直接观测到的关键现象，对理解宇宙基本构成和引力理论具有重要意义。

Method: FLASH 实验采用两个低温谐振腔（cryogenic resonant cavities）扫描117-360 MHz的射频频谱。信号读取系统使用微带超导量子干涉放大器（Microstrip Superconducting Quantum Interference Amplifiers, MSAs）作为低噪声放大器，并结合软件定义无线电（Software-Defined Radio, SDR）技术进行信号采集、预处理和压缩。

Result: 目前该电子读取系统正在开发中，旨在将极弱物理信号（低至10⁻²² W）转换为适合永久存储和离线分析的格式。

Conclusion: FLASH 实验通过创新的低温谐振腔探测技术和先进的电子读取系统，为暗物质和高频引力波的直接探测提供了一种新的实验方法，其电子读取系统的开发是实现这一目标的关键技术环节。

Abstract: We introduce the FLASH haloscope experiment and present its electronic read-out system, currently under development. FLASH searches for Dark Matter (DM) particles and High-Frequency Gravitational Waves (HFGWs) using two cryogenic resonant cavities to scan the radio frequency spectrum between 117 and 360 MHz, looking for signals as weak as $10^{-22}$ W. The signal readout uses Microstrip Superconducting Quantum Interference Amplifiers (MSAs) as low-noise amplifiers and Software-Defined Radio (SDR) techniques to acquire, preprocess and reduce the physics signal into a format suitable for permanent storage and offline analysis.

</details>


### [43] [Indirect monitoring of fast-charge cycling behavior of an energy-storage device-analysis of ambient temperature variations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23541)
*Pertti O. Tikkanen*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该研究通过对公开实验室报告中温度数据的重新分析，从环境温度信号中提取了关于同时进行的其他电池测试的未公开信息，包括循环次数、周期、不对称性等参数，并发现其他设备在338次3C倍率充放电循环中未出现可检测的热降解迹象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 公开的认证实验室报告记录了储能设备在10天内的自放电行为，其中测试设备和测试室（通风橱）的温度变化图主要用于监测而未进行深入分析。环境温度变化被归因于"同一通风橱中同时循环的其他电池"，但这一信号可能包含更多未分析的信息。

Method: 研究采用重新分析（reanalysis）方法，仅基于环境温度信号，结合一些温和合理的假设，提取同时进行的其他电池测试的未公开信息。该方法不依赖原始测试设备数据，而是从环境监测信号中推断其他测试参数。

Result: 分析结果显示：1) 确定了充放电循环次数；2) 获得了循环周期；3) 发现了充放电半周期不对称性；4) 最重要的是，提供了证据表明提到的"其他设备"在室温下以3C倍率完成了338次完整充放电循环，且未出现任何可检测的热降解特征。

Conclusion: 环境温度信号本身包含丰富信息，通过适当的分析方法可以提取关于同时进行的电池测试的详细参数。该研究展示了从监测数据中挖掘未公开信息的潜力，特别是发现了其他设备在338次3C倍率循环中未出现热降解的证据。

Abstract: I present a reanalysis of temperature data from a publicly available certified laboratory report that documented the self-discharging behavior of an energy-storage device during 10 days. Graphs of temperature variations of both the tested device itself and the test chamber (fume hood) were given mainly for monitoring without further analysis, and variations in the ambient temperature signal were attributed to "other cells being cycled simultaneously in the same fume hood".
  I show that the ambient temperature signal alone -- together with some quite mild and reasonable assumptions -- allow to extract previously unpublished information on the simultaneously run test on the other cells: 1) the number of charge/discharge cycles 2) the cycle period, 3) the charge/discharge half-cycle asymmetry, and -- most significantly -- evidence that 4) the mentioned "other device" completed 338 full charge/discharge cycles at 3C rate at room temperature without any detectable thermal degradation signature.

</details>


### [44] [Methods for an Electron Emission Digital Twin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23553)
*Salvador Barranco Carceles,Veronika Zadin,Steve Wells,Aquila Mavalankar,Ian Underwood,Anthony Ayari*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该论文提出了电子发射数字孪生方法（MEEDiT），通过整合先进的场致热电子发射模型与实验数据表征，实现对硅电子发射器的实时物理一致性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管热电子和场致电子发射理论已有百年发展，但实验数据分析与电子发射器设计仍主要依赖经验而非科学方法。这是由于电子发射涉及多种复杂过程，导致现象极其复杂。

Method: 开发了电子发射数字孪生方法（Methods for an Electron Emission Digital Twin, MEEDiT），该方法整合了最先进的场致热电子发射（thermo-field electron emission）模型与实验数据表征技术。

Result: 通过将MEEDiT应用于硅电子发射器，该方法能够弥合简单实验测量与"隐藏"物理量（如温度和场增强因子）之间的差距。MEEDiT提供了三维模拟的物理一致性，同时具备神经网络的速度优势。

Conclusion: MEEDiT实现了资源高效的实时表征，并能够提取在操作过程中原本无法获取的关键数据，为电子发射器的设计与分析提供了科学化工具。

Abstract: The effective design and operation of electron emitters is the core of critical technologies such as high-resolution electron imaging and spectroscopy or X-ray production for medical imaging. Despite 100 years of theoretical development in thermo- and field-electron emission models, the analysis of experimental data and design of electron emitters remains an art more than a science. This is due to the many processes that are involved in electron emission, which result in an extremely complex phenomenon. Here we describe and develop the Methods for an Electron Emission Digital Twin (MEEDiT), which integrates state-of-the-art thermo-field electron emission models and experimental data characterisation. By applying MEEDiT to silicon electron emitters, we demonstrate an approach that bridges the gap between simple experimental measurements and 'hidden' physical quantities like temperature and field enhancement. MEEDiT provides the physical consistency of a 3D simulation with the speed of a neural network, enabling resource-effective, real-time characterization and the extraction of critical data that is otherwise inaccessible during operation.

</details>

### [45] [A conjecture on a tight norm inequality in the finite-dimensional l_p](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24017)
*A. S. Holevo,A. V. Utkin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出一个关于d维空间lp范数（lp-norm）的紧致不等式（tight inequality），该不等式表述简单但证明困难。作者给出了d=3时的证明，并对d≤200进行了数值验证，最后简要讨论了相关量子信道输出熵最小化问题的解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在提出并验证d维空间lp范数的一个紧致不等式，该不等式虽然表述简单但证明困难。研究动机源于该不等式在量子信息理论中的应用，特别是与量子信道输出熵最小化问题相关。

Method: 作者采用数学证明与数值验证相结合的方法：对于d=3的情况给出了严格的数学证明，同时对d≤200的维度进行了详细的数值检查（detailed numerical check）以确认猜想。方法还涉及对相关量子信道问题的对称性分析。

Result: 研究结果为：成功证明了d=3时lp范数不等式的成立，并通过数值验证确认了d≤200范围内该猜想的正确性。论文还简要综述了相关量子信道输出熵最小化问题的解，这些解依赖于问题的对称性。

Conclusion: 论文得出结论：提出的lp范数紧致不等式在d=3时得到证明，在d≤200时通过数值验证支持。该不等式与量子信息理论中的Rényi熵（Rényi entropy）和凸函数最大化问题密切相关，其证明依赖于问题的对称性。

Abstract: We suggest a tight inequality for norms in $d$-dimensional space $l_p $ which has simple formulation but appears hard to prove. We give a proof for $d=3$ and provide a detailed numerical check for $d\leq 200$ confirming the conjecture. We conclude with a brief survey of solutions for kin problems which anyhow concern minimization of the output entropy of certain quantum channel and rely upon the symmetry properties of the problem.
  Key words and phrases: $l_p $-norm, Rényi entropy, tight inequality, maximization of a convex function.

</details>


### [46] [Entanglement transference and non-inertial quantum reference frames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23601)
*Everett A. Patterson,Sijia Wang,Robert B. Mann*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了量子参考系（QRFs）中全局量子特性与视角性（perspectival）特性之间的关系，发现全局纠缠（entanglement）可以分解为视角性纠缠和相干性（coherence）的组合，这一现象称为纠缠转移（entanglement transference）。研究将此结果应用于非惯性QRFs，重新审视纠缠退化问题，发现视角性纠缠退化可被相干性资源增加所抵消。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 鉴于近期对视角性量子参考系（perspectival quantum reference frames, QRFs）的兴趣，研究旨在建立视角性量子特性与全局非视角性对应物之间的联系。这一联系至关重要，因为量子信息理论中的大多数已知结果都是在全局背景下推导的。

Method: 研究确定了全局纠缠分解为视角性纠缠和相干性（coherence）组合的充分条件，这一现象称为纠缠转移（entanglement transference）。将此理论框架应用于非惯性量子参考系（non-inertial QRFs），重新审视纠缠退化（entanglement degradation）问题。

Result: 研究发现，在视角性图像中，纠缠退化（entanglement degradation）可以被相干性资源（coherence resources）的增加所抵消。非惯性问题也可能为理解弯曲时空（curved spacetime）中的视角性量子参考系提供线索。

Conclusion: 研究建立了全局量子特性与视角性量子特性之间的重要联系，揭示了纠缠转移现象。在非惯性量子参考系中，视角性纠缠退化与相干性资源之间存在补偿关系，这一发现对理解弯曲时空中的量子参考系具有重要意义。

Abstract: Given the recent interest in perspectival quantum reference frames (QRFs), we ask how quantum properties in the perspectival picture relate to their global, non-perspectival counterparts. It is instructive to establish this link, as most known results in quantum information theory are derived in the latter context. Specifically, we find sufficient conditions under which global entanglement decomposes into a combination of perspectival entanglement and coherence -- a phenomenon that we call entanglement transference. We apply this result to non-inertial QRFs, in particular, revisiting the problem of entanglement degradation. We find that entanglement degradation in the perspectival picture can be offset by an increase in coherence resources. The non-inertial problem may also provide clues to understanding perspectival QRFs in curved spacetime.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立超越传统热力学速度极限的普适性信息几何不等式，该不等式不受底层动力学（马尔可夫或非马尔可夫演化）的限制，并探索其在量子过程层析成像中的实际应用。

Result: 建立了适用于混合态领域的精确信息几何不等式，在单量子比特情况下该不等式可饱和为严格等式；基于此发展出非迭代线性回归方法，成功估计了Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad（GKSL）主方程的哈密顿量和耗散参数，数值模拟验证了几何估计器的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了普适的信息几何不等式并展示了其在量子过程层析成像中的实际应用价值，通过非迭代线性回归方法避免了非线性优化的局部极小值问题，但需注意在纯态边界附近逆度量张量奇异性带来的误差缓解必要性。

Abstract: We establish an exact information-geometric inequality that remains valid regardless of the underlying dynamics, encompassing both Markovian and non-Markovian evolutions within the mixed-state domain. This inequality can be viewed as an extension of thermodynamic speed limits, which are typically formulated as inequalities. For single qubits, we show that this inequality saturates into a strict equality because the density matrix belongs to the quantum exponential family, with the Pauli matrices serving as sufficient statistics. From a practical perspective, this identity enables a non-iterative linear regression approach to continuous-time quantum process tomography, bypassing the local minima issues common in non-linear optimization. We demonstrate the efficiency of this method by estimating the Hamiltonian and dissipation parameters of the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad (GKSL) master equation. Numerical simulations confirm the validity of this geometric estimator and highlight the necessity of error mitigation near the pure-state boundary where the inverse metric becomes singular.

### [48] [Reaching states below the threshold energy in spin glasses via quantum annealing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23602)
*Christopher L. Baldwin*

Main category: quant-ph
