<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子退火通常用于寻找困难自旋玻璃和优化问题的基态，但其在近似优化中的应用同样重要。本文旨在研究量子退火在典型平均场自旋玻璃模型中的近似优化行为，特别是其能否突破传统阈值能量限制。

Method: 研究采用球形p-自旋模型（spherical p-spin models）作为典型平均场自旋玻璃模型。通过推导并数值求解热力学极限下成立的封闭积分微分方程，确保结果不受有限尺寸效应影响，且退火时间明确独立于系统尺寸。

Result: 量子退火能有效利用两阶段淬火效应，在O(1)时间内定位亚阈值状态。其不仅能达到与经典退火算法相同的低于阈值的能量水平，且速度显著更快：对于退火时间τ，量子退火的剩余能量以τ^{-α}衰减，在考虑情况下指数α可达模拟退火的两倍。

Conclusion: 量子退火在近似优化中表现优异，能突破传统阈值能量限制，在常数时间内找到亚阈值状态，且退火速度显著优于经典模拟退火算法。该方法通过热力学极限下的精确分析，确保了结果的普适性和可靠性。

Abstract: Although quantum annealing is usually considered as a method for locating the ground states of difficult spin-glass and optimization problems, its use in approximate optimization -- finding low- but not zero-energy states in a reasonably short amount of time -- is no less important. Here we investigate the behavior of quantum annealing at approximate optimization in the canonical mean-field spin-glass models, the spherical $p$-spin models, and find that it performs surprisingly well. Whereas it had long been assumed that infinite-range spin glasses have a unique ``threshold'' energy at which all quench and annealing dynamics become trapped until exponential timescales, recent work has shown that two-stage quenches can in fact reach states below the naive threshold in more generic situations. We demonstrate that quantum annealing is also capable of exploiting this effect to locate sub-threshold states in $O(1)$ time. Not only can it attain energies as far below the threshold as classical annealing algorithms, but it can do so significantly faster: for an annealing schedule taking time $τ$, the residual energy under quantum annealing decays as $τ^{-α}$ with an exponent up to twice as large as that of simulated annealing in the cases considered. Importantly, by deriving and numerically solving closed integro-differential equations that hold in the thermodynamic limit, our results are free from finite-size effects and hold for annealing times that are unambiguously independent of system size.

Abstract: Fluxonium superconducting qubits have demonstrated long coherence times and high single- and two-qubit gate fidelities, making them a favorable building block for superconducting quantum processors. We investigate the dominant limitations to fluxonium qubit energy relaxation time $T_1$ using a set of eight planar, aluminum-on-silicon qubits. We find that a circuit-based model for capacitive dielectric loss best captures the frequency dependence of $T_1$, which we analyze within both a two-level and a six-level energy relaxation model. We convert the measured $T_1$ into an effective capacitive quality factor $Q_\mathrm{C}^{\mathrm{eff}}$ to compare qubits on equal footing, accounting for independently estimated contributions from $1/f$ flux noise and radiative loss to the control and readout circuitry. We apply this methodology to compare qubits from two fabrication processes: a baseline process and one that applies a fluorine-based wet treatment prior to Josephson junction deposition. We resolve a small improvement of (13.8 $\pm$ 8.4$)\%$ in the process mean $Q_\mathrm{C}^{\mathrm{eff}}$, indicating that the fluorine treatment may have reduced loss from the metal-substrate interface, but did not address the primary source of loss in these fluxonium qubits.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Clifford lensing技术，利用Clifford操作同时对量子态和可观测量进行变换，将相位信息相干地局域化到减少的自由度集合上。建立了量子纠错码与干涉构造之间的对应关系，并开发了用于估计子系统支持相位的部分阴影层析协议。

Abstract: Quantum probes that enable enhanced exploration and characterization of complex systems are central to modern science, spanning applications from biology to astrophysics and chemical design. In large many-body quantum systems, interactions delocalize phase information across many degrees of freedom, dispersing it away from accessible measurements and limiting the scalability of quantum metrology. Here we show that experimentally accessible Clifford operations acting jointly on quantum states and observables can refocus this distributed information. These operations implement what we term {\it Clifford lensing}--transformations that coherently localize phase information onto a reduced set of degrees of freedom, mapping optimal measurements onto observables of reduced Pauli weight. We establish a correspondence between quantum error-correcting codes and interferometric constructions that enforce deterministic phase kickback, and generalize this to circuits that concentrate many-body phase information onto a controllable subset of qubits. We further develop partial shadow tomography protocols for estimating subsystem-supported phases. We experimentally demonstrate these principles in liquid-state nuclear magnetic resonance systems of up to fifteen qubits, achieving optimal sensing with constrained resources. Our results establish a scalable route to coherent control of information flow in interacting quantum systems, enabling many-body quantum sensing and multimode interferometry across complex architectures.

### [54] [Quantum walk with a local spin interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24444)
*Manami Yamagishi,Naomichi Hatano,Kohei Kawabata,Chusei Kiumi,Akinori Nishino,Franco Nori,Hideaki Obuse*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了量子行走者（quantum walker）与局域磁杂质（magnetic impurity）的相互作用模型。首先分析了单量子行走者与磁杂质的束缚态（bound state），然后研究了两量子行走者通过磁杂质间接相互作用的系统，模拟了XX型和SU(2)海森堡型（Heisenberg type）相互作用的碰撞动力学，并探讨了Kondo物理（Kondo physics）的体现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在探索量子行走者与局域磁杂质的相互作用机制，特别是模拟类似于Kondo模型（Kondo model）的物理系统，其中多个量子行走者通过磁杂质产生间接相互作用。

Method: 首先对单量子行走者与磁杂质系统进行解析分析，获得特定参数下的束缚态本征值和本征向量。然后对两量子行走者系统进行数值模拟，研究XX型和SU(2)海森堡型相互作用的碰撞动力学，并使用纠缠负性（entanglement negativity）量化纠缠程度。

Result: 对于XX相互作用，两量子行走者碰撞时纠缠负性急剧增加，且不同统计性质（费米子、玻色子、可区分粒子）的时间依赖性存在差异。对于SU(2)相互作用，最接近单重态（singlet state）的束缚本征态在碰撞中受扰动最小，这被认为是Kondo物理在实空间重整化群（real-space renormalization-group）最低层次的体现。

Conclusion: 研究表明量子行走者与磁杂质的相互作用系统能够展现Kondo物理的基本特征，特别是通过束缚态稳定性和碰撞动力学揭示了类似于Kondo效应的物理机制，为在量子行走框架中研究多体物理现象提供了新视角。

Abstract: We introduce a model of quantum walkers interacting with a magnetic impurity localized at the origin. First, we study a model of a single quantum walker interacting with a localized magnetic impurity. For a simple case of parameter values, we analytically obtain the eigenvalues and the eigenvectors of bound states, in which the quantum walker is bound to the magnetic impurity. Second, we study a model with two quantum walkers and one magnetic impurity, in which the two quantum walkers indirectly interact with each other via the magnetic impurity, as in the Kondo model. We numerically simulate the collision dynamics when the spin-spin interaction at the origin is of the XX type and the SU(2) Heisenberg type. In the case of the XX interaction, we calculate the entanglement negativity to quantify how much the two quantum walkers are entangled with each other, and find that the negativity increases drastically upon the collision of the two walkers. We compare the time dependence for different statistics, namely, fermionic, bosonic, and distinguishable walkers. In the case of the SU(2) interaction, we simulate the dynamics starting from the initial state in which one fermionic walker is in a bound eigenstate around the origin and the other fermionic walker is a delta function colliding with the first walker. We find that a bound eigenstate closest to the singlet state of the first walker and the magnetic impurity is least perturbed by the collision of the second walker. We speculate that this is a manifestation of Kondo physics at the lowest level of the real-space renormalization-group procedure.

</details>


### [55] [Geometric Curvature Governs Work in Open Quantum Steady States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24557)
*Eric R. Bittner*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了开放量子稳态系统中准静态功受控制参数空间中涌现的几何曲率支配，这种曲率源于稳态相干性，为开放量子热力学建立了几何框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典热力学具有几何表述，其中功与状态空间中循环所围面积相关。然而，在驱动、耗散的量子系统中是否保持类似结构仍是一个开放问题。

Method: 针对驱动耗散二能级系统，构建了功一形式（work one-form），其曲率决定了循环过程中产生的功。通过分析强退相干条件下的功消失现象，识别相干性作为非平凡几何的必要条件。

Result: 准静态功由控制参数空间中涌现的几何曲率支配，该曲率源于稳态相干性。功在强退相干下消失，确认相干性是非平凡几何的必要条件。循环方向反转会改变功的符号，证实其几何起源。

Conclusion: 研究结果为开放量子热力学建立了几何框架，并确定曲率作为热力学响应的组织原则，对腔量子电动力学中的驱动光-物质系统具有直接意义。

Abstract: Classical thermodynamics admits a geometric formulation in which work is associated with areas enclosed by cycles in state space. Whether an analogous structure persists in driven, dissipative quantum systems remains an open question. Here we show that quasistatic work in open quantum steady states is governed by an emergent geometric curvature in control-parameter space arising from steady-state coherence. For a driven dissipative two-level system, we construct a work one-form whose curvature determines the work produced in cyclic processes. The work vanishes under strong dephasing, identifying coherence as a necessary condition for nontrivial geometry. However, its magnitude is set not by the coherence itself but by the spatial structure of the curvature: cycles enclosing comparable areas produce different work depending on their location in parameter space. Reversing the cycle orientation reverses the sign of the work, confirming its geometric origin. These results establish a geometric framework for open quantum thermodynamics and identify curvature as the organizing principle of thermodynamic response, with direct implications for driven light--matter systems in cavity quantum electrodynamics.

</details>

### [56] [A visual introduction to curved geometry for physicists](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24409)
*Karol Urbański*

Main category: physics.ed-ph

TL;DR: 本文为熟悉狭义相对论的学生提供微分几何基础概念的视觉化入门介绍，通过可视化方法解释微分几何基本原理，建立对常曲率黎曼流形和洛伦兹流形的直观理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为熟悉狭义相对论的学生提供微分几何基础概念的视觉化入门介绍。通过视觉化方法降低学习门槛，帮助学生建立对微分几何的直观理解，特别是针对黎曼流形（Riemannian manifolds）和洛伦兹流形（Lorentzian manifolds）的常曲率情况。

Method: 采用视觉化方法解释微分几何基本原理，通过可视化推导托马斯进动（Thomas precession）展示微分几何的实用性。同时提出一种适合无微分几何知识学生生成卡特-彭罗斯图（Carter-Penrose diagrams）的简单方法，并展示在时空图上表示扭曲的新方法。

Result: 成功提供了微分几何基础概念的视觉化解释，建立了对常曲率黎曼流形和洛伦兹流形的直观理解。通过托马斯进动的视觉推导，既展示了微分几何的实用性，又突出了闵可夫斯基空间（Minkowski space）中某些教学视角至关重要的复杂性。

Conclusion: 本文通过视觉化方法有效降低了微分几何的学习门槛，为狭义相对论学生提供了直观的入门途径。提出的新方法不仅简化了卡特-彭罗斯图的生成，还改进了时空图中扭曲的表示方式，具有显著的教学价值。

Abstract: This article provides a gentle, visual introduction to the basic concepts of differential geometry appropriate for students familiar with special relativity. Visual methods are used to explain basics of differential geometry and build intuition for all types of Riemannian and Lorentzian manifolds of constant curvature. A visual derivation of the Thomas precession is given, showcasing the utility of differential geometry while also pointing a spotlight at certain intricacies of Minkowski space crucial from a pedagogical perspective. In addition, a straightforward method to generate some Carter-Penrose diagrams -- suitable for students with no differential geometry knowledge -- is presented, and a new method of indicating distortion on spacetime diagrams is shown.

</details>

### [57] [Searching for Anomalies with Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23593)
*Vinicius Mikuni,Benjamin Nachman*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 大型基础模型（foundation model）在CMS实验数据中识别出异常区域，但背景估计在验证区域有效，在信号区域却失效，需要进一步审查。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基础模型（foundation model）有望扩展异常检测的发现能力，但在CMS实验数据中观察到质量边带（mass sideband）的意外行为，需要对此进行完整分析。

Method: 对大型OmniLearned基础模型选定的相空间（phase space）进行完整分析，包括完整的背景估计（background estimate），并在验证区域（validation regions）和信号区域（signal region）分别评估。

Result: 背景估计在验证区域能很好地描述数据，但在信号区域无法准确建模，表明基础模型识别的区域存在异常特征。

Conclusion: 基础模型识别的事件需要进一步审查，同时研究方法也需要更深入的检验，以理解信号区域背景估计失效的原因。

Abstract: Foundation models have the potential to extend the discovery reach for anomaly detection searches. When studying the large OmniLearned foundation model on data from the CMS experiment, unexpected behavior was observed in a mass sideband. The purpose of this paper is to perform a full analysis, including a complete background estimate, on the phase space picked out by the large model. We find that the background estimation describes the data well in validation regions, but is unable to accurately model the signal region. We invite further scrutiny of these events and our methods.

</details>

Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Y. Z. Zhang,Z. Zhang,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文测量了喷注中B±介子的共线（collinear）和横向动量依赖（transverse-momentum-dependent）碎裂函数以及径向分布（radial profile），发现随着喷注横向动量增加，胶子碎裂（gluon fragmentation）对B±介子的贡献逐渐增大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在测量喷注中B±介子的碎裂函数和径向分布，以补充近期关于重味强子（heavy-flavor hadrons）喷注碎裂函数的测量结果，并探索胶子碎裂过程对B±介子产生的贡献。

Method: 使用LHCb探测器在2016-2018年收集的质子-质子对撞数据，质心能量为√s=13 TeV，对应积分亮度5.4 fb⁻¹。B±介子通过J/ψ(→μ⁺μ⁻)K±衰变道进行重建。

Result: 测量了喷注中B±介子的共线碎裂函数、横向动量依赖碎裂函数以及径向分布。结果表明，随着喷注横向动量增加，胶子碎裂对B±介子的贡献逐渐增大。

Conclusion: 该研究补充了重味强子喷注碎裂函数的近期测量结果，揭示了胶子碎裂过程在B±介子产生中的重要性，特别是随着喷注横向动量的增加，胶子碎裂的贡献呈现增长趋势。

Abstract: The collinear and transverse-momentum-dependent jet fragmentation function and the radial profile for $B^{\pm}$ mesons in jets are measured. The $B^{\pm}$ mesons are reconstructed through the $J/ψ(\to μ^{+} μ^{-}) K^{\pm}$ decay channel using proton-proton collision data collected during 2016-2018 with the LHCb detector at a center-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $5.4$ fb$^{-1}$. The results complement recent measurements of jet fragmentation functions for heavy-flavor hadrons and suggest a growing contribution of gluon fragmentation to $B^{\pm}$ mesons as the jet transverse momentum increases.

</details>

K. Zhou,X. R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究利用BESIII探测器收集的J/ψ衰变数据，首次测量了反中子-质子（$\bar{n}p$）非弹性散射到含K介子末态的截面，为研究反核子-核子相互作用提供了新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究反中子-质子（antineutron-proton）相互作用的动机在于探索反核子-核子（antinucleon-nucleon）相互作用的物理特性。通过J/ψ衰变产生反中子的新方法为这类研究提供了独特机会。

Method: 方法基于BESIII探测器在BEPCII储存环收集的$(10087\pm44)\times 10^6$个J/ψ事件。反中子通过J/ψ→pπ⁻$\bar{n}$衰变产生，并通过探测质子和π介子进行标记，反中子动量范围为0-1174 MeV/c，靶质子由束流管材料中的氢提供。

Result: 测量得到$\bar{n}p \rightarrow K^{+}K^{-}π^{+}$反应截面为$0.53^{+0.15}_{-0.12} \pm 0.08$ mb，$\bar{n}p \rightarrow K^{+}K^{-}π^{+}π^{0}$反应截面为$1.09^{+0.36}_{-0.30} \pm 0.31$ mb，其中第一项为统计误差，第二项为系统误差。由于统计量有限，未研究这些过程中的中间态。

Conclusion: 观测到清晰的反中子-质子散射事件表明，该方法在未来研究反中子-质子相互作用方面具有潜力。基于J/ψ衰变产生反中子的新方法为探索反核子-核子相互作用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Based on a novel method for producing antineutrons via $J/ψ$ decays, we report a study of $\bar{n}p$ inelastic scattering into final states containing kaons. The analysis uses $(10087\pm44)\times 10^6$ $J/ψ$ events collected at the BESIII detector operating at the BEPCII storage ring. Antineutrons are produced via $J/ψ\to p π^{-} \bar{n}$ decays and tagged by the detected protons and pions, resulting in antineutron momenta ranging from 0 to 1174~MeV/$c$, while target protons are provided by the hydrogen in the beam-pipe material. The cross sections of the reactions $\bar{n}p \rightarrow K^{+}K^{-}π^{+}$ and $\bar{n}p \rightarrow K^{+}K^{-}π^{+}π^{0}$ are measured to be $0.53^{+0.15}_{-0.12} \pm 0.08$~mb and $1.09^{+0.36}_{-0.30} \pm 0.31$~mb respectively, where the first uncertainties are statistical and the second systematic. Due to limited statistics, the intermediate states in these processes are not investigated. The observation of clean antineutron-proton scattering events indicates the potential of this approach for future investigations of antineutron-proton interactions.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究稀有衰变B⁺→K⁺τ⁺τ⁻对于测试标准模型（Standard Model）和探索新物理（new physics）具有重要意义，因为此类过程在标准模型中受到高度抑制。

Method: 利用Belle和Belle II实验收集的1.2×10⁹个Υ(4S)介子数据，采用全重建（full reconstruction）技术：首先完全重建Υ(4S)→B⁺B⁻衰变中的一个B介子，然后在剩余产物中搜索B⁺→K⁺τ⁺τ⁻候选事例，重建带电K介子和τ轻子（tau lepton）的轻子衰变。

Result: 未观察到显著超出背景（background）的信号，在90%置信水平（confidence level）下设定分支比上限ℬ(B⁺→K⁺τ⁺τ⁻)<0.56×10⁻³，比先前唯一结果改进四倍。

Conclusion: 该研究显著改进了B⁺→K⁺τ⁺τ⁻衰变的分支比上限，为测试标准模型和寻找新物理提供了更严格的约束条件。

Abstract: We report a search for the rare decay $B^{+} \rightarrow K^{+} τ^{+} τ^{-}$ using $1.2 \times 10^9$ $Υ(4S)$ mesons produced near threshold in electron-positron collisions and collected by the Belle and Belle~II experiments. We fully reconstruct the hadronic decay of one $B$ meson produced in the $Υ(4S)\rightarrow B^{+} B^{-}$ decay, and search for $B^{\pm}\rightarrow K^{\pm} τ^{+}τ^{-}$ candidates among the remaining collision products, reconstructing a charged kaon and leptonic decays of the $τ$ leptons. We optimize the selection for best sensitivity and look for an excess over background at low values of the residual energy detected in the calorimeter after full event reconstruction. We observe no significant excess and set the limit $\mathcal{B}(B^{+}\rightarrow K^{+}τ^{+}τ^{-})< 0.56\times 10^{-3}$ at the 90% confidence level, improving on the only previous result by a factor of four.

*H. Abele,G. Angloher,B. Arnold,M. Atzori Corona,A. Bento,E. Bossio,F. Buchsteiner,J. Burkhart,F. Cappella,M. Cappelli,N. Casali,R. Cerulli,A. Cruciani,G. Del Castello,M. del Gallo Roccagiovine,S. Martin,B. Mauri,A. Mazzolari,L. McCallin,H. Neyrial,C. Nones,L. Oberauer,L. Peters,F. Petricca,W. Potzel,F. Pröbst,F. Pucci,F. Reindl,M. Romagnoni,J. Rothe,N. Schermer,J. Schieck,S. Schönert,C. Schwertner,L. Scola,G. Soum-Sidikov,L. Stodolsky,A. Schröder,R. Strauss,R. Thalmeier,C. Tomei,L. Valla,M. Vignati,M. Vivier,A. Wallach,P. Wasser,A. Wex,L. Wienke*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在测量极低核反冲能量（约10 eV量级）下的相干弹性中微子-核散射（CEνNS），这能够实现在极低动量转移下的CEνNS研究，并为新物理提供增强的灵敏度。

Method: 研究开发了一个似然框架，利用反应堆功率变化在低信噪比条件下分离信号和背景，并评估主要系统不确定性的影响。该方法结合了调试期间观测到的低能过剩（LEE）的数据驱动处理。

Result: 对于使用7克CaWO₄靶的技术运行，研究发现对多个超越标准模型（beyond the Standard Model）场景具有竞争性灵敏度，这些场景不需要CEνNS观测。对于物理运行，假设完全抑制低能过剩，预计在1年内能以4.7σ显著性观测CEνNS，统计精度约20%。

Conclusion: 该研究能够实现在迄今CEνNS探测的最低动量转移下测定弱混合角（weak mixing angle），并为中微子电荷半径和新媒介子模型提供领先的基于CEνNS的约束。

Abstract: The NUCLEUS experiment aims to measure coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering (CE$ν$NS) at unprecedentedly low nuclear recoil energies using gram-scale cryogenic calorimeters operated at the Chooz nuclear power plant in France. Access to recoil energies at the $\mathcal{O}(10~\mathrm{eV})$ scale enables CE$ν$NS studies at extremely low momentum transfer and provides enhanced sensitivity to new physics. In this work, we present sensitivity projections for the upcoming NUCLEUS technical and physics runs, incorporating a data-driven treatment of the low-energy excess (LEE) observed during commissioning. We develop a likelihood framework that exploits reactor-power variation to disentangle signal and background in a low signal-to-background regime and to assess the impact of the dominant systematic uncertainties. For the Technical Run with a 7 g CaWO$_4$ target, we find competitive sensitivity to several scenarios beyond the Standard Model, which do not require a CE$ν$NS observation. For the Physics Run, assuming complete suppression of the LEE, we project a 4.7 $σ$ observation of CE$ν$NS with a statistical precision of about 20 % in 1 year, enabling a determination of the weak mixing angle at the lowest momentum transfer probed to date with CE$ν$NS and leading CE$ν$NS-based constraints on the neutrino charge radius and new mediator models.

### [62] [Ising noise filter: physics-informed filtering for particle detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24075)
*I. Kharuk*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出伊辛噪声滤波器（Ising noise filter），这是一种基于图论的可移植预滤波算法，用于粒子加速器和天体物理探测器的早期背景抑制。该方法将探测器命中点映射到二元自旋网络，并通过最小化能量泛函来避免组合爆炸问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于径迹拟合的噪声抑制方法面临严重的组合爆炸问题，需要开发更高效的早期背景抑制算法。该研究旨在为粒子加速器和天体物理探测器提供可移植的预滤波解决方案。

Method: 该方法将单个探测器命中点映射到二元自旋网络，通过最小化能量泛函实现噪声抑制。相互作用核（interaction kernels）基于物理信息设计，针对实验的底层物理和几何特性进行定制。

Result: 在Baikal-GVD中微子望远镜中，该滤波器实现了快速、标准质量的噪声抑制，对天体物理中微子的召回率达到96.8%。在NICA对撞机的SPD探测器中，对玩具蒙特卡洛样本的召回率达到97%。当与Peterson-Hopfield网络结合进行径迹寻找时，物理信息耦合将TrackML得分从0.5提升至0.95。

Conclusion: 伊辛噪声滤波器为粒子物理和天体物理实验提供了一种高效、可移植的早期背景抑制方法。该方法通过物理信息设计的相互作用核有效避免了组合爆炸问题，并在不同实验环境中展现出优异的性能。

Abstract: We present the Ising noise filter, a highly portable, graph-based pre-filtering algorithm for early-stage background suppression in particle accelerators and astrophysical detectors. Standard noise rejection methods relying on track fitting suffer from severe combinatorial explosion. Our method bypasses this by mapping individual detector hits to a network of binary spins and minimizing an energy functional. The interaction kernels are physics-informed, tailored to the underlying physics and geometry of the experiment. We demonstrate the efficacy of this approach in two distinct experimental regimes. Applied to the Baikal-GVD neutrino telescope the filter yields fast, standard-quality noise rejection with 96.8\% recall for astrophysical neutrinos. For the SPD detector at the NICA collider the filter attains recall of 97\% on a toy Monte Carlo sample. Furthermore, when combined with a Peterson--Hopfield network for track finding, our physics-informed coupling improves the TrackML score from 0.5 to 0.95.

</details>


### [63] [Parallel adaptive reweighting importance sampling for Bayesian astrophysics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21249)
*Miaoxin Liu,Alvin J. K. Chua*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为并行自适应重加权重要性采样（PARIS）的新方法，用于高效采样高维多模态后验分布，特别适用于天体物理和引力波天学的贝叶斯推断问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高效采样高维多模态后验分布（high-dimensional, multi-modal posteriors）是贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）在天体物理特别是引力波天文学中的核心挑战。传统的自适应策略（adaptive strategies）在高维多模态场景中表现不佳：难以捕捉复杂的非线性相关性，且超参数（hyperparameters）通常需要繁琐的问题特定调优。

Method: 本文引入并行自适应重加权重要性采样（Parallel Adaptive Reweighting Importance Sampling, PARIS）。该方法将提议分布（proposal distribution）建模为高斯混合模型（Gaussian mixture），其分量中心是现有样本，分量权重与当前重要性权重（importance weights）匹配。新样本从提议分布中抽取，因此集中在高权重区域，同时未探索区域的候选点获得有意膨胀的权重。

Result: PARIS在示例玩具问题和更现实的引力波参数估计（gravitational-wave parameter estimation）任务中进行了评估。该方法实现了准确的后验重建和证据估计（evidence estimation），相比竞争方法显著减少了函数评估次数。

Conclusion: PARIS通过持续重加权所有样本至最新提议分布，实现了任何初始过加权在收集额外邻近样本后的自我校正。该方法展示了在天体物理数据分析中广泛应用的潜力。

Abstract: Efficiently sampling from high-dimensional, multi-modal posteriors is a central challenge in Bayesian inference for astrophysics, especially gravitational-wave astronomy. Popular families of methods like Markov-chain Monte Carlo, nested sampling, and importance sampling all rely on proposal distributions to guide exploration. Because prior knowledge of the target is often limited, practitioners can adopt adaptive proposals that iteratively refine themselves using information gained from previously drawn samples. Traditional adaptive strategies, however, struggle in high-dimensional multi-modal settings: complex, non-linear correlations are hard to capture, and hyperparameters typically require tedious, problem-specific tuning. To address these issues, we introduce Parallel Adaptive Reweighting Importance Sampling (PARIS). PARIS models its proposal as a Gaussian mixture whose component centers are the existing samples and whose component weights match the current importance weights. New draws from the proposal therefore concentrate around high-weight regions, while candidate points in unexplored areas receive intentionally inflated weights. As the algorithm continuously reweights all samples up to the latest proposal, any initial over-weighting self-corrects once additional neighbor samples are collected. To enable rapid reweighting, we present an efficient update scheme and evaluate PARIS on illustrative toy problems and more realistic gravitational-wave parameter estimation tasks. PARIS achieves accurate posterior reconstruction and evidence estimation with substantially fewer function evaluations than competing approaches, highlighting its promise for widespread use in astrophysical data analysis.

</details>


<div id='gr-qc'></div>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [64] [Cosmology with Logarithmic Corrected Horizon Entropy According to the Generalized Entropy and Variable-G Correspondence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23551)
*Chen-Hao Wu,Yen Chin Ong*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 基于GEVAG框架，研究对数修正（logarithmic correction）对早期宇宙学的影响，发现负系数使有效引力常数加倍，正系数使其极小化，后者更自然地实现慢滚暴胀（slow-roll inflation）并可能改善"时间箭头"问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 根据GEVAG框架，对Bekenstein-Hawking面积律的任何修正都会导致变引力常数理论，其中有效引力常数变得与面积相关。特别关注量子引力中的对数修正对早期宇宙学的影响，包括暴胀条件。

Method: 应用GEVAG框架研究对数修正对早期宇宙学的影响，分析不同系数符号下的有效引力常数行为，并与常数引力常数方法进行比较。

Result: 发现对数修正项系数为负时，有效引力常数变为当前值的两倍；系数为正时，有效引力常数变得非常小，这可能改善"时间箭头"问题。慢滚暴胀在后者情况下更为自然，且GEVAG方法可避免负系数时可能出现的突然奇点（sudden singularity）。

Conclusion: GEVAG方法相比常数引力常数方法具有优势，能避免某些奇点问题。研究还检验了广义第二定律的有效性，并对各参数范围进行了讨论。

Abstract: According to the GEVAG (Generalized Entropy Varying-G) framework, any modification to the Bekenstein-Hawking area law would also lead to a varying-$G$ gravity theory in which the effective gravitational constant $G_\text{eff}$ becomes area-dependent. Among a myriad of generalized entropy functions explored in the literature, of special interest is the logarithmic correction of quantum gravity. In this work, we apply GEVAG to investigate the effect of logarithmic correction on very early-time cosmology, including the conditions for inflation. We found that if the coefficient of the logarithmic correction term is negative, $G_\text{eff}$ becomes twice that of the current value; whereas, a positive coefficient leads to a very small value of $G_\text{eff}$, which may ameliorate the "arrow of time" problem. In fact, slow-roll inflation becomes more natural in the latter case. We make some comparisons with the constant-$G$ approach and reveal the advantages of the GEVAG approach. For example, it can evade the sudden singularity that could otherwise arise when the coefficient of the logarithmic correction term is negative. We also check the validity of the generalized second law and comment on the range of the various parameters.

</details>


### [65] [On regular black strings spacetimes in nonlinear electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23556)
*G. Alencar,V. H. U. Borralho,T. M. Crispim,M. S. Cunha*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了广义相对论与非线性电动力学（NED）的耦合，以解决四维黑洞弦的轴向奇点问题。通过模型无关分析，作者证明了在弱场区域恢复麦克斯韦极限的任何NED拉格朗日量都无法产生正则的纯电黑洞弦。尽管如此，他们仍构建了新的精确黑洞弦解，包括Bardeen和Hayward正则黑洞类的柱对称类比。

Method: 采用模型无关分析方法，将球对称时空的"不可行定理"扩展到柱对称情形。通过严格的数学证明，建立了NED拉格朗日量在弱场区域恢复麦克斯韦极限时的基本约束。同时运用特定数学框架构建了新的精确黑洞弦解。

Result: 研究证明，任何在弱场区域恢复麦克斯韦极限的非线性电动力学拉格朗日量都无法产生正则的纯电黑洞弦。然而，成功构建了包括Bardeen和Hayward正则黑洞类柱对称类比的新精确解，这些解的曲率不变量处处有限，用正则核心取代了轴向奇点。

Conclusion: 该研究全面分类了非线性电动力学正则化柱对称时空的条件，揭示了球对称与柱对称之间的拓扑差异如何影响非线性规范理论中非奇异引力对象的全局结构和物理可行性。新构建的精确解通过了严格的因果性和幺正性约束检验。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the coupling of General Relativity with Nonlinear Electrodynamics (NED), governed by a general Lagrangian $\mathcal{L}(\mathcal{F})$, to address the axial singularity of four-dimensional black strings. Through a model-independent analysis, we scrutinize the viability of regular configurations by extending no-go theorems, originally formulated for spherical spacetimes, to cylindrical symmetries. We provide a comprehensive mathematical proof that regular, purely electric black strings cannot be generated by any NED Lagrangian that recovers the Maxwell limit in the weak-field regime, establishing a fundamental constraint for cylindrical topologies. Despite these limitations, we employ specific mathematical frameworks to construct new exact solutions for black strings, including cylindrical analogues of the well-known Bardeen and Hayward regular black hole classes. Each solution is analytically derived, and we demonstrate that their curvature invariants remain finite everywhere, effectively replacing the axial singularity with a regular core. Furthermore, we evaluate the physical consistency of these new metrics by subjecting them to stringent causality and unitarity constraints. Our results provide a comprehensive classification of the conditions under which NED can regularize cylindrical spacetimes and offer new insights into how topological differences between spherical and axial symmetries influence the global structure and the physical viability of non-singular gravitational objects in nonlinear gauge theories.

### [66] [Energy conditions of bouncing solutions in quadratic curvature gravity coupled with a scalar field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23564)
*Yuki Hashimoto,Kazuharu Bamba,Sanjay Mandal*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究检验了在二次曲率引力（quadratic curvature gravity）与标量场最小耦合下产生的非奇异反弹宇宙学解中经典能量条件（energy conditions）的有效性。分析表明，在标量场描述中，零、弱和主导能量条件在整个演化中满足，而强能量条件在反弹阶段必然违反；在有效能量-动量张量描述中，所有四个能量条件在反弹附近都违反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是检验在修改引力理论（modified theories of gravity）背景下，非奇异反弹宇宙学解（nonsingular bouncing cosmological solutions）中经典能量条件的有效性。特别关注二次曲率引力与标量场最小耦合产生的解，旨在澄清高阶曲率项在促进宇宙反弹中的作用。

Method: 研究方法采用系统分析，在两种不同的能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor）表述下检验零、弱、强和主导能量条件（null, weak, strong, and dominant energy conditions）。第一种方法假设能量-动量张量仅由标量场（scalar field）源产生；第二种方法构建有效能量-动量张量，包含表征偏离广义相对论（general relativity）的高阶曲率修正。

Result: 研究结果显示，在标量场描述中，零、弱和主导能量条件在整个宇宙演化过程中保持满足，而强能量条件在反弹阶段必然违反，这使得避免初始奇点（initial singularity）成为可能。相反，当考虑有效能量-动量张量时，所有四个能量条件在反弹附近都违反，突显了基础引力动力学的内在非爱因斯坦性质（non-Einsteinian nature）。

Conclusion: 结论表明，高阶曲率项在促进非奇异宇宙反弹中起关键作用，并阐明了修改引力理论中所需的能量条件违反。这些发现强调了不同能量-动量张量表述下能量条件满足情况的显著差异，为理解修改引力理论中的反弹机制提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We examine the validity of classical energy conditions in nonsingular bouncing cosmological solutions arising in quadratic curvature gravity minimally coupled to a scalar field. Focusing on the null, weak, strong, and dominant energy conditions, we perform a systematic analysis under two distinct formulations of the energy-momentum tensor. In the first approach, the energy-momentum tensor is assumed to be sourced solely by the scalar field, whereas in the second, an effective energy-momentum tensor is constructed that incorporates the higher-curvature corrections characterizing deviations from general relativity. Our results reveal that, in the scalar-field description, the null, weak, and dominant energy conditions remain satisfied throughout the cosmological evolution, while the strong energy condition is necessarily violated during the bounce phase, enabling the avoidance of the initial singularity. In contrast, when the effective energy-momentum tensor is considered, all four energy conditions are violated near the bounce, highlighting the intrinsically non-Einsteinian nature of the underlying gravitational dynamics. These findings clarify the role of higher-order curvature terms in facilitating nonsingular cosmological bounces, providing important insights into the energy condition violations required in modified theories of gravity.

### [67] [Radial Oscillations of Viscous Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23622)
*Lennox S. Keeble,Jaime Redondo-Yuste*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了粘性对中子星径向振荡模式的影响，发现粘性在毫秒时间尺度上阻尼振荡，并引起振荡频率的分数偏移，偏移量随星体致密度和粘性增加而增大。对于高粘性情况，振荡频率降低甚至变为零（过阻尼模式）。研究还表明粘性无法稳定不稳定的无粘性星体，但会轻微改变引力坍缩阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星振荡模式是第三代引力波探测器的关键目标，编码了其组成核物质的关键信息。本研究旨在探讨粘性对冷、多方、球对称中子星振荡的影响，以增进对粘性星震学（viscous asteroseismology）的理解。

Method: 研究聚焦于纯径向振荡，在线性阶微扰框架内采用两种流体动力学理论：Eckart提出的非因果协变Navier-Stokes方程推广，以及Bemfica、Disconzi、Noronha和Kovtun（BDNK）提出的因果推广理论。研究在微扰框架内分析粘性效应。

Result: 粘性在毫秒时间尺度上阻尼径向模式，并引起振荡频率的分数偏移，偏移量随星体致密度和粘性增加而增大。对于体粘性ζ∼10³⁰ g/cm/s的基本模式，偏移可达百分之一水平。对于更高粘性（ζ≳10³¹ g/cm/s），振荡频率降低为零，形成过阻尼模式。在引力坍缩方面，两种理论中的粘性均无法稳定不稳定的无粘性星体，但BDNK理论中的粘性会轻微改变坍缩阈值。

Conclusion: 研究结果增进了对粘性影响中子星振荡模式的理解，这是下一代引力波探测器进行粘性星震学研究的关键组成部分。粘性效应在星体振荡中具有显著影响，特别是在高粘性条件下会导致模式过阻尼。

Abstract: Oscillation modes of neutron stars, a key target for third-generation gravitational wave detectors, encode key information about their constituent nuclear matter. In this work, we study the effect of viscosity on oscillations of cold, polytropic, spherically symmetric neutron stars. We focus on purely radial oscillations and work perturbatively to linear order within two hydrodynamic frameworks: the acausal covariant generalization of the Navier-Stokes equations proposed by Eckart, and the causal generalization formulated by Bemfica, Disconzi, Noronha, and Kovtun (BDNK). We find that viscosity damps the radial modes on millisecond timescales and induces fractional shifts in the oscillation frequency which increase both with the compactness and viscosity of the star, reaching up to the percent level for the fundamental mode with bulk viscosities $ζ\sim10^{30}\mathrm{g}/\mathrm{cm}/\mathrm{s}$. For more viscous stars, the oscillation frequency decreases, becoming zero (i.e., an overdamped mode) for $ζ\gtrsim10^{31}\mathrm{g}/\mathrm{cm}/\mathrm{s}$. We also study the linear threshold of gravitational collapse. Consistent with recent analytic results in the small viscosity regime, we find that viscosity in Eckart theory cannot stabilize an unstable inviscid star. We provide numerical evidence that viscosity in BDNK theory is similarly unable to prevent gravitational collapse, but it slightly modifies the threshold of collapse. Overall, our results advance our understanding of the impact of viscosity on the oscillation modes of neutron stars, a key component of viscous asteroseismology with next-generation gravitational wave detectors.

### [68] [Testing Dark Energy with Black Hole Ringdown](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23634)
*Laurens Smulders,Johannes Noller,Sergi Sirera*

TL;DR: 本文研究表明，动力学暗能量（dynamical dark energy）理论可在黑洞铃荡（ringdown）的准正则模（quasi-normal mode）谱上产生O(1)量级的修正。通过以立方伽利略子（cubic Galileon）为例，作者建立了宇宙学与黑洞区域间的参数化联系，推导了诱导的准正则模偏移，并预测了暗能量约束能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动力学暗能量理论的时间依赖性自然导致黑洞周围形成宇宙学"毛发"（cosmological 'hair'）。本文旨在探索这种宇宙学毛发如何影响黑洞的准正则模谱，从而为暗能量约束提供新途径。

Method: 以立方伽利略子作为具体案例，这是目前已知唯一稳定的此类解。作者参数化地连接了宇宙学与黑洞区域，推导了诱导的准正则模偏移，并对暗能量约束进行了预测。

Result: 研究发现，动力学暗能量可在黑洞铃荡的准正则模谱上产生O(1)量级的修正。对于LVK（LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA）合作组，暗能量场轮廓的约束精度可达10^{-2}；对于LISA（Laser Interferometer Space Antenna）任务，约束精度可达10^{-4}。

Conclusion: 黑洞铃荡的准正则模谱为探测动力学暗能量提供了新窗口。通过分析准正则模偏移，可对暗能量场轮廓施加严格约束，为引力波天文学开辟了新的暗能量探测途径。

Abstract: We show that dynamical dark energy theories can imprint $O(1)$ modifications on the quasi-normal mode (QNM) spectrum characterising black hole ringdown. The time dependence of dynamical dark energy naturally gives rise to cosmological 'hair' around a black hole. Taking the cubic Galileon as a concrete example, which admits the only known stable solution of this kind, we parametrically connect the cosmological and black hole regimes, derive the induced QNM shifts and forecast the resulting dark energy constraints. We find that the dark energy field profile can be constrained with an accuracy of up to $10^{-2}$ for LVK and $10^{-4}$ for LISA.

### [69] [A rotating GUP black hole: metric, shadow, and bounds on quantum parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23680)
*Federica Fragomeno,Samantha Hergott,Saeed Rastgoo,Evan Vienneau*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次将修正的纽曼-詹尼斯算法应用于静态球对称广义不确定性原理启发的量子黑洞度规，推导出其旋转对应版本，并分析了该模型的奇点结构、热力学性质及与事件视界望远镜观测数据的约束关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于首次推导出的静态球对称广义不确定性原理（generalized uncertainty principle）启发的量子黑洞度规，需要将其扩展到旋转情况以更符合实际天体物理场景。

Method: 采用修正的纽曼-詹尼斯算法（modified Newman-Janis algorithm）将静态球对称量子黑洞度规转化为旋转版本，并计算了该黑洞的视界位置、温度、熵、阴影参数等物理量。

Result: 结果显示：1）旋转度规在静态情况下已解决的奇点因纽曼-詹尼斯算法副作用重新引入，但慢旋转极限下无奇点；2）量子参数改变了视界位置、温度和熵，并允许自旋参数与质量比小于1时存在裸奇点（naked singularities）；3）通过对比M87*和Sgr A*的事件视界望远镜数据，为量子参数设定了约束界限。

Conclusion: 结论表明：修正的纽曼-詹尼斯算法成功生成了旋转量子黑洞度规，该模型具有正确的极限行为；量子参数显著影响黑洞热力学性质；通过与观测数据对比，为模型参数设定了约束，并显示若模型有效，M87*的自转角动量存在上限。

Abstract: Recently, for the first time, a metric of a static spherically symmetric generalized uncertainty inspired quantum black hole was derived. We apply the modified Newman-Janis algorithm to this metric and derive its rotating counterpart. We show that this metric has all the correct limits, while due to Newman-Janis side effects, the singularity which was resolved in the static case, is introduced back into the model. However, the slowly-rotating limit of this black hole is singularity-free. Furthermore, we show that the presence of quantum parameters modifies the location of the horizons, temperature, and entropy of the black hole, and allows the existence of naked singularities even if the ratio of the spin parameter to mass of the black hole is less than unity. Finally, by computing the shadow parameters of this black hole and comparing them with data from the Event Horizon Telescope for both M87* and Sgr A*, we set bounds on one of the quantum parameters of the model, and show that there is a limit on the angular momentum of M87* if this model is valid.

Abstract: We analyze various gravity theories involving de-Sitter, quadratic $\mathcal{R}^2$ and non-minimally coupled scalar in the light of application of the Dyson-Schwinger technique involving exact background solution of the Green's function. We denote specific set of solutions for the metric to move towards a quantum analysis of the theory. This kind of solutions is identified as conformally flat metric. Such a conclusion naturally arises in the use of the Dyson-Schwinger equations in the study of the Yang-Mills theory through the mapping theorem. We show a sequence of cosmological phase transitions starting from the breaking of such conformal invariance that can be hindered by the presence of the non-minimal coupling.

Abstract: We develop a comprehensive thermodynamic description for a zero-temperature boson gas in curved spacetime, integrating energy conservation with information-theoretic principles. ### [72] [Bouncing Cosmological Models and Energy Conditions in $f(Q, L_m)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24162)
*S. A. Kadam,V. A. Kshirsagar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究在修正的$f(Q, L_m)$引力框架下探索反弹解，分析了对称反弹、超反弹、振荡反弹和物质反弹四种模型，通过哈勃参数、尺度因子演化及状态方程参数验证了反弹场景的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索修正$f(Q, L_m)$引力理论框架下的反弹宇宙学解，分析不同反弹模型在该理论中的表现，以验证修正引力理论对宇宙早期反弹场景的适用性。

Method: 研究方法包括在修正$f(Q, L_m)$引力理论中检验四种反弹模型：对称反弹（symmetric bounce）、超反弹（super bounce）、振荡反弹（oscillatory bounce）和物质反弹（matter bounce）。分析重点关注哈勃参数（Hubble parameter）、尺度因子（scale factor）演化以及状态方程（equation of state, EoS）参数的行为。

Result: 研究结果显示，尺度因子和哈勃参数的动力学有效支持反弹场景。在反弹时期，状态方程参数落入幽灵区域（phantom region），进一步证实了反弹的可行性。通过评估各模型的能量条件，发现反弹时期零能量条件（null energy condition）被违反，这成功刻画了模型的反弹行为特征。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，在修正$f(Q, L_m)$引力框架下，四种反弹模型均能有效实现宇宙反弹场景，反弹时期的状态方程参数处于幽灵区域且零能量条件被违反，验证了该理论对反弹宇宙学模型的适用性。

Abstract: This study explores the bouncing solutions within the framework of modified $f(Q, L_m)$ gravity. We examine four prominent bouncing models, the symmetric bounce, super bounce, oscillatory bounce, and matter bounce, each of which has been extensively analyzed in the context of modified gravity theories. Our investigation focuses on the behavior of the Hubble parameter, the evolution of the scale factor, and the equation of state (EoS) parameters. Notably, the dynamics of the scale factor and Hubble parameter effectively support the bouncing scenario. During the bouncing epoch, the EoS parameters fall within the phantom region, reinforcing the viability of the bounce. To further validate the bouncing scenario, we assess the energy conditions associated with each model. Our findings reveal a violation of the null energy condition at the bouncing epoch, which successfully characterizes the model's bouncing behavior.

</details>


### [73] [Phase Structure of Scalarized Black Holes in Einstein-Scalar-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24164)
*Carlos Herdeiro,Hyat Huang,Jutta Kunz,Meng-Yun Lai,Eugen Radu,De-Cheng Zou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文重新审视爱因斯坦-标量-高斯-博内引力中的标量化黑洞，分析广义相对论史瓦西解与标量化黑洞之间的热力学相变结构，发现相变类型由标量-高斯-博内耦合函数决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探究爱因斯坦-标量-高斯-博内（Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet）引力理论中标量化黑洞的热力学性质，特别是分析广义相对论史瓦西（Schwarzschild）解与标量化黑洞之间的相变行为。

Method: 研究限制于球对称构型，考察了多类标量-高斯-博内耦合函数：包括触发自发标量化（spontaneous scalarization）的最简单二次耦合、指数耦合，以及导致纯非线性标量化（purely nonlinear scalarization）的耦合函数。

Result: 对于二次耦合，标量化解在热力学上不利，无相变发生；指数耦合的相结构强烈依赖于耦合参数，可能出现无相变、连续二阶相变（second-order transition）或不连续一阶相变（first-order transition）；纯非线性标量化耦合则导致一阶相变或无相变。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了标量化黑洞丰富的相结构，这些结构完全由标量-高斯-博内耦合函数控制，表明耦合函数的选择决定了黑洞解之间的热力学相变类型和性质。

Abstract: We revisit scalarized black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity and analyze the thermodynamic phase transition between the Schwarzschild solution of general relativity and scalarized black holes. Restricting to spherically symmetric configurations, we investigate several classes of scalar-Gauss-Bonnet coupling functions. For the simplest quadratic coupling that triggers spontaneous scalarization, the scalarized solutions are thermodynamically disfavored and no phase transition occurs. For an exponential coupling, the phase structure depends strongly on the coupling parameter, allowing for the absence of a transition, a continuous second-order transition, or a discontinuous first-order transition. For couplings leading to purely nonlinear scalarization, we find either a first-order transition or no transition. These results reveal a rich phase structure of scalarized black holes controlled by the scalar-Gauss-Bonnet coupling.

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种用于处理壳层穿越奇点（shell-crossing singularities）产生激波（shocks）的规范选择方法，解决了先前分析中因不当规范选择导致的问题，为研究广义协变有效黑洞模型中的激波动力学提供了基础框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前对壳层穿越奇点（shell-crossing singularities）产生激波的分析受到不当规范选择的影响，且缺乏选择一致规范的系统性方法。这解释了先前处理中的困难。

Method: 本研究为有效量子引力（effective quantum gravity）与尘埃壳层（dust shell）耦合系统开发了一种规范选择方法。该方法在经典广义相对论（classical general relativity）中进行了说明，并通过数值模拟进行了验证。

Result: 数值验证结果与以色列连接条件（Israel junction condition）一致。研究还表明，当在整个空间切片上施加时，Painlevé-Gullstrand和Schwarzschild等规范与尘埃壳层的存在不兼容。

Conclusion: 本研究开发的框架为研究广义协变有效黑洞模型（generally covariant effective black-hole models）中的壳层穿越奇点和激波动力学提供了基础。

Abstract: Previous analyses of shocks generated by shell-crossing singularities are affected by inappropriate gauge choices, and no systematic method is available for selecting a consistent gauge. In this work, we develop such a method for effective quantum gravity coupled to a dust shell. We illustrate it in classical general relativity and verify it numerically, with results in agreement with the Israel junction condition. We also show that gauges such as the Painlevé-Gullstrand and Schwarzschild ones are incompatible with the presence of a dust shell when imposed on the whole spatial slice. This explains the difficulties in previous treatments. The framework developed here provides a basis for studying shell-crossing singularities and shock dynamics in generally covariant effective black-hole models.

### [75] [Thermodynamic, Optical, and Orbital Signatures of Regular Asymptotically Flat Black Holes in Quasi-Topological Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24212)
*Zainab Malik*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究对一类由变形静态球对称度规描述的规则渐近平坦黑洞进行了解析和数值表征。通过分析视界存在条件、霍金温度、阴影半径、光子环李雅普诺夫指数等物理量，揭示了变形参数如何影响黑洞的热力学、光学特征和吸积过程。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法基于变形静态球对称度规，从视界存在条件和规则性出发推导允许参数域和极值界限。随后分析霍金温度、阴影半径、光子环李雅普诺夫指数和ISCO结合效率等物理量。进一步扩展到Novikov-Thorne薄盘吸积模型，推导通量核、有效温度分布和测光光度标度。

Result: 结果显示一致趋势：增加变形参数使解偏离史瓦西行为，降低温度、阴影尺寸和光子轨道不稳定率，同时增强轨道结合效率和吸积光度；增加指数ν则抑制变形效应并恢复类史瓦西可观测量。研究提供了连接视界结构、热力学、光学特征、动力学不稳定性和薄盘吸积诊断的紧凑现象学映射。

Conclusion: 该研究系统表征了规则黑洞家族中变形参数对物理观测量的影响，建立了从微观结构到宏观观测的完整现象学联系，为理解规则黑洞的物理特性提供了全面框架。

Abstract: This study provides an analytic and numerical characterization of a class of regular, asymptotically flat black holes described by a deformed static spherical metric. The model is grounded in a four-dimensional non-polynomial quasi-topological framework in which higher-curvature corrections remain dynamically nontrivial while the static spherical sector retains a reduced-order structure, enabling tractable black-hole solutions with regular cores. Starting from the existence conditions of horizons and regularity, the allowed parameter domain and the extremal bound are derived. Hawking temperature, shadow radius, photon-ring Lyapunov exponent, and ISCO binding efficiency are then analyzed across the physically allowed parameter space. We further extend the analysis to Novikov--Thorne thin-disk accretion by deriving the flux kernel, effective-temperature profile, and bolometric luminosity scaling, and by providing representative numerical datasets for these quantities. A coherent trend emerges: increasing the deformation parameter drives the solution away from Schwarzschild behavior, reducing temperature, shadow size, and photon-orbit instability rate while enhancing orbital binding efficiency and accretion luminosity; increasing the exponent $ν$ suppresses deformation effects and restores Schwarzschild-like observables. These results provide a compact phenomenological map linking horizon structure, thermodynamics, optical signatures, dynamical instability, and thin-disk accretion diagnostics in this regular black-hole family.

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种将quintessence势能导数与直接可观测宇宙学参数联系起来的解析方法，避免了状态方程参数w的显式依赖，为暗能量模型的观测约束提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We derive expressions for the first and second derivatives of the quintessence potential $V(φ)$, in terms of $λ= -V^{\prime}/V$ and $Γ= (V^{\prime \prime}/V)/(V^\prime/V)^2$, as functions of the quintessence density fraction $Ω_φ$ and the cosmographic parameters $q$, $j$, and $s$. Our mapping is not explicitly a function of the equation of state parameter $w$. We use these results, along with recent observational data, to derive expansions of $V(φ)$ about the present-day value of the scalar field, $φ_0$.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一套研究广泛引力理论中恒星平衡问题的通用工具，展示了引力强度减弱带来的普遍效应，包括Buchdahl极限的缓解和规则黑洞静态解的存在性，为超越广义相对论的引力理论研究提供了分析框架。

Abstract: We provide a set of general tools to study the problem of stellar equilibrium in any gravitational theory in which spherically symmetric spacetimes satisfy master field equations taking the form of an equality between an identically conserved tensor, with derivatives of up to second order in the metric, and an identically conserved matter tensor. We derive the most general expression for the Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff equation of stellar equilibrium that is compatible with these minimal requirements. A general discussion of the conditions that guarantee geodesic completeness at the center of symmetry is also presented. The equations of stellar equilibrium are integrated in a subset of the space of allowed deformations of general relativity proposed by Ziprick and Kunstatter, allowing us to illustrate universal aspects associated with the weakening of the strength of gravity, such as the mitigation of the Buchdahl limit obtained in general relativity or the existence of static solutions describing regular black holes with perfect fluid cores.

Result: 结果显示场质量增加会减少阻尼并驱动系统趋向长寿命的准共振行为；散射截面遵循相同的势垒物理，有效势垒增大抑制了透射和低频吸收，而高斯-博内特耦合在稳定范围内影响相对温和。

Abstract: We analyze quasinormal modes, grey-body factors, and absorption cross-sections of a massive scalar field in four-dimensional Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet black-hole spacetimes within a stability-constrained coupling window. High-order WKB-Padé spectra show that increasing field mass typically reduces damping and drives the system toward long-lived, quasi-resonant behavior. The scattering sector follows the same potential-barrier physics: larger effective barriers suppress transmission and low-frequency absorption, while the Gauss--Bonnet coupling has a comparatively mild impact over the stable range. These results provide a compact baseline for massive-field spectroscopy in higher-curvature black-hole backgrounds.

### [80] [Magnetic-monopole resummation justifies perturbatively calculated collider production cross sections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24200)
*Jean Alexandre,Nick E. Mavromatos,Vasiliki A. Mitsou,Emanuela Musumeci*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种受Dyson-Schwinger形式启发的单圈重整化方案，应用于自旋1/2磁单极子的有效场论，发现了非微扰的紫外固定点结构，为对撞机中树级磁单极子产生过程提供了形式化理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在为对撞机搜索中使用的树级Drell-Yan和光子融合磁单极子（MM）产生过程提供形式化理论依据。当前缺乏对磁单极子产生截面对应的质量界限的严格理论支持，需要通过非微扰方法解决强耦合问题。

Method: 采用受强耦合量子场论Dyson-Schwinger（DS）形式启发的单圈重整化方案（one-loop resummation scheme），应用于U(1)_em × U(1)'规范群不变的有效场论（EFT）。该方法主要针对基本（无结构）磁单极子，但也可应用于复合磁单极子对形成的最后阶段。

Result: 在重整化理论中发现了纯粹非微扰的紫外固定点（ultra-violet fixed point）结构。实现了重整化耦合与磁荷的自洽识别，该识别与狄拉克量子化条件（Dirac quantization condition）兼容。这为对撞机搜索中使用的树级产生过程及其对应截面和质量界限提供了首次形式化理论支持。

Conclusion: DS重整化方案为磁单极子有效场论提供了非微扰理论框架，使得对撞机搜索中使用的树级产生过程获得理论正当性。该方法不仅适用于基本磁单极子，还可扩展至复合磁单极子形成过程，为通过实验约束重整化EFT参数提供了途径。

Abstract: A one-loop resummation scheme, inspired by Dyson-Schwinger (DS) formalism of strongly coupled quantum field theories, is applied to spin-1/2 magnetic monopoles (MMs), in the context of an effective field theory (EFT), invariant under the gauge group U(1)_em x U(1)', where U(1)' is a dual strongly coupled Abelian interaction, associated with a "dark photon". An ultra-violet fixed point structure is found in the resummed theory, which is purely non-perturbative, due to different boundary conditions of the resummation equations, compared to the weak coupling (perturbative) case. A self-consistent identification of the renormalized coupling of the MM to the electromagnetic photon in the fixed-point theory with the magnetic charge, compatible with the Dirac quantization condition, is made. This provides for the first time a formal justification of the use of tree-level Drell-Yan and photon-fusion MM production processes in collider searches, and of the corresponding cross sections and MM mass bounds thereof. The latter provide a means to constrain the resummed-EFT parameters experimentally. The DS resummation applies here primarily to the case of elementary (structureless) MMs. However, this approach may also be applied to the last stage (collapse) of the formation of composite MM pairs at colliders, in case they behave as quantum excitations, with their core radius comparable to the Compton wavelength, thereby avoiding the extreme suppression of their production.

</details>


### [81] [Chiral enhancement in the vector-like fourth family: Case of $b \to s γ$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24267)
*Junichiro Kawamura,Yuji Omura*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明向量型第四代夸克（vector-like fourth family of quarks）在$b\to sγ$过程中诱导了标准模型（Standard Model）中不存在的真正手征增强（chiral enhancement）。这种增强源于双重态和单重态共存使得手征翻转（chirality flip）可在圈内发生，导致与重向量型质量成正比的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型中的$b\to sγ$过程缺乏真正的手征增强效应。研究向量型第四代夸克如何通过其独特的双重态和单重态共存特性，在圈内实现手征翻转，从而产生显著增强效应。

Method: 通过引入向量型第四代夸克，利用其双重态和单重态共存特性，使手征翻转发生在圈内而非外部费米子线上。分析由此产生的与重向量型质量成正比的贡献，并计算增强因子$\overlineλ_d v_H/m_b$。

Result: 发现增强因子可达$\mathcal{O}(40)$，即使对于$\mathcal{O}(\mathrm{TeV})$量级的向量型夸克质量和小的混合角，也能导致与标准模型预测的显著偏差。在众多精密观测量中，$\mathrm{Br}(\overline{B}\to X_sγ)$分支比对这种场景提供了最严格的约束。

Conclusion: 向量型第四代夸克在$b\to sγ$过程中诱导了显著的手征增强效应，这种效应源于圈内手征翻转机制。该增强效应即使在TeV尺度质量和小的混合角下仍可观测，为探测新物理提供了敏感探针。

Abstract: We demonstrate that a vector-like fourth family of quarks induces a genuine chiral enhancement in $b\to sγ$, which is absent in the Standard Model (SM). The coexistence of doublet and singlet states allows the chirality flip to occur inside the loop, leading to contributions proportional to the heavy vector-like mass. The resulting amplitude is enhanced by a factor $\overlineλ_d v_H/m_b$, which can be as large as $\mathcal{O}(40)$ for moderate Yukawa couplings. This leads to sizable deviation from the SM prediction even for $\mathcal{O}(\mathrm{TeV})$ vector-like quark masses and small mixing angles. We find that $\mathrm{Br}(\overline{B}\to X_sγ)$ provides the most stringent constraint on this scenario among a wide range of precision observables.

</details>


### [82] [Dynamical generation of charmonium-like tetraquarks in an off-shell coupled-channel formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24271)
*Hee-Jin Kim,Hyun-Chul Kim*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了粲偶素态（charmonium-like states）在3.6-4.3 GeV质量范围内的动力学生成，通过离壳耦合道（off-shell coupled-channel）形式论识别了六个极点，包括标量、轴矢量、张量和矢量态，其中χ_{c1}(3872)被重现为D\bar{D}^*阈值附近的束缚态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究粲偶素态（charmonium-like states）在3.6-4.3 GeV质量范围内的动力学生成机制，特别关注自旋宇称（spin-parity）为J^{PC}=0^{++}, 1^{++}, 2^{++}和3^{--}的态。研究动机源于理解这些奇特态（exotic states）的形成是否源于强子分子态（hadronic molecular states）的耦合道动力学。

Method: 采用离壳耦合道形式论（off-shell coupled-channel formalism），基于尊重重夸克自旋味对称性（heavy-quark spin-flavor symmetry）和手征对称性（chiral symmetry）的有效拉格朗日量（effective Lagrangians）构建核振幅（kernel amplitudes）。为聚焦于动力学生成态，明确排除了s-道极点图（s-channel pole diagrams），仅包含t-道和u-道介子交换（t- and u-channel meson exchanges），并通过求解积分方程识别复能量平面上的极点。

Result: 在复能量平面上识别了六个极点：标量（0^{++}）区发现一个低于D\bar{D}阈值的束缚态和一个位于√s_R=(3861-i23) MeV的共振态；轴矢量（1^{++}）区重现了实验观测到的χ_{c1}(3872)作为D\bar{D}^*阈值附近的束缚态，以及一个位于(3961-i32) MeV的更宽共振态，后者可能是X(3940)的候选者；此外还发现了一个位于4005 MeV的窄张量（2^{++}）态和一个位于4030 MeV的矢量（3^{--}）态。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，耦合道动力学（coupled-channel dynamics），特别是涉及D^*\bar{D}^*道的相互作用，在粲偶素奇特态（charmonium-like exotic states）的形成中起着关键作用。该方法成功重现了已知态如χ_{c1}(3872)并预测了新的共振态，为理解这些奇特态的结构提供了理论支持。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamical generation of charmonium-like ($I=0$) with spin-parity $J^{PC}=0^{++}, 1^{++}, 2^{++}$, and $3^{--}$ in the mass range of $3.6$ to $4.3$ GeV. We employ the off-shell coupled-channel formalism, constructing kernel amplitudes from effective Lagrangians that respect heavy-quark spin-flavor and chiral symmetries. To focus solely on dynamically generated states, we explicitly exclude $s$-channel pole diagrams and include only $t$- and $u$-channel meson exchanges. Solving the integral equations, we identify six poles in the complex energy plane. In the scalar ($0^{++}$) sector, we find a bound state below the $D\bar{D}$ threshold and a resonance at $\sqrt{s_R}=(3861-i\,23)\,\mathrm{MeV}$. For the axial-vector ($1^{++}$) sector, the experimentally observed $χ_{c1}(3872)$ is reproduced as a bound state near the $D\bar{D}^*$ threshold, alongside a broader resonance at $(3961-i\,32)\,\mathrm{MeV}$, which is a plausible candidate for the $X(3940)$. Furthermore, we find a narrow tensor ($2^{++}$) state at $4005\,\mathrm{MeV}$ and a vector ($3^{--}$) state at $4030\,\mathrm{MeV}$. The present results demonstrate that coupled-channel dynamics, particularly involving the $D^*\bar{D}^*$ channel, play a crucial role in the formation of these charmonium-like exotic states.

### [83] [A Breath of Fresh Air for Molière: Detecting Molière Scattering using Jet Substructure Observables in Oxygen Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23596)
*Arjun Srinivasan Kudinoor,Arthur Yi-Ting Lin,Daniel Pablos,Krishna Rajagopal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过混合强/弱耦合模型分析超相对论氧-氧碰撞中的喷注-介质相互作用，发现Molière散射对于解释CMS实验数据至关重要，并首次理论研究了喷注内部结构在OO碰撞中的改变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超相对论氧-氧（OO）碰撞为研究高能喷注部分子与夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）中准粒子之间的大角度、高动量转移Molière散射提供了理想平台。这些稀有散射事件有助于探测QGP中短距离尺度上出现的准粒子特性。

Method: 采用混合强/弱耦合模型（hybrid strong/weak coupling model），在模型中纳入喷注部分子与介质准粒子之间的Molière散射。通过分析Soft Drop分裂角R_g和能量-能量关联函数（EECs）来研究喷注内部结构的变化。

Result: Molière散射显著增宽了Soft Drop分裂角R_g，导致OO碰撞中R=0.4和R=0.8喷注的R_g≥0.2比例相对于pp碰撞增加。能量-能量关联函数显示大角度关联增强，反映了喷注诱导的尾流和Molière散射效应。对于R_jet∼0.8的喷注，EEC中印刻了Molière散射导致的偏转角尺度。

Conclusion: 喷注子结构测量在OO碰撞中是探测强耦合介质中短距离准粒子的有前景途径。OO/pp比值若如计算所示高于1，可作为硬散射QGP准粒子的模型独立探测信号。这些结果为理解QGP微观结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: Ultra-relativistic oxygen-oxygen (OO) collisions are a promising arena in which to probe rare, large-angle, high momentum-transfer $2\rightarrow2$ Molière scatterings between energetic jet partons and quasiparticles in quark-gluon plasma (QGP). As a jet propagates through the droplet of QGP formed in the same collision, its constituents lose energy to and excite wakes in the medium, and may scatter off quark- and gluon-like quasiparticles in QGP. Using the hybrid strong/weak coupling model, we show that including Molière scatterings between jet partons and medium quasiparticles is essential to reproduce recent CMS measurements of charged-particle suppression in OO collisions with this model. We then present the first theoretical study of how jet-medium interactions modify the internal structure of jets in OO collisions. We find that Molière scatterings broaden the Soft Drop splitting angle $R_g$, enhancing the population of $R=0.4$ and $R=0.8$ jets with $R_g\gtrsim0.2$ in OO collisions relative to pp collisions. Energy-energy correlators (EECs) provide a complementary probe, exhibiting enhanced large-angle correlations within jets due to jet-induced wakes and Molière scattering. In both cases, we propose an experimental measurement where the relevant OO/pp ratio can, if enhanced above unity in future data as in our calculations, be a distinctive, model-independent, detection of hard scattering off QGP quasiparticles. We furthermore use our calculations of EECs to show how the angular scale corresponding to the deflection of jet or medium partons by Molière scattering is imprinted in the EEC for jets with radius $R_{\rm jet}\sim0.8$ in OO collisions. These results demonstrate that jet substructure measurements in OO collisions are promising avenues to probe the quasiparticles that emerge at short distances within an otherwise strongly coupled medium.

Method: 在Reissner-Nordstrom、Hayward和Simpson-Visser度规下，采用解析和数值方法研究中微子振荡中的引力调制CP破坏。通过分析味振荡曲线的形态特征，探索参数间的相互影响。

Conclusion: 引力调制的中微子CP破坏可作为识别时空背景特征的探针。通过分析振荡曲线的振幅和周期变化，可同时获取中微子质量信息和引力参数，为探索弯曲时空中的中微子物理提供新视角。

Abstract: Flavor oscillations in curved space-time provide a novel channel to explore the unknown parameters of neutrinos. In this work, the gravity-modulated CP violations (CPVs) in neutrino oscillations were investigated under the Reissner-Nordstrom, Hayward, and Simpson-Visser metric. The interplay among the CPV, the properties of neutrinos, and the space-time is illustrated with analytical and numerical methods. The morphologies of the flavor-oscillation curves show that the information on the mass-ordering, the absolute mass, and the gravitational parameters could be encoded into the amplitudes and periods of the CPVs. Hence, the characteristic of the space-time background may be identified through its modulation effects on the CPV, such as amplification, damping on the amplitudes.

### [85] [Meson mixing effects on the speed of sound in isospin-imbalanced matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23760)
*Alejandro Ayala,Bruno S. Lopes,Ricardo L. S. Farias,Luis C. Parra*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在线性西格玛模型框架下研究同位旋不平衡强相互作用物质，发现同位旋凝聚必然产生戈德斯通模，该模通过带电π介子与σ场混合强制建立手征凝聚与同位旋凝聚的非平凡关系，并解释了声速峰值的位置和形状。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索同位旋不平衡强相互作用物质的性质，使用双味线性西格玛模型（two-flavor Linear Sigma Model）作为低能QCD的有效模型。关注同位旋化学势下物质的热力学行为及其与手征对称性的关系。

Method: 采用单圈阶（one loop order）计算，同时包含夸克、π介子和σ介子的涨落，并保持手征对称性。通过热力学势计算声速，分析戈德斯通模（Goldstone mode）对凝聚相中带电π介子与σ场混合的影响。

Result: 发现同位旋凝聚的形成必然产生戈德斯通模，该模强制建立了手征凝聚与同位旋凝聚之间的非平凡关系。声速作为同位旋化学势的函数出现显著峰值，虽然该峰值可在树图阶仅包含夸克的分析中描述，但介子动力学引入了进一步约束，影响峰值的位置和宽度。

Conclusion: 声速峰值的位置和形状是戈德斯通模动力学及相关带电π介子-σ混合的结果。介子动力学的包含使理论预测与格点QCD模拟（lattice QCD simulations）良好吻合，突显了戈德斯通模在理解同位旋不平衡强相互作用物质中的关键作用。

Abstract: We explore isospin imbalanced strongly interacting matter within the two-flavor Linear Sigma Model with quarks, an effective model for low-energy QCD. At one loop order, including quark, pion, and sigma fluctuations while respecting chiral symmetry, we find that the formation of an isospin condensate necessarily gives rise to a Goldstone mode. This mode enforces a nontrivial relation between the chiral and isospin condensates through the mixing of charged pions and the sigma field in the condensed phase. From the resulting thermodynamic potential, we compute the speed of sound and observe a pronounced peak as a function of the isospin chemical potential. Although the peak of the speed of sound may be described at tree-level and including only quarks in the analysis, meson dynamics introduces further constraints that influence the position and width of the peak which making it to align well with lattice QCD simulations. Therefore we identify that the shape and position of the peak is a consequence of the Goldstone mode dynamics and of the associated charged pion sigma mixing.

Abstract: An attempt to evade the strict uniqueness of consistent interactions involving spin-2 particles is made by modifying the Noether procedure from the outset. The byproduct is a gauge-invariant mass for the vector and novel consistent interactions, here derived and tested up to quartic order. ### [87] [Two-component dark matter from a flavor-dependent $U(1)$ gauge extension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24072)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过放松真空期望值层级假设，允许标量混合（scalar mixing）自然导致最轻的$\mathbb{Z}_2$-odd粒子成为标量而非费米子。对这两种两分量暗物质（two-component dark matter）实现方案进行专门的现象学分析，重点关注耦合的热冻结（thermal freeze-out）动力学和遗迹丰度（relic abundance）。

Result: 模型允许了质量上新的两分量暗物质实现方案：除了先前研究的纯费米子方案外，现在还包括一个费米子和一个标量组分的混合方案。通过考虑观测到的遗迹密度（relic density）和当前直接探测（direct-detection）限制，识别出了可行的参数空间区域。

Conclusion: 在更一般的质量谱框架下，该$U(1)_X$规范扩展模型支持两种性质不同的两分量暗物质实现方案，为暗物质现象学提供了更丰富的可能性，并通过遗迹丰度和直接探测约束确定了可行的参数空间。

Abstract: We revisit the dark matter phenomenology of a flavor-dependent $U(1)_X$ gauge extension of the Standard Model, where anomaly cancellation predicts the existence of exactly three fermion generations and requires the presence of three right-handed neutrinos. In Ref.~\cite{VanLoi:2023utt}, a strong hierarchy between the vacuum expectation values of two singlet scalars, $\La_2 \gg \La_1$, renders all $\mathbb{Z}_2$-odd scalar states heavy, resulting in a two-component dark matter scenario composed exclusively of fermions. In the present work, we relax this simplifying assumption and consider a more general mass spectrum. In particular, scalar mixing can naturally lead to a situation in which the lightest $\mathbb{Z}_2$-odd particle is a scalar rather than a fermion. As a consequence, the model admits a qualitatively new realization of two-component dark matter consisting of one fermionic and one scalar component, in addition to the purely fermionic scenario studied previously. We perform a dedicated phenomenological analysis of these two-component dark matter realizations, focusing on the coupled thermal freeze-out dynamics and the resulting relic abundance. Constraints from the observed relic density and current direct-detection limits are taken into account, and viable regions of parameter space are identified.

### [88] [Dilaton Sum Rules of Gravitational Form Factors in QCD at Order $α_s$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24303)
*Claudio Corianò,Stefano Lionetti,Dario Melle,Leonardo Torcellini*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在QCD框架内构建了强子引力形状因子的部分子描述，重点关注能量-动量张量与两个胶子流的三点函数。通过动量空间共形场论方法，在考虑规范固定效应后，将关联函数围绕共形极限组织，揭示了自旋-0分量由共形反常主导，满足质量无关的色散求和规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立QCD中强子引力形状因子的部分子描述（partonic description），特别关注能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor）与两个胶子流的三点函数。尽管QCD缺乏精确的共形对称性（conformal symmetry），但需要发展适用于强子引力形状因子的理论框架。

Method: 采用动量空间共形场论（CFT）方法，适当调整以考虑规范固定效应（gauge-fixing effects），将关联函数围绕共形极限组织。通过张量分解为自旋-2、自旋-1和自旋-0分量，其中自旋-0分量由共形反常（conformal anomaly）主导。

Result: 相应的反常形状因子（anomaly form factor）满足质量无关的色散求和规则（mass-independent dispersive sum rule），并允许类似膨胀子（dilaton-like）的解释。在光锥极限（light-cone limit）下，该项与额外的无迹结构（traceless structure）成为主导，表明存在与强子引力形状因子相关的有效反常介导描述。

Conclusion: 研究成功构建了QCD中强子引力形状因子的部分子描述框架，揭示了共形反常在其中的关键作用。反常形状因子的性质及其在光锥极限下的主导地位，为理解强子引力形状因子提供了有效的反常介导描述途径。

Abstract: We formulate a partonic description of hadronic gravitational form factors within QCD, focusing on the three-point function of the energy-momentum tensor and two gluon currents. Despite the lack of exact conformal symmetry in QCD, the correlator may be organized around the conformal limit through momentum-space CFT methods, suitably adjusted for gauge-fixing effects. This yields a tensor decomposition into spin-2, spin-1, and spin-0 sectors, with the spin-0 contribution governed by the conformal anomaly. The corresponding anomaly form factor satisfies a mass-independent dispersive sum rule and allows a dilaton-like interpretation. In the light-cone limit, this term and an additional traceless structure become dominant, indicating an effective anomaly-mediated description relevant to hadronic gravitational form factors.

### [89] [Factorized dispersion relations for two coupled systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23664)
*Alexander Figotin*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明，由两个耦合子系统构成的物理系统的色散关系具有因子化形式 G₁G₂=γG_c，并通过三个示例验证了这一结果，其中对Mindlin-Reissner板理论进行了完整的渐近分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究由两个耦合子系统构成的物理系统的色散关系（dispersion relations）特性，旨在建立这些系统色散关系的普遍数学形式，并理解模式混合（mode hybridization）的定量特征。

Method: 应用行列式展开定理（determinant expansion theorem）分析耦合系统矩阵的块结构（block structure），通过三个具体示例验证理论结果：行波管（traveling wave tube）、飞机机翼振动和Mindlin-Reissner板理论（Mindlin-Reissner plate theory）。

Result: 证明了任何由两个耦合子系统构成的物理系统的色散关系都满足因子化形式 G₁G₂=γG_c，其中G₁和G₂是子系统色散函数，G_c是耦合函数，γ是耦合参数。对Mindlin-Reissner板理论的渐近分析表明，所有四个分支都携带两个子系统因子的印记。

Conclusion: 因子化形式为模式混合（mode hybridization）提供了精确的定量度量，耦合色散分支在交点附近的局部几何结构通常是双曲型的，且存在一个机械类比模型展示相同的因子化结构和避免交叉现象。

Abstract: We establish that the dispersion relations of any physical system composed of two coupled subsystems, governed by a space-time homogeneous Lagrangian, admit a factorized form G_{1}G_{2}=γG_{\mathrm{c}}, where G_{1} and G_{2} are the subsystem dispersion functions, G_{\mathrm{c}} is the coupling function, and γis the coupling parameter. The result follows from a determinant expansion theorem applied to the block structure of the coupled system matrix, and is illustrated through three examples: the traveling wave tube, vibrations of an airplane wing, and the Mindlin-Reissner plate theory. For the Mindlin-Reissner example we carry out a complete asymptotic analysis of the coupled dispersion branches, establishing that the factorized form provides a precise quantitative measure of mode hybridization: all four branches carry the imprint of both subsystem factors for any nonzero coupling, while asymptotically recovering the identity of pure uncoupled modes at large frequencies and wavenumbers. We further analyze the universal local geometry of the coupled dispersion branches near their intersection - the cross-point model - showing it is generically hyperbolic, and present a mechanical analog in which the wavenumber is replaced by a scalar parameter, exhibiting the same factorized structure and avoided crossin

</details>


### [90] [On symbol correspondences for quark systems II: Asymptotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23893)

Conclusion: 结论表明该方法可推广到其他紧致对称群，特别是紧致单连通半单李群（compact simply connected semisimple Lie groups）。同时指出了SU(3)情况下的特殊性需要进一步研究，为更广泛的对称群分析提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the semiclassical asymptotics of twisted algebras induced by symbol correspondences for quark systems ($SU(3)$-symmetric mechanical systems) as defined in our previous paper [3]. The linear span of harmonic functions on (co)adjoint orbits is identified with the space of polynomials on $\mathfrak{su}(3)$ restricted to these orbits, and we find two equivalent criteria for the asymptotic emergence of Poisson algebras from sequences of twisted algebras of harmonic functions on (co)adjoint orbits which are induced from sequences of symbol correspondences (the fuzzy orbits). Then, we proceed by ``gluing'' the fuzzy orbits along the unit sphere $\mathcal S^7\subset \mathfrak{su}(3)$, defining Magoo spheres, and studying their asymptotic limits. We end by highlighting the possible generalizations from $SU(3)$ to other compact symmetry groups, specially compact simply connected semisimple Lie groups, commenting on some peculiarities from our treatment for $SU(3)$ deserving further investigations.

### [91] [Determinant Formulas for Scattering Matrices of Schrödinger Operators with Finitely Many Concentric $δ$-Shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24028)
*Masahiro Kaminaga*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究三维空间中具有有限个同心δ壳相互作用的薛定谔算子的定态散射问题。通过部分波约化，将每个角动量通道的散射系数表示为有限维边界矩阵的行列式之比。特别针对两壳层s波情形，推导了显式散射公式并分析了阈值效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有有限个同心δ壳相互作用的薛定谔算子的散射理论。这类模型在量子力学中描述点状相互作用，其散射问题的解析处理具有理论价值，特别是多壳层相互作用产生的阈值效应需要系统分析。

Method: 采用自伴实现（self-adjoint realization）和边界预解公式（boundary resolvent formula）作为理论基础。通过部分波约化（partial-wave reduction），将散射问题转化为有限维矩阵问题。特别针对两壳层s波情形，推导了显式散射系数公式。

Result: 对于每个角动量ℓ，通道散射系数满足S_ℓ(k)=det K_ℓ(k^2-i0)/det K_ℓ(k^2+i0)，其中K_ℓ(z)=I_N+m_ℓ(z)Θ是约化边界矩阵。在两壳层s波情形下，获得了S_0(k)的显式公式，并识别出阈值临界配置（threshold-critical configuration），其中通常的有限散射长度（scattering length）失效。

Conclusion: 同心δ壳相互作用模型的散射问题可通过有限维边界矩阵完全描述。在阈值临界配置下，散射行为出现异常：S_0(k)→-1（当k↓0），而非通常的有限散射长度。这揭示了多壳层相互作用产生的非平凡阈值效应。

Abstract: We study stationary scattering for Schrödinger operators in $\R^3$ with finitely many concentric $δ$--shell interactions of constant real strengths. Starting from the self--adjoint realization and the boundary resolvent formula for this model, we show that, after partial--wave reduction, the same finite-dimensional boundary matrices that arise in the resolvent formula also determine the channel scattering coefficients. More precisely, for each angular momentum $\ell$, the channel coefficient $S_\ell(k)$ satisfies $S_\ell(k)=\det K_\ell(k^2-i0)/\det K_\ell(k^2+i0)$ for almost every $k>0$, where $K_\ell(z)=I_N+m_\ell(z)Θ$ is the $\ell$--th reduced boundary matrix. Thus, in each channel, the positive--energy scattering problem is reduced to a finite-dimensional matrix problem, and the scattering phase is recovered from $\det K_\ell(k^2+i0)$.
  We then study the first nontrivial case of two concentric shells in the $s$--wave channel, where the interaction between the shells produces nontrivial threshold effects. We derive an explicit formula for $S_0(k)$ and analyze its behavior as $k\downarrow0$. In the regular threshold regime, we obtain an explicit scattering length. We further identify a threshold--critical configuration characterized by the existence of a nontrivial zero--energy radial solution, regular at the origin, whose exterior constant term vanishes. In the corresponding nondegenerate exceptional case, the usual finite scattering length breaks down, and instead $S_0(k)\to -1$ as $k\downarrow0$.

### [92] [Particle-Hole Pair Localization on the Fermi Surface and its Impact on the Correlation Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24395)
*Niels Benedikter*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过近似玻色化（approximate bosonization）方法，比较了两种描述费米子关联能（correlation energy）的不同途径，发现完全集体化的玻色自由度描述仅能达到最优值的约92%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来研究表明，近似玻色化可用于在平均场标度极限下证明相互作用费米子关联能的随机相位近似（random phase approximation）。然而，两种主要方法在强调集体自由度（费米表面上的离域粒子-空穴对）或动量空间中的局域粒子-空穴对方面存在差异，这引发了离域化影响程度的问题。

Method: 采用近似玻色化方法，将费米表面附近的粒子-空穴激发解释为玻色子。比较两种不同途径：一是强调集体自由度（费米表面斑块上离域的粒子-空穴对），二是动量空间中完全局域的粒子-空穴对。

Result: 对于规则相互作用势，两种方法得到的关联能精度相同。然而，使用少量完全集体化的玻色自由度描述仅能获得最优值的约92%作为上界。尽管如此，这种简单方法接近最优界的程度仍然值得关注。

Conclusion: 完全集体化的玻色自由度描述虽然简单，但仅能达到关联能最优值的约92%上界。这表明粒子-空穴对离域化的影响有限，但该简单方法接近最优界的表现仍具意义。

Abstract: In recent years it has been shown how approximate bosonization can be used to justify the random phase approximation for the correlation energy of interacting fermions in a mean-field scaling limit. At the core is the interpretation of particle-hole excitations close to the Fermi surface at bosons. The main two approaches however differ in emphasizing collective degrees of freedom (particle-hole pairs delocalized over patches on the Fermi surface) or particle-hole pairs exactly localized in momentum space. Both methods lead to equal precision for the correlation energy with regular interaction potentials. This poses the question how big the influence of delocalizing particle-hole pairs really is. In the present note we show that a description with few, completely collective bosonic degrees of freedom only yields an upper bound of about 92% of the optimal value. Nevertheless it is remarkable that such a simple approach comes that close to the optimal bound.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者采用综述方法，首先简要总结当前对超新星爆炸机制的理解，然后概述塑造超新星引力波信号的物理过程。该方法侧重于理论分析而非具体计算或模拟。

Abstract: The detection of gravitational waves from a core-collapse supernova in the Milky Way or its vicinity represents a unique opportunity to probe the inner workings of these explosions. In this review, I briefly summarize our current understanding of the supernova explosion mechanism and then outline the physical processes that shape the supernova gravitational wave signal. The review highlights how the various components of the signal have the potential to constrain the progenitor rotation, the proto-neutron star structure, the nuclear equation of state, the nature of hydrodynamic instabilities, and the violence of turbulent motions in the supernova core. I also highlight some open questions and uncertainties in the theory of supernova gravitational wave astronomy as well as challenges for further progress. Specifically, there is a need to develop large model databases, systematic uncertainty quantification and methods for evidence assessment to prepare for multi-messenger observations from a Galactic supernova.

Two classes of vacua, namely zero vacuum and constant non-zero vacuum can be realized within a centerless Heisenberg algebra. The tau functions for soliton solutions are obtained by a dressing method and vertex operators are constructed for both types of vacua. We are able to select and classify the soliton solutions in terms of the type of vertices involved. A judicious choice of vertices yields in a closed form a particular set of multi soliton solutions for the Burgers hierarchy. We develop and analyze a class of gauge-Bäcklund transformations that generate further multi soliton solutions from those obtained by dressing method by letting them interact with various integrable defects.

### [95] [Thermodynamics of Hairy Black Holes in Quantum Regimes: Insights from Horndeski Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23721)
*Behnam Pourhassan,Izzet Sakalli,Houcine Aounallah,Fabiano F. Santos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了n维Schwarzschild-Tangherlini-AdS黑洞热力学和量子功分布的非微扰量子引力修正。修正熵$S = S_0 + η e^{-S_0}$导致比热、内能、自由能等热力学量的显著改变，并在小视界半径下诱导Hawking-Page相变。量子功分布分析显示自由能差在小视界半径下发生符号反转，表明非微扰效应从根本上改变了AdS黑洞的相结构和蒸发能量学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索非微扰量子引力效应对AdS黑洞热力学和量子功分布的修正。传统微扰修正无法完全描述量子引力效应，需要考察非微扰修正如何改变黑洞的相结构和蒸发过程的热力学行为。

Method: 研究方法基于修正熵公式$S = S_0 + η e^{-S_0}$，其中$S_0$为Bekenstein-Hawking熵。从此出发推导了修正的比热、内能、亥姆霍兹自由能和吉布斯自由能的闭式表达式。在扩展相空间中分析相结构，并利用Jarzynski等式和Jensen不等式研究蒸发过程中的量子功分布。

Result: 主要结果包括：比热在$r_h^{*}=l\sqrt{(n-3)/(n-1)}$处保持经典发散，但量子修正使小视界半径下的比热幅度抑制达78%。非微扰修正为$n≥4$的黑洞诱导了Hawking-Page相变，这是半经典极限下不存在的。修正吉布斯自由能在小$r_h$下变为负值，开辟了经典对应物不存在的热力学通道。量子功分布分析显示自由能差$ΔF$在小视界半径下发生符号反转，使平均量子功从负变为正，且符号反转随时空维度增大而增强。

Conclusion: 结论表明非微扰量子引力效应定性地改变了AdS黑洞的相结构和蒸发能量学。这些效应无法通过单纯的微扰修正来捕捉，揭示了量子引力对黑洞热力学的深刻影响，特别是在小视界半径和高维时空中的显著修正。

Abstract: We study non-perturbative quantum gravitational corrections to the thermodynamics and quantum work distribution of the $n$-dimensional Schwarzschild--Tangherlini--Anti-de Sitter black hole. Starting from the corrected entropy $S = S_0 + η\, e^{-S_0}$, where $S_0$ is the Bekenstein--Hawking entropy, we derive the modified specific heat, internal energy, Helmholtz free energy, and Gibbs free energy in closed form. The specific heat retains the classical divergence at $r_h^{*}=l\sqrt{(n-3)/(n-1)}$ for $n\geq 4$, but the quantum correction suppresses its magnitude by up to $78\%$ at small horizon radii. In the extended phase space, the uncharged black hole admits no van der Waals critical point; however, the non-perturbative correction induces a Hawking--Page transition for $n\geq 4$ that is absent in the semi-classical limit. The corrected Gibbs free energy turns negative at small $r_h$, opening a thermodynamic channel with no classical counterpart. Using the Jarzynski equality and Jensen inequality, we obtain the quantum work distribution during evaporation. The free energy difference $ΔF$ between two black hole states undergoes a sign reversal at small horizon radii for $n\geq 4$ when $η=1$, flipping the average quantum work from negative to positive. This sign reversal grows with the spacetime dimension, reaching $\langle W\rangle \approx +4.31$ for $n=10$. These findings demonstrate that non-perturbative quantum gravitational effects qualitatively alter the phase structure and evaporation energetics of AdS black holes, and they cannot be captured by perturbative corrections alone.

### [96] [M-theory and T-geometry: Higgs branch moduli and charged matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23731)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过非紧致8维几何构造，其中$\mathbb{R}^{4}/Γ_{ADE}$纤维化在Biberbach 4-流形上。采用幂零上三角希格斯化方法，利用Bieberbach空间的旋转完整群实现置换群作用。

Result: 成功构造了新的3d $\mathcal{N}=2^{\ast}$和$\mathcal{N}=4^{\ast}$规范理论。希格斯分支模量由幂零元素相关的Slodowy切片特定元素编码，同一切片的其他元素产生未破缺规范代数下的非手征带电物质。

Abstract: M-theory geometric engineering on manifolds of special holonomy yields a rich class of novel field theories. In this paper, we construct new 3d $\mathcal{N}=2^{\ast}$ and $\mathcal{N}=4^{\ast}$ gauge theories, realized as mass-deformations of theories with 16 supercharges, within this framework. These arise from non-compact 8d geometries given by fibrations of $\mathbb{R}^{4}/Γ_{ADE}$ over Biberbach 4-manifolds. The existence of consistent $Spin(7)$-structures on the 8d spaces requires the rotational holonomy of the Biberbach spaces to act on the $Sp(1)$-structure of the fibers. Furthermore, we analyze Higgsing the 7d $\mathcal{N}=1$ $ADE$ gauge theories induced by the action of a permutation group on the centres of the corresponding $\mathbb{R}^{4}/Γ_{ADE}$ spaces. We show that this operation admits a natural interpretation in terms of nilpotent, upper-triangular, Higgsing, although it breaks supersymmetry. Supersymmetry is restored by fibering the singular geometry over a compact internal space, whose structure group is chosen to coincide with the permutation group to implement the nilpotent Higgsing. We refer to such backgrounds as T-geometries, where ``T'' denotes the triangular nature of the nilpotent Higgsing. Within this framework, we investigate the nilpotent Higgsing of the 3d $\mathcal{N}=2^{\ast}$ and 4d $\mathcal{N}=1^{\ast}$ theories, where the rotational holonomy groups of the Bieberbach spaces realize the permutation groups. We demonstrate that the Higgs branch moduli are encoded by specific elements of the Slodowy slices associated with nilpotent elements. Moreover, we demonstrate that additional elements of the same slice give rise to non-chiral charged matter under the unbroken gauge algebra. We establish that both the Higgs branch moduli and the charged matter are massless and admit a natural interpretation as localized matter.
