### [97] [On the ultraviolet behavior of the invariant charge in quantum electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24092)
*N. V. Krasnikov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究量子电动力学（QED）中不变电荷（invariant charge）的紫外行为，证明对于复动量，不变电荷不存在朗道极点（Landau pole）奇异性，并可通过取实部定义新的有限不变电荷。同时利用1/N微扰论（1/N perturbation theory）分析紫外行为，发现虚电荷QED与实电荷QED的1/N展开一致，为其他非渐近自由模型提供启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究量子电动力学（QED）中不变电荷的紫外行为，特别是朗道极点奇异性问题。传统QED在紫外区域存在朗道极点，这引发了对理论自洽性的关注，需要探索避免该奇异性的可能途径。

Method: 采用两种主要方法：首先分析复动量下不变电荷的行为，通过取标准不变电荷的实部定义新的不变电荷；其次运用1/N微扰论，研究虚电荷QED（具有渐近自由但非物理的模型）的紫外行为，并比较其与实电荷QED的结果。

Result: 对于复动量，不变电荷不存在朗道极点奇异性，新定义的不变电荷（实部）有上界且无朗道极点。在1/N展开中，虚电荷QED的k阶修正紫外渐近行为为α_k ∼ (ln(p²/μ²))^{-k-1}（k>1）和特殊形式（k=1），且该行为与实电荷QED一致。修改的1/N展开具有紫外有限性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过考虑复动量或采用1/N微扰论，可以避免QED中的朗道极点问题。虚电荷QED与实电荷QED的1/N展开一致性暗示，其他非渐近自由模型（如超对称QED、标量QED或Wess-Zumino模型）的不变电荷紫外渐近行为可能与领头对数近似（leading log approximation）一致。

Abstract: In this paper we study the ultraviolet behavior of the invariant charge in QED. We show that for complex momenta the invariant charge does not have Landau pole singularity. We can define new invariant charge as real part of standard invariant charge. New invariant charge is limited from above and does not have Landau pole singularity. Also we use the $1/N$ perturbation theory for the investigation of the ultraviolet behavior of the invariant charge. To this aim we consider QED with imaginary charge which is asymptotically free but nonphysical model. In QED with nonphysical imaginary charge we can reliably calculate the ultraviolet asymptotics for the $(1/N)^k$ correction to the invariant charge, namely: $α_k(\frac{p^2}{μ^2}, α) \sim (\ln(\frac{p^2}{μ^2}))^{-k-1}$ at $k > 1$ and $α_1(\frac{p^2}{μ^2}, α) \sim (\frac{\ln(\ln(\frac{p^2}{μ^2})}{\ln^2(\frac{p^2}{μ^2})})$ at $k =1$. The $1/N$ perturbation theory coincides for QED with imaginary charge and standard QED with real charge. It means in particular that ultraviolet behavior of the $(1/N)^k$ correction $α_k(\frac{p^2}{μ^2}, α)$ in real QED coincides with the corresponding asymptotics for QED with imaginary charge. We propose also to use the modified $1/N$ expansion which is ultraviolet finite. The comparison of the standard QED and nonphysical QED with imaginary charge gives hint that in other non asymptotically free models like supersymmetric QED, scalar QED or Wess-Zumino model ultraviolet asymptotics of the invariant charge coincides with leading log approximtion.

</details>

Method: 同时考虑通用联络（universal connection）情形以及与特定单李代数（simple Lie algebra）如$\mathfrak{su}(2)$相关的联络情形，分析这类平坦联络（flat connections）在点构型空间中的单值性。

Abstract: We study Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov (KZ) connection in the presence of irregular singularities, that is, poles of higher order. ### [100] [Entanglement Entropy of Massive Scalar Fields: Mass Suppression, Violation of Universal mR Scaling, and Implications for Black Hole Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24158)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Das和Shankaranarayanan引入的球壳晶格模型（spherical shell lattice model），对质量标量场进行系统数值分析，研究熵对场质量和纠缠区域大小的依赖性。

Result: 基态纠缠熵受场质量指数抑制，反映有限关联长度存在，但几何面积律标度对所有质量保持稳健；激发态额外熵不展示mR变量的普适标度，数据点不坍缩到单一曲线，显示简单标度破坏，源于波包激发的有限宽度引入额外长度尺度。

Abstract: We investigate the entanglement entropy of a massive scalar field using the spherical shell lattice model introduced by Das and Shankaranarayanan. A systematic numerical analysis is performed to study the dependence of the entropy on the field mass and on the size of the entangling region for both ground and excited states.
  For the ground state, we find that the entanglement entropy is exponentially suppressed by the field mass, reflecting the presence of a finite correlation length, while the geometric area-law scaling remains robust for all masses.
  For localized excited states, however, we uncover a qualitatively different behavior. The excess entropy does not exhibit universal scaling in the dimensionless variable mR. Instead, numerical results show that data points with identical mR but different (m,R) pairs do not collapse onto a single curve, demonstrating a clear violation of simple scaling. This breakdown is traced to the presence of an additional length scale associated with the finite width of the wave-packet excitation.
  This result identifies the coexistence of multiple infrared scales as a key feature of excited-state entanglement in massive quantum field theories.
  Mutual information provides an additional finite diagnostic of correlations in the chosen nested geometry. The numerical results show a strong dependence on the field mass, although the detailed behavior is sensitive to the geometric setup used in the calculation.
  These findings clarify how particle mass and excitation structure jointly determine entanglement properties, and suggest that the matter contribution to the generalized entropy in semiclassical gravity may depend on independent infrared parameters rather than on a single correlation scale. Implications for black hole entropy and the island formula are briefly discussed.

We aim to adapt and generalize this approach to the Ramond sector.Our result is a closed-form analytic expression for four-point correlation numbers involving Ramond fields.

### [103] [soliton_solver: A GPU-based finite-difference PDE solver for topological solitons in two-dimensional non-linear field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24370)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 软件采用理论无关的数值核心架构，使用Numba CUDA核实现GPU加速计算。物理模型通过模块化理论组件引入，实现计算框架与具体理论的分离。数值后端提供有限差分离散化（finite-difference discretization）、能量最小化和GPU驻留可观测量评估。CUDA-PyOpenGL渲染管道支持直接可视化演化场构型。

Conclusion: soliton_solver提供了一个灵活且可扩展的平台，用于模拟和可视化二维非线性场论中的拓扑孤子。其模块化设计允许以最小修改将新理论集成到共享数值基础设施中，为跨尺度物理研究提供了统一的计算工具。

Abstract: This paper introduces soliton_solver, an open-source GPU-accelerated software package for the simulation and real-time visualization of topological solitons in two-dimensional non-linear field theories. The software is structured around a theory-agnostic numerical core implemented using Numba CUDA kernels, while individual physical models are introduced through modular theory components. This separation enables a single computational framework to be applied across a broad class of systems, from nanoscale magnetic spin textures in condensed matter physics to cosmic strings spanning galaxies in high energy physics. The numerical backend provides finite-difference discretization, energy minimization, and GPU-resident evaluation of observables. A CUDA--PyOpenGL rendering pipeline allows direct visualization of evolving field configurations without staging full arrays through host memory. The package is distributed in Python via PyPI and supports both reproducible batch simulations and interactive exploration of metastable configurations, soliton interactions, and model-dependent initial states. We describe the software architecture, numerical workflow, and extensibility model, and we present representative example applications. We also outline how additional theories can be incorporated with minimal modification of the shared numerical infrastructure.

We very briefly comment on the nilpotency property of the consistently modified versions of the conserved (anti-)BRST charges, too. Our present observations are very sacrosanct because they have been proven by (i) using the beauty of the symmetry properties, and (ii) exploiting the theoretical strength of the basic canonical (anti)commutators.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在将Leung-Stelle和Lin-Skrzypek-Stelle关于半超对称膜的一致截断工作，系统性地纳入Cassani等人发展的例外广义几何分析框架中。这有助于建立不同截断方案之间的统一理论联系。

Method: 每个解在Strickland-Constable引入的$Spin(n,n)\times \mathbb{R}^+$广义几何中定义一个无挠（torsion-free）$Spin(n)$结构，其中$n$是膜横向空间的维度。通过将此结构嵌入适当的例外广义几何，从而定义相应的截断方案。

Result: 作为副产品，论文推导出：1) IIA NS5膜到六维$\mathcal{N}=(2,0)$超引力（supergravity）耦合张量多重态（tensor multiplet）的新一致截断；2) D6膜到七维纯半最大超引力（pure half-maximal supergravity）的新截断；3) D7膜到八维纯半最大超引力的新截断。

Conclusion: 论文成功地将先前关于半超对称膜的一致截断工作整合到例外广义几何的统一框架中，并在此过程中发现了几个新的截断方案，扩展了对弦论中膜几何与超引力降维之间关系的理解。

Abstract: In this note we show how the consistent truncations on half-supersymmetric branes of Leung and Stelle and Lin, Skrzypek and Stelle fit into the general exceptional generalised geometry analysis of Cassani \emph{et al.}. Each solution defines a torsion-free $Spin(n)$ structure in the $Spin(n,n)\times \mathbb{R}^+$ generalised geometry introduced by Strickland--Constable, where $n$ is the dimension of the space transverse to the brane. Embedding this into the appropriate exceptional generalised geometry then defines the truncation. As a by-product we derive a new consistent truncation on the IIA NS5-brane to six-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=(2,0)$ supergravity coupled to a tensor mutliplet, and new consistent truncations on the D6- and D7-branes to seven- and eight-dimensional pure half-maximal supergravity respectively.

</details>

Conclusion: 论文讨论了通过黑洞（black holes）和引力波（gravitational waves）检验该量子引力提案的可行与不可行途径，为该理论的实验验证提供了方向性指导。

Abstract: Quantum field theory (QFT) on fractal spacetimes is a program aiming at quantizing the gravitational interaction consistently at all energy scales thanks to an intrinsically or dynamically induced multiscale or multifractal-like spacetime geometry that regularizes the infinities of standard QFT. Viable and unviable ways to test this proposal through black holes and gravitational waves are discussed.

### [108] [The conformal dimension of the Brownian sphere is two](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24473)
*Jason Miller,Yi Tian*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文证明了布朗球面（Brownian sphere）的共形维数（conformal dimension）等于其拓扑维数2，而非其豪斯多夫维数4。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共形维数是度量空间的重要拟对称不变量（quasisymmetric invariant），位于拓扑维数和豪斯多夫维数之间。布朗球面作为球面度量测度空间的均匀测度表示，其豪斯多夫维数为4，但共形维数的具体值尚不明确。

Method: 通过分析布朗球面（又称布朗映射，Brownian map）的共形维数性质，该研究探讨了度量空间在拟对称变换下的豪斯多夫维数下确界。

Result: 主要结果表明，布朗球面的共形维数等于其拓扑维数2，这远小于其豪斯多夫维数4，且处于理论范围[2,4]的下界。

Conclusion: 布朗球面的共形维数达到其理论最小值，即等于拓扑维数2，这一发现揭示了该随机几何对象在拟对称变换下的维度特性。

Abstract: The conformal dimension of a metric space $(X, d)$ is equal to the infimum of the Hausdorff dimensions among all metric spaces quasisymmetric to $(X, d)$. It is an important quasisymmetric invariant which lies non-strictly between the topological and Hausdorff dimensions of $(X, d)$. We consider the conformal dimension of the Brownian sphere (a.k.a. the Brownian map), whose law can be thought of as the uniform measure on metric measure spaces homeomorphic to the standard sphere $\mathbf S^2$ with unit area. Since the Hausdorff dimension of the Brownian sphere is $4$, its conformal dimension lies in $[2, 4]$. Our main result is that its conformal dimension is equal to $2$, its topological dimension.

</details>

Result: 主要结果为成功构造了G值晶格杨-米尔斯-希格斯理论在完全对称性破缺区域的大质量高斯标度极限，该极限在理论阿贝尔化后呈现高斯行为。

Conclusion: 结论表明该工作补充了Chatterjee针对SU(2)群的特殊结果，为任意紧致连通矩阵李群的杨-米尔斯-希格斯理论在完全对称性破缺区域的高斯标度极限提供了普遍构造。

Abstract: Given any compact connected matrix Lie group $G$ and any lattice dimension $d\ge 2$, we construct a massive Gaussian scaling limit for the $G$-valued lattice Yang-Mills-Higgs theory in the "complete breakdown of symmetry" regime. This limit arises as the lattice spacing tends to zero and the (inverse) gauge coupling constant tends to infinity sufficiently fast, causing the theory to "abelianize" and yield a Gaussian limit. This complements a recent work by Chatterjee (arXiv:2401.10507), which obtained a similar scaling limit in the special case $G= SU(2)$.

*Abdelmalek Abdesselam*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该方法依赖于du Sautoy和Grunewald关于幂零群子群增长ζ函数（subgroup growth zeta functions）的工作，以及Delange对Wiener-Ikehara Tauberian定理的推广。这些工具被用于分析随机覆盖的连通分支数分布。

Result: 证明了当基本群为幂零群时，随机覆盖的连通分支数服从中心极限定理。这为作者与Shannon Starr先前在环面（基本群为秩至少为2的自由阿贝尔群）上的结果提供了非阿贝尔推广。

Conclusion: 该研究成功地将随机覆盖连通分支数的中心极限定理从阿贝尔情形推广到幂零群情形，建立了更一般的理论框架，并展示了子群增长ζ函数和Tauberian定理在随机覆盖理论中的应用价值。

Abstract: There is a well understood way of generating random coverings of a fixed manifold by sampling homomorphisms from the fundamental group of this manifold into the symmetric group. We prove a central limit theorem for the number of connected components of these random coverings when the fundamental group is nilpotent. This provides a nonabelian generalization of an earlier result by the author and Shannon Starr in the case of the torus where the fundamental group is a free abelian group of rank at least two. Our result relies on the work of du Sautoy and Grunewald on the subgroup growth zeta functions of nilpotent groups, and on Delange's generalization of the Wiener-Ikehara Tauberian theorem.

### [111] [Aluminum solidification and nanopolycrystal deformation via a Graph Neural Network Potential and Million-Atom Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24360)
*Ian Störmer,Julija Zavadlav*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 该MLP模型具有近从头算（ab initio）精度和良好的计算扩展性，能够进行纳秒级、百万原子规模的模拟，克服了多晶凝固模拟中的有限尺寸效应。与经典势函数和现有MLP模型相比，该模型在堆垛层错能（stacking-fault energetics）和扩散行为方面的准确性避免了凝固晶粒结构和后凝固力学行为的定性错误。

Abstract: Solidification governs the microstructure and, therefore, the mechanical response of metal components, yet the atomistic details of nucleation and defect formation are often difficult to determine experimentally. Molecular dynamics can bridge this gap, but only if the interatomic model is both accurate and computationally efficient. Here, we develop a Machine Learning Potential (MLP) for aluminum and demonstrate its near ab initio fidelity when trained with the sequential-refinement workflow that fine-tunes the model on low-energy structures. The favorable scaling of the model enables nanosecond simulations involving millions of atoms, thereby overcoming finite-size effects in simulations of polycrystalline solidification and subsequent mechanical testing. Comparison with classical potentials and recent MLP models, including a general-purpose model, shows that inaccuracies in stacking-fault energetics and diffusion can lead to qualitatively incorrect solidified grain structures and post-solidification mechanical behavior. Since our framework is based on an equivariant graph neural network, it allows for straightforward extensions to multi-component systems, providing valuable guidance for the future design and fine-tuning of both specialized and universal MLPs in computational mechanics simulations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study Schrödinger operators on the real line whose potentials are generated by the Fibonacci substitution sequence and a rule that replaces symbols by compactly supported potential pieces. We consider the case in which one of those pieces is identically zero, and study the dimension of the spectrum in the large-coupling regime. Our results include a generalization of theorems regarding explicit examples that were studied previously and a counterexample that shows that the naïve generalization of previously established statements is false. In particular, in the aperiodic case, the local Hausdorff dimension of the spectrum does not necessarily converge to zero uniformly on compact subsets as the coupling constant is sent to infinity.

### [113] [Beyond the Central Limit: Universality of the Gamma Distribution from Padé-Enhanced Large Deviations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23567)
*Mario Castro,José A. Cuesta*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 该论文提出伽马分布（gamma distribution）的普遍性源于大偏差理论（large deviation theory）中的帕德逼近（Padé approximants），这为跨学科观测到的伽马统计提供了机制无关的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管中心极限定理（central limit theorem）为高斯分布（Gaussian distribution）的普遍性提供了理论基础，但许多物理系统（如地震、微生物生长、流行病传播）却一致表现出伽马分布而非高斯统计。现有领域特定的机制解释对模型细节的微小变化缺乏稳健性。

Method: 采用大偏差理论框架，使用帕德逼近代替缩放累积量生成函数（scaled cumulant generating function）导数的多项式展开，从而尊重中心极限定理所违反的正性约束（positivity constraints）。

Result: 伽马分布自然地从大偏差理论中涌现，伽马普遍性（gamma universality）作为高斯普遍性的约束类比出现，为不同学科中伽马分布的普遍存在提供了机制无关的解释。

Conclusion: 伽马普遍性源于数学约束而非特定物理机制，这解释了为什么伽马分布在不同学科中普遍出现，为理解正随机变量系统的统计行为提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: The central limit theorem provides the theoretical foundation for the universality of the normal distribution: under broad conditions, the asymptotic distribution of a sum of independent random variables approaches a Gaussian. Yet, physical systems described by positive random variable -- from earthquakes to microbial growth to epidemic spreading -- consistently exhibit gamma rather than Gaussian statistics -- what leads to field-specific mechanistic explanations that are non robust to small changes in the model details. We show that gamma distributions emerge naturally from large deviation theory when Padé approximants replace polynomial expansions of the derivative of the scaled cumulant generating function, respecting positivity constraints that the central limit theorem violates. Gamma universality thus emerges as the constrained analog of Gaussian universality, providing a mechanism-free explanation for its pervasive appearance across different disciplines.

</details>

### [114] [Fading ergodicity and quantum dynamics in random matrix ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23616)
*Rafał Świętek,Maksymilian Kliczkowski,Miroslav Hopjan,Lev Vidmar*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过校准Rosenzweig-Porter模型和超度量（ultrametric）模型的Thouless时间，证明它们在多体希尔伯特空间中属于相同的遍历性破缺普适类，并将Rosenzweig-Porter模型的分形相（fractal phase）与渐逝遍历性（fading-ergodicity）机制联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究提出渐逝遍历性作为多体遍历性破缺的机制，但需要验证不同随机矩阵模型是否属于同一普适类。研究旨在探索Rosenzweig-Porter模型和超度量模型在多体自旋-1/2希尔伯特空间中的对应关系。

Method: 通过校准两个模型的Thouless时间参数，分析局域可观测量矩阵元素的统计特性。进一步通过量子淬火动力学、时间涨落、功率谱和存活概率等分析来验证对应关系。

Result: 研究发现两个模型属于相同的遍历性破缺普适类，Rosenzweig-Porter模型的分形相对应于渐逝遍历性机制。局域可观测量在渐逝遍历性区域内、在短于海森堡时间（Heisenberg time）的尺度上达到热化。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解不同模型中的遍历性破缺提供了统一框架，揭示了渐逝遍历性机制在多体系统中的普适性特征，建立了随机矩阵模型与多体遍历性破缺现象之间的直接联系。

Abstract: Recent work has proposed fading ergodicity as a mechanism for many-body ergodicity breaking. Here, we show that two paradigmatic random matrix ensembles -- the Rosenzweig-Porter model and the ultrametric model -- fall within the same universality class of ergodicity breaking when embedded in a many-body Hilbert space of spins-1/2. By calibrating the parameters of both models via their Thouless times, we demonstrate that the matrix elements of local observables display similar statistical properties, allowing us to identify the fractal phase of the Rosenzweig-Porter model with the fading-ergodicity regime. This correspondence is further supported through the analyses of quantum-quench dynamics of local observables, their temporal fluctuations and power spectra, and survival probabilities. Our findings reveal that local observables thermalize within the fading-ergodicity regime on timescales shorter than the Heisenberg time, thus providing a unified framework for understanding ergodicity breaking across these distinct models.

### [115] [Universal scaling laws for dynamical-thermal hysteresis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24007)
*Yachao Sun,Xuesong Li,Yanting Wang,Jing Zhou,Haiyang Bai,Yuliang Jin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了动态磁滞（dynamic hysteresis）中磁滞回线面积与磁场扫描速率之间的普适标度律，发现存在两个标度区域：低速区的1/3幂律和高速区的2/3幂律，由热涨落与磁场扫描的竞争决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态磁滞作为材料对外场速率依赖的滞后响应现象，在高效变压器和气体存储系统等应用中至关重要。然而，磁滞回线面积A如何随磁场扫描速率R标度这一基本问题尚未解决，且已报道的标度指数存在非普适性。

Method: 通过磁材料实验、伊辛模型（Ising model）和金属有机框架（metal-organic framework）模拟，以及随机朗之万方程（stochastic Langevin equation）的解析解，系统验证了标度律的普适性。

Result: 研究发现存在两个普适标度区域：当R < R*时，A - A₀ ∝ R¹/³；当R > R*时，A - A₀ ∝ R²/³，其中A₀为准静态面积，交叉速率R* ∝ T/Tc取决于温度T和材料临界温度Tc。

Conclusion: 该框架不仅解决了长期存在的标度指数非普适性问题，还为动态磁滞的应用提供了直接的设计原则，揭示了热涨落与磁场扫描竞争控制的普适交叉行为。

Abstract: Dynamic hysteresis, the rate-dependent lagged response of materials to external fields, underpins applications from energy-efficient transformers to gas storage systems. A fundamental yet unresolved question is how the hysteresis loop area $A$ scales with the field sweep rate $R$. Here, we reveal that a competition between the field sweep and thermal fluctuations governs a universal crossover between two scaling regimes: $A - A_0 \propto R^{1/3}$ for $R < R^*$ and $A - A_0 \propto R^{2/3}$ for $R > R^*$, where $A_0$ is the quasi-static area and the crossover rate $R^* \propto T/T_c$ depends on the temperature $T$ and the material's critical temperature $T_c$. We demonstrate these scaling laws universally across experiments of magnetic materials, simulations of Ising and metal-organic framework models, and analytical solutions of a stochastic Langevin equation. This framework not only resolves the long-standing non-universality of reported scaling exponents but also provides a direct design principle for the application of dynamic hysteresis.

</details>


### [116] [Mpemba effect in a two-dimensional bistable potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24148)
*Hisao Hayakawa,Satoshi Takada*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个二维径向对称双稳势中过阻尼朗之万系统的精确可解姆彭巴效应模型，通过分段二次-对数势函数实现了福克-普朗克算符到薛定谔型本征值问题的精确映射，获得了反常弛豫的解析解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在构建一个无需约束壁的二维精确可解模型，以探究姆彭巴效应（Mpemba effect）在非平衡弛豫现象中的机制。先前的一维模型通常需要硬壁约束，而本工作通过径向几何扩展了反常弛豫的理论框架。

Method: 采用分段二次-对数势函数构建二维径向对称双稳势，该函数在匹配半径处连续可微，从而实现了福克-普朗克算符（Fokker-Planck operator）到薛定谔型本征值问题的精确映射。弛豫谱和本征模通过合流超几何函数在各区域获得解析解。

Result: 推导了控制长时间弛豫的模式振幅显式表达式，发现最慢模式的系数对初始逆温度β_ini呈现非单调依赖性。当势的全局最小值远离原点且第二最小值靠近原点时，建立了基于两个最慢模式的Kullback-Leibler散度充分交叉条件，并证明了姆彭巴效应可在相应参数下实现。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个罕见的二维解析可解模型，展示了无约束壁情况下的反常弛豫现象，扩展了先前带硬壁的一维构造，并阐明了径向几何在非平衡弛豫现象中的作用。

Abstract: We present an exactly solvable model of the Mpemba effect in an overdamped Langevin system confined in a two-dimensional radially symmetric bistable potential. The potential is constructed as a piecewise quadratic-logarithmic function that is continuous and differentiable at the matching radii, enabling an exact mapping of the corresponding Fokker-Planck operator to a Schroedinger-type eigenvalue problem. The relaxation spectrum and eigenmodes are obtained analytically in each region in terms of confluent hypergeometric functions, with eigenvalues determined from matching conditions.
  Focusing on isotropic equilibrium initial states at inverse temperature $β_{\rm ini}$ quenched to a bath at inverse temperature $β$, we derive explicit expressions for the mode amplitudes governing long-time relaxation. We demonstrate that the coefficient of the slowest mode exhibits non-monotonic dependence on $β_{\rm ini}$ and identify a sufficient crossing condition for the Kullback-Leibler divergence in terms of the two slowest modes, if the global minimum of the potential is located far away from the origin and the second minimum exists near the origin. For corresponding parameters, we demonstrate that the Mpemba effect can be realized.
  Our results provide a rare example of an analytically tractable two-dimensional model exhibiting anomalous relaxation without any confining walls, extending previous one-dimensional constructions with a hard wall and clarifying the role of radial geometry in nonequilibrium relaxation phenomena.

</details>


### [117] [Universality of order statistics for Brownian reshuffling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24151)
*Zdzislaw Burda,Mario Kieburg,Tomasz Maciocha*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究一维布朗运动粒子在渐近势场 $V(x) \sim x^γ$ 中的顺序统计量（order statistics），发现领导者（leaders）重排的概率分布具有普适性，与 $γ$ 无关，而重排时间尺度则依赖于 $γ$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在渐近势场 $V(x) \sim x^γ$（$γ>0$）中，大量独立相同粒子进行一维布朗运动时，粒子位置的顺序统计量特性，特别是领导者（最靠前的粒子）如何随时间重排。

Method: 分析 $N$ 个独立相同粒子在渐近势场中的布朗运动，推导出在稳态下，第 $k$ 大粒子在时间 $t_1$ 到 $t_2$ 期间变为第 $j$ 大粒子的概率生成函数（generating function）。

Result: 领导者重排的概率分布具有普适性，与势场指数 $γ$ 无关；重排时间尺度 $t \sim (\ln N)^\frac{2(1-γ)}γ τ$ 依赖于 $γ$；领导者列表的平均百分比重叠系数（average percentage overlap coefficient）取普适形式 ${\rm erfc}(\sqrtτ)$。

Conclusion: 在渐近势场中的布朗运动粒子系统中，领导者重排的统计特性具有普适性，独立于势场指数 $γ$，而重排的时间尺度则依赖于 $γ$，这为理解此类系统的动力学行为提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We discuss the order statistics of the particle positions of a gas of $N$ identical independent particles performing Brownian motion in one dimension in a potential that asymptotically behaves like $V(x) \sim x^γ$ for $x\rightarrow+\infty$, with a positive power $γ>0$. We show that in the stationary state, the order statistics that describe how the leaders are reshuffled are universal and independent of $γ$. What depends on $γ$ is the timescale of the leaders' reshuffling, which scales as a power of the logarithm of the population size: $t \sim (\ln N)^\frac{2(1-γ)}γ τ$, where $τ$ is of order one. We derive the probability that the particle which has the $k$th largest value of $x$ at some time $t_1$ will have the $j$th largest value at time $t_2=t_1+t$ in the form of an explicit expression for the generating function for the reshuffling probabilities for all $k\ge 1$ and $j\ge 1$. The generating function, expressed in scaled time $τ$, is independent of $γ$. In particular, we show that the average percentage overlap coefficient of leader lists takes the universal, $γ$-independent form ${\rm erfc}(\sqrtτ)$ for long lists.

</details>


### [118] [Digitally Optimized Initializations for Fast Thermodynamic Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24183)
*Mattia Moroder,Felix C. Binder,John Goold*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种混合数字-热力学算法，通过受姆潘巴效应启发的优化初始化策略，显著加速热力学计算中的弛豫过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热力学计算利用物理系统的弛豫动力学执行矩阵运算，但此类方法的关键限制在于系统达到足够精度平衡所需的热化时间往往较长。

Method: 提出混合数字-热力学方案：经典数字处理器高效计算能抑制慢弛豫模式的初始化状态，随后物理系统通过其固有弛豫动力学执行剩余计算。聚焦于二次能量景观的过阻尼朗之万动力学，分析相关福克-普朗克算符的谱结构并识别相应的最优初始协方差。

Result: 该方法实现了热化时间的可预测减少，由编码矩阵的谱决定。推导了所得加速的解析表达式，并以矩阵求逆和行列式计算的热力学实现作为具体示例进行数值分析。

Conclusion: 优化初始化协议为加速热力学计算提供了一条简单且广泛适用的途径，通过数字预处理抑制慢弛豫模式，显著提升热力学计算效率。

Abstract: Thermodynamic computing harnesses the relaxation dynamics of physical systems to perform matrix operations. A key limitation of such approaches is the often long thermalization time required for the system to approach equilibrium with sufficient accuracy. Here, we introduce a hybrid digital-thermodynamic algorithm that substantially accelerates relaxation through optimized initializations inspired by the Mpemba effect. In the proposed scheme, a classical digital processor efficiently computes an initialization that suppresses slow relaxation modes, after which the physical system performs the remaining computation through its intrinsic relaxation dynamics. We focus on overdamped Langevin dynamics for quadratic energy landscapes, analyzing the spectral structure of the associated Fokker-Planck operator and identifying the corresponding optimal initial covariances. This yields a predictable reduction in thermalization time, determined by the spectrum of the encoded matrix. We derive analytic expressions for the resulting speedups and numerically analyze thermodynamic implementations of matrix inversion and determinant computation as concrete examples. Our results show that optimized initialization protocols provide a simple and broadly applicable route to accelerating thermodynamic computations.

</details>


### [119] [Dynamical thermalization and turbulence in social stratification models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24190)
*Klaus M. Frahm,Dima L. Shepelyansky*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了社会网络中线性振子的非线性混沌动力学，将振子能量（频率）分层视为社会财富状态模型，揭示了混沌热化导致的Rayleigh-Jeans分布及其低能模式凝聚现象，类比于全球财富不平等。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过线性振子耦合系统模拟社会分层现象，其中振子能量（频率）的分层被视为社会财富状态的物理类比，探索非线性相互作用下社会系统的动力学行为。

Method: 采用哈密顿演化方法研究社会网络链接耦合的线性振子系统，该系统包含振子能量（频率）分层和附加非线性相互作用，分析系统的两个运动积分：能量和概率范数。

Result: 在混沌边界以上，混沌动力学导致动态热化，形成给定能量（财富）状态上的Rayleigh-Jeans分布；低能状态下出现RJ凝聚现象，类比于全球财富不平等（约一半人口仅拥有总财富的几个百分点）。在能量泵浦和吸收存在时，系统展现出非线性波的Kolmogorov-Zakharov湍流特征。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了物理系统与社会分层现象之间的类比关系，揭示了非线性相互作用下社会财富分布的动力学机制，为理解社会不平等提供了新的物理模型视角。

Abstract: We study the nonlinear chaotic dynamics in a system of linear oscillators coupled by social network links with an additional stratification of oscillator energies, or frequencies, and supplementary nonlinear interactions. It is argued that this system can be viewed as a model of social stratification in a society with nonlinear interacting agents with energies playing a role of wealth states of society. The Hamiltonian evolution is characterized by two integrals of motion being energy and probability norm. Above a certain chaos border the chaotic dynamics leads to dynamical thermalization with the Rayleigh-Jeans (RJ) distribution over states with given energy or wealth. At low energies, this distribution has RJ condensation of norm at low energy modes. We point out a similarity of this condensation with the wealth inequality in the world countries where about a half of population owns only a couple of percent of the total wealth. In the presence of energy pumping and absorption, the system reveals features of the Kolmogorov-Zakharov turbulence of nonlinear waves.

### [120] [Run, Tumble and Paint](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24277)
*Emir Sezik,Callum Britton,Alex Touma,Gunnar Pruessner*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文计算了Run-and-Tumble粒子（run-and-tumble particle）的"状态依赖"访问概率（state-dependent visit probability），即粒子在首次通过位置x时保持其内部推进状态的概率，使用Doi-Peliti场论（Doi-Peliti field theory）框架进行分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 访问概率（visit probability）是表征活性物质（active matter）模型的基本工具，但先前研究大多忽略了该概率如何依赖于驱动活性粒子的内部自由度。本文旨在解决Run-and-Tumble粒子内部状态对访问概率的依赖性。

Method: 采用一维Doi-Peliti场论框架，通过扩展先前工作中的示踪机制（tracer mechanism）来纳入"极性沉积"（polar deposition）过程，从而计算状态依赖的访问概率。

Result: 成功在Doi-Peliti场论框架内优雅地捕捉了状态依赖的访问概率，并进一步推导了向右（或向左）移动的Run-and-Tumble粒子覆盖的总体积，与布朗运动（Brownian motion）的已知表达式进行了比较。

Conclusion: 本文建立了计算Run-and-Tumble粒子状态依赖访问概率的场论方法，为研究活性粒子内部状态对极端值统计（extreme value statistics）的影响提供了理论框架。

Abstract: The visit probability, quantifying whether a particle has reached a given point for the first time by a specified time, provides access to various extreme value statistics and serves as a fundamental tool for characterising active matter models. However, previous studies have largely neglected how the visit probability depends on the internal degree of freedom driving the active particle. To address this, we calculate the "state-dependent'' visit probability for a Run-and-Tumble particle, that is the probability that the particle first passes through $x$ before time $t$, keeping track of its internal state during first passage. This process may be thought of as the particle "painting'' the positions it passes through for the time in the colour of its self-propulsion state. We perform this calculation in one dimension using Doi-Peliti field theory, by extending the tracer mechanism from previous works to incorporate such "polar deposition'' and demonstrate that state-dependent visit probabilities can be elegantly captured within this field-theoretic framework. We further derive the total volume covered by a right- (or left-) moving Run-and-Tumble particle and compare our results with known expressions for Brownian motion.

### [121] [Algorithms for generating planar networks simulating hierarchical patterns of cracks formed during film drying](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24171)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Hierarchical crack patterns that arise during the drying of thin films of colloidal dispersions or polymer solutions on a solid substrate are of interest both from a fundamental standpoint and in the context of the creation of transparent electrodes for optoelectronics. This paper analyzes the morphology of such patterns based on image processing of real-world samples. Graph theory is used to extract chains of edges and analyze the network topology. A method based on the hierarchy of connections is applied to classify cracks by generation. The limitations of existing classification approaches related to the discreteness of the time scale and the use of only a part of the entire pattern are discussed. Three approaches are used to generate artificial hierarchical networks: random uniform partitioning, recursive Voronoi partitioning, and a crack growth simulation model, each modified to reproduce the hierarchical structure. A comparison was made of the geometric characteristics (distribution of crack angles, edge lengths, cell areas, and circularity coefficient) and topological properties (distribution of the number of cell sides) of real and simulated networks. It was shown that the simulation model best reproduces the key features of real cracks, including the characteristic right angles of their connections.

Abstract: We introduce the order-separated Grassmann higher-order tensor renormalization group (OS-GHOTRG) method for QCD with staggered quarks in the strong-coupling expansion. We use the method in two dimensions to compute the free energy, the particle-number density, and the chiral condensate as a function of the chemical potential up to third order in the inverse coupling $β$. Antibodies are represented as Y-shaped particles composed of seven tangential hard spheres with attractive patches on the terminal beads, while the matrix consists of randomly distributed hard-sphere obstacles bearing adhesive sites. The model captures antibody behavior in crowded biological environments with strong short-range antibody-matrix attractions. The theoretical approach combines Wertheim's multidensity thermodynamic perturbation theory, the Flory-Stockmayer theory of polymerization, and scaled particle theory for fluids in porous media. We analyze thermodynamic properties, percolation thresholds, and phase behavior, and compare the selected results with new computer simulations. The interplay between antibody-antibody and antibody-matrix interactions produces a complex phase behavior, including re-entrant phase separation with a closed-loop coexistence region at higher temperatures and conventional liquid-gas separation at lower temperatures.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在比较三种不同的平均场势模型（Maier-Saupe、Marrucci-Greco和Ilg-Karlin-Öttinger模型）在描述向列相液晶有序化方面的表现，这些模型在介观尺度上包含了不同的物理特征，如空间梯度和序参量的非线性依赖性。

Method: 采用向列相多粒子碰撞动力学（nematic Multi-particle Collision Dynamics, N-MPCD）模拟方法，研究受限向列相液晶在方形域中的行为。从具有张量闭合的Fokker-Planck描述中推导粗粒化方程，分析二维情况下有序化随相互作用强度U的变化。

Result: 临界相互作用强度取决于平均场势的选择。对于所有三种平均场势，都确认了普适的平衡态和亚稳态构型。当系统尺寸R和相互作用强度U较大时，N-MPCD预测与连续介质Landau-de Gennes理论预测一致，但在小R和U接近临界值时存在差异。

Conclusion: 研究建立了N-MPCD参数（系统尺寸R和相互作用强度U）与连续介质Landau-de Gennes理论参数之间的严格对应关系。对于小R和U接近临界相互作用强度的情况，N-MPCD预测与连续介质理论存在差异，这需要在新一代多尺度和多物理场理论中进一步探索和量化。

Abstract: We use nematic Multi-particle Collision Dynamics (N-MPCD) simulations to study confined nematic liquid crystals in square domains, with three distinct mean-field potentials: the classical Maier-Saupe and Marrucci-Greco models, and a more recent model due to Ilg, Karlin, and Öttinger. These potentials incorporate diverse physical features, including spatial gradients and nonlinear dependencies on the order parameter, to describe nematic ordering at mesoscopic scales. We derive coarse-grained equations from a Fokker-Planck description with tensorial closures, and analyse the emergence of order as a function of interaction strength, $U$, in two dimensions. The critical interaction strength depends on the choice of the mean-field potential. We also analytically estimate the nematic coherence length in three dimensions, to establish a rigorous correspondence between the N-MPCD parameters (the system size $R$ and $U$) and the continuum Landau-de Gennes theoretical parameters. We systematically study equilibrium and metastable configurations, including relaxation pathways to stable equilibria, on square domains, for all three mean-field potentials. Our results confirm universal equilibrium and metastable configurations for all three mean-field potentials. Our results also suggest that the N-MPCD predictions are consistent with the continuum Landau-de Gennes predictions, regardless of the choice of the underlying mean-field potential and approximations, for large $R$ and $U$. There are differences for small $R$ and for $U$ near the critical interaction strength, that need to be further explored and quantified for new-age multiscale and multiphysics theories.

### [125] [Density and shape govern the dynamical self-organization of active matter on a droplet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23735)
*Romain Leroux,Andre Estevez-Torres,Raphael Voituriez,Ananyo Maitra,Nicolas Lobato-Dauzier,Jean-Christophe Galas*

Method: 开发了一个体外模型，纯化的微管（microtubules）和驱动蛋白（kinesin）马达簇在球形水包油液滴表面自组织成二维活性向列相（active nematic）皮层。通过调节微管密度和引入几何扰动（如可控挤压）来研究系统行为。

Abstract: Morphogenesis emerges from dynamic feedback among geometry, mechanics, and chemistry; however, disentangling these contributions in living systems remains challenging. Here, we focus on the interplay between geometry and mechanics by developing a minimal in vitro model in which purified microtubules and kinesin motor clusters self-organize into a two-dimensional active nematic cortex at the surface of spherical water-in-oil droplets. The spherical geometry enforces a total topological charge of +2, here realized by four +1/2 defects whose trajectories reveal robust, self-sustained oscillations. Using full-surface reconstructions, we show that the collective dynamics of the defects lead to a periodic switching between planar and tetrahedral arrangements through alternating coiling and hemisphere-crossing phases. By tuning microtubule density, the system spans a continuum from a classic defect-dominated active nematic to a regime resembling an extensile filament confined to a curved surface, where low density is associated with increased trajectory variability and direction reversals. Geometric perturbations introduced through controlled squeezing redistribute curvature and induce the nucleation of additional defects, thereby reorganizing the entire topological landscape while preserving total charge. Together, these results show that periodic morphogenetic-like cycles, defect topology, and material organization can arise solely from the interplay of activity, density, and curvature. This reconstituted system provides a versatile platform for elucidating the coupling between mechanics and geometry underlying shape formation in active biological matter.

### [126] [A simple model for conserved intracellular dynamics exhibits multiscale pattern formation, traveling protein domains and arrested coarsening of lipids in the membrane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23856)
*Benjamin Winkler,Sergio Alonso,Markus Bär*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 脂质动力学经历经典相分离，而蛋白动力学在中等总蛋白含量下呈现振荡相分离，表现为长波长不稳定性和移动域；当两种不稳定性共存时，产生多尺度模式，较大尺度的移动和旋转蛋白域与较小尺度的静态脂质域共存。

Abstract: We model the spatiotemporal dynamics of cellular protein concentrations near membranes composed of different lipids using a three-variable continuum model for membrane-bound protein, cytosolic protein, and the local composition of a binary lipid membrane. The model contains two globally conserved quantities: the total protein content and the average fractions of the two lipid species. It combines a conserved reaction-diffusion model for protein dynamics with a Cahn-Hilliard equation for lipid demixing. Linear stability analysis of the homogeneous steady state and direct numerical simulations show that the lipid dynamics undergoes classical phase separation, whereas the protein dynamics exhibits oscillatory phase separation for intermediate total protein contents, associated with a long-wavelength instability and traveling domains. In parameter regions where both instabilities are present, we find multiscale patterns with larger-scale traveling and rotating protein domains coexisting with smaller-scale stationary lipid domains. In this regime, traveling protein domains coexist with arrested coarsening of stationary lipid domains above a critical coupling. We further show that the main instabilities and phase diagram are well captured by an extension of a recently proposed conserved FitzHugh-Nagumo model for non-reciprocal pattern formation. The extended model consists of two non-reciprocally coupled Cahn-Hilliard equations with different interface tensions, reflecting the distinct physical properties of lipids and proteins. This also explains the observed asymmetry between static lipid patterns and traveling protein patterns.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了一种基于统计力学（statistical mechanics）的模型，通过结合力分布与倾斜键势能（tilted bond potential）来计算键解离所需的活化能（activation energy）。该方法可应用于微球框架（micro-sphere framework）和八链模型（eight chain model）来构建三维本构关系。

Result: 该模型成功应用于三个实际问题：(1) 聚合物链中牺牲键断裂（sacrificial bond rupture）的增韧机制；(2) 双网络水凝胶（double network hydrogels）的增韧；(3) 将局部链模型整合到捕捉弹性体损伤的三维本构关系中。

Abstract: The mechanics of single-chain stretching and rupture are central to understanding the resilience of biological polymers and designing strong and tough soft materials such as double-network gels and multi-network elastomers. In this work, we develop a statistical mechanics based model that enables one to determine the distribution of forces along the chain segments. By combining the force distribution with a tilted bond potential that captures the stretch energy stored in these bonds, we calculate the corresponding activation energy required for bond dissociation. This allows us to determine the probability of bond (and consequently chain) failure. The proposed approach is simple, direct, and readily adaptable for constructing higher-level coarse-grained descriptions of damage and fracture in polymer networks. We demonstrated this by applying the theory to three problems of practical interest: (1) toughening via sacrificial bond rupture in polymer chains, (2) toughening of double network hydrogels, and (3) incorporation of the local chain model into a 3-dimensional constitutive relation that captures damage in elastomers. The latter was implemented through the micro-sphere framework, which accounts for different chain orientations, as well as the computationally inexpensive eight chain model. The findings from this work provide a physically-based model to quantify the stretching and failure of a single chain and pave the way to the integration of local damage models into 3-dimensional networks.

### [128] [Ambient-environment dependence of dynamic contact angles: Droplet tilting vs. captive bubble methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23907)
*Koki Iwasaki,Hiroyuki Ebata,Hiroaki Katsuragi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过构建基于俘获气泡法（captive bubble method）的实验系统，验证了在空气和水环境中测量动态接触角（dynamic contact angle）的一致性。研究发现，对于光滑表面和砂纸抛光表面，两种环境下的动态接触角基本一致；但对于微结构表面，在空气和水中的润湿行为存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量水滴在固体表面的接触角是评估表面润湿性（wettability）的常用方法，但在水环境中使用俘获气泡法（captive bubble method）测量的动态接触角是否与空气中测量结果一致，尚未得到实验验证。本研究旨在通过实验验证这一关键问题。

Method: 研究构建了基于俘获气泡法的实验系统，对三种表面类型进行了动态接触角测量：光滑聚合物表面、砂纸抛光表面以及具有微结构的疏水表面。测量分别在空气和水两种环境中进行，以比较动态接触角的一致性。

Result: 对于光滑表面，空气和水中的动态接触角几乎相同。砂纸抛光表面在空气中呈现Wenzel状态，在水中呈现反向气液Wenzel状态，但两种环境下的动态接触角仍具有可比性。然而，微结构PMMA表面在空气中显示疏水行为，在脱气条件下水中却表现出亲水行为且滞后性（hysteresis）很小。

Conclusion: 研究证实，对于光滑和砂纸抛光表面，俘获气泡法可在空气和水中获得可比较的动态接触角。但对于微结构表面，两种环境下的润湿行为存在显著差异，这为理解水环境中的润湿性提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Measuring the contact angle of a water droplet on a solid surface in air is one of the simplest and most widely used methods for evaluating surface wettability across a wide range of research fields. Wettability can also be evaluated in aqueous environments using the captive bubble method, in which an air bubble is attached to a solid surface. However, it has not yet been experimentally verified whether dynamic contact angles measured by this approach correspond to those obtained in air. In this study, we constructed an experimental system based on the captive bubble method. Dynamic contact angles were measured both in air and in water for smooth polymer surfaces, sandpaper polished surfaces, and hydrophobic surfaces with microstructures. For smooth surfaces, the dynamic contact angles obtained in air and water were nearly identical. Similar agreement was also observed for sandpaper polished surfaces, which exhibited the Wenzel state in air and the reversed gas liquid Wenzel state in water, indicating that comparable dynamic contact angles can be obtained in air and water by the captive bubble method. In contrast, microstructured PMMA surfaces that showed hydrophobic behavior in air exhibited hydrophilic behavior with very small hysteresis in water under degassed conditions. These results provide new insights into wettability in aqueous environments.

### [129] [Multi-filament coordination rescues active transport from inertia-induced spinning arrest](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24053)
*Anuradha Rajput,Arnab Bhattacharjee,Annwesha Dutta*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 当多个活性丝状体（active filaments）通过切向力驱动并连接于一个重头部时，增加丝状体数量可通过空间位阻效应抑制螺旋缠绕构象，从而恢复定向运输而非旋转停滞状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索切向力驱动的活性丝状体在连接重头部时为何会陷入旋转停滞状态，以及如何通过多丝状体结构克服这种惯性诱导的运动停滞（inertia-induced motility arrest）。

Method: 采用三维朗之万动力学（three-dimensional Langevin dynamics）模拟切向力驱动的珠-弹簧链（bead-spring chains），这些链锚定于一个共同的重头部，通过系统改变丝状体数量Nf来研究其运输恢复机制。

Result: 增加丝状体数量Nf可系统性地恢复定向运输，具体表现为：(1)均方位移恢复单调增长（运输恢复），(2)空间切向自相关失去负值信号（构象恢复），(3)切向时间自相关停止过零（取向恢复）。在高弯曲刚度下，Nf*≈3时完全消除缠绕；在中等刚度下，运输仍可恢复但存在残余缠绕。

Conclusion: 多丝状体结构通过两种物理机制恢复运输：高刚度时空间约束迫使丝状体形成协调束维持定向推进；低刚度时空间相互作用破坏取向相干性，产生增强的活性扩散。这为合成微泳体设计和生物系统中多丝状体组织提供了新见解。

Abstract: Active filaments driven by tangential forces can become trapped in a spinning state when attached to a heavy head, where activity and inertia drive persistent rotation rather than directed transport. Using three-dimensional Langevin dynamics of tangentially driven bead-spring chains anchored to a common heavy head, we demonstrate that increasing the filament number $\Nf$ systematically \emph{rescues} directed transport by sterically preventing the coiled conformations that underlie spinning. The rescue is established through three independent diagnostics: (i)~the mean-square displacement recovers monotonic growth (transport rescue), (ii)~the spatial tangent autocorrelation loses its negative dip signaling helical coiling (conformational rescue), and (iii)~the tangent time autocorrelation ceases crossing zero (orientational rescue). At high bending stiffness ($\kb = 1000$), coiling is fully eliminated at a critical filament number $\Nf^* \approx 3$. At moderate stiffness ($\kb = 100$), residual coiling persists ($\min C_s \approx -0.13$) yet transport is still rescued -- demonstrating that the destruction of spinning \emph{coherence}, not coiling elimination, is the essential mechanism. The multi-filament architecture achieves up to five orders of magnitude transport enhancement. Two physically distinct rescue pathways emerge: at high stiffness, steric constraints force filaments into a coordinated bundle sustaining directed propulsion; at low stiffness, steric interactions destroy orientational coherence, producing enhanced active diffusion. These results demonstrate a purely mechanical, density-independent route to overcome inertia-induced motility arrest, with implications for synthetic microswimmer design, motor-driven filament assays, and multi-filament organization in biological systems.

### [130] [Models of 3D confluent tissue as under-constrained glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24438)
*Chengling Li,Matthias Merkel,Daniel M. Sussman*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过三维Voronoi模型的大规模模拟，证实了亚阿伦尼乌斯（sub-Arrhenius）玻璃态动力学是跨维度欠约束材料的普遍特征，解决了二维系统因长波长波动和等静点问题带来的解释困难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前二维Voronoi模型研究显示生物组织模型可在阿伦尼乌斯（Arrhenius）与亚阿伦尼乌斯动力学间连续调控，但二维系统受长波长波动和二维熔化情景影响，且模型恰处于等静点（isostatic point），这些因素阻碍了结果向其他系统的推广。

Method: 采用三维Voronoi模型的扩展版本进行大规模模拟，通过分析结构弛豫时间（structural relaxation time τ_α）、四点磁化率（four-point susceptibility）、结构因子（structure factor）及力学性质，与二维模型结果进行对比验证。

Result: 三维Voronoi模型的结构弛豫时间可在亚阿伦尼乌斯与阿伦尼乌斯行为间调控，四点磁化率、结构因子和力学性质均显示与二维模型一致的趋势，为欠约束材料的亚阿伦尼乌斯玻璃态动力学提供了跨维度的强有力证据。

Conclusion: 亚阿伦尼乌斯玻璃态动力学是跨维度欠约束材料的普遍特征，该研究扩展了已知具有高度异常玻璃态现象学的无序材料类别。

Abstract: The dynamics of glassy materials slows down upon cooling, typically showing either Arrhenius or super-Arrhenius behavior. However, it was recently shown that 2D cell-based models for biological tissues can be continuously tuned between Arrhenius and sub-Arrhenius dynamics. In previous work, using the 2D Voronoi model, we proposed that such atypical dynamical behavior could be a generic feature of the broad class of mechanically under-constrained materials. Our earlier study had left two important points open: (1) many 2D systems are affected by long-wavelength fluctuations and the 2D melting scenario, and (2) the 2D Voronoi model sits exactly at the isostatic point, making it a marginal case rather than a strictly under-constrained one. Both points complicate the interpretation of our 2D Voronoi model results and their generalization to other systems; to remedy this, here we use large-scale simulations to study the glassy behavior of the 3D extension of the Voronoi model. We first show that the structural relaxation time $τ_α$ of the 3D Voronoi model can be tuned between sub-Arrhenius and Arrhenius behavior, like the 2D Voronoi model. We then establish that the four-point susceptibility, the structure factor, and the model's mechanical properties all display trends consistent with the 2D Voronoi model. These results provide strong evidence that sub-Arrhenius glassy dynamics are a generic feature of under-constrained materials across dimensions. Our work thus broadens the class of disordered materials known to have highly unusual glassy phenomenology.

### [131] [Radial Distribution Function in a Two Dimensional Core-Shoulder Particle System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24537)
*Michael Wassermair,Gerhard Kahl,Andrew J Archer,Roland Roth*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究比较了经典密度泛函理论中计算径向分布函数g(r)的两种方法：测试粒子法（test-particle route）和Ornstein-Zernike方程法，发现在二维核-肩粒子系统中，测试粒子法的结果并不总是优于Ornstein-Zernike方程法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在经典密度泛函理论中，径向分布函数（radial distribution function）g(r)可通过两种截然不同的方法计算。通常认为测试粒子法（仅需一次泛函导数）比Ornstein-Zernike方程法（需要二次泛函导数）更精确，但这一预期需要验证。

Method: 研究采用二维核-肩粒子系统（two dimensional core-shoulder particle system）作为模型体系，分别应用测试粒子法和Ornstein-Zernike方程法计算径向分布函数g(r)。

Result: 结果显示，在该特定系统中，测试粒子法得到的g(r)结果并不总是优于通过Ornstein-Zernike方程法获得的结果，挑战了传统预期。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，对于二维核-肩粒子系统，测试粒子法在计算径向分布函数时并不总是比Ornstein-Zernike方程法更准确，这为密度泛函理论中近似方法的适用性提供了重要见解。

Abstract: An important quantity in liquid state theory is the radial distribution function $g(r)$. It can be calculated within the framework of classical density functional theory in two very distinct ways. In the test-particle route, one fixes a single fluid particle, turning it into an external potential in which the inhomogeneous structure of the fluid is calculated by minimising the functional. The second route to $g(r)$ in density functional theory employs the Ornstein-Zernike equation and the pair direct correlation function, that can be obtained from the second functional derivatives of the excess free energy functional. Since typically an approximate excess free energy functional is employed, one generally expects that the test-particle route, which requires only one functional derivative, to be more accurate than the Ornstein-Zernike route. Here we study a two dimensional core-shoulder particle system and present results that challenge this expectation. Our results show that in this system test-particle results for $g(r)$ are not always better than results obtained via the Ornstein-Zernike route.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.supr-con'></div>

### [132] [Possible Pairing Symmetry of BaPtAs$_{1-x}$Sb$_{x}$ with an Ordered Honeycomb Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23535)
*Tsuyoshi Imazu,Naoya Furutani,Tadashi Adachi,Kazutaka Kudo,Yoshiki Imai,Jun Goryo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过μ子自旋弛豫测量发现BaPtSb在超导转变温度以下存在自发内磁场，表明时间反演对称性破缺（TRSB）。基于第一性原理计算的有效紧束缚模型分析表明，Sb浓度变化会改变配对对称性：x=1时最稳定的是具有TRSB的手性d波态，而x=0时无TRSB的节点f波或常规s波态具有竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究BaPtAs₁₋ₓSbₓ固溶体的可能配对对称性，该材料具有有序蜂窝状Pt和pnictogen网络。特别关注Sb浓度变化如何影响超导配对对称性，特别是时间反演对称性破缺（TRSB）状态的变化。

Method: 采用μ子自旋弛豫（muon-spin relaxation）测量观察BaPtSb（x=1）在超导转变温度以下的自发内磁场。基于第一性原理计算构建x=0和x=1的有效紧束缚模型（effective tight-binding model），分析费米面形状的显著差异，探讨配对对称性随Sb浓度变化的可能场景。

Result: 在BaPtSb（x=1）中观察到超导转变温度以下的自发内磁场，表明存在时间反演对称性破缺（TRSB）。计算分析发现，手性d波态（chiral d-wave state）在x=1时最稳定且具有TRSB，而在x=0时，无TRSB的节点f波（nodal f-wave）或常规s波（conventional s-wave）态具有竞争力。

Conclusion: BaPtAs₁₋ₓSbₓ固溶体的超导配对对称性随Sb浓度变化而改变：x=1时表现为具有时间反演对称性破缺的手性d波态，x=0时则倾向于无TRSB的节点f波或常规s波态。这种配对对称性的转变与费米面形状的显著差异相关。

Abstract: We investigate the possible pairing symmetry of superconducting $\rm{BaPtAs}_{1-\it{x}}\rm{Sb}_{\it{x}}$ solid solution with an ordered-honeycomb network of Pt and pnictogens. A spontaneous internal magnetic field below the superconducting transition temperature is observed in BaPtSb ($x = 1$) via the muon-spin relaxation measurement. We then pursue a scenario where the pairing symmetry is changed from a time-reversal symmetry-breaking (TRSB) state to another one by changing the Sb-concentration utilizing the effective tight-binding model obtained from the first principles calculations for $x = 0$ and $x = 1$, at which we see a significant difference in the shape of the dominant Fermi surfaces. We find that the chiral $d$-wave state with TRSB is most stable at $x = 1$, whereas the nodal $f$-wave or the conventional $s$-wave states without TRSB are competitive at $x = 0$.

</details>


### [133] [Superconducting properties of lifted-off Niobium nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24379)
*A. Kotsovolou,F. Soofivand,P. Singha,D. Cecca,R. Balice,F. Carillo,C. Puglia,G. De Simoni,F. Bianco,F. Paolucci*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了氧扩散对采用剥离技术（lift-off）制备的铌（Nb）纳米线超导转变的影响，发现纳米线表现为二维超导体，且随着线宽减小，超导转变宽度增加，为优化铌基混合量子器件提供了关键见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合超导体/半导体（hybrid superconductor/semiconductor）器件在量子科学与技术中至关重要。铌（Niobium, Nb）有望替代铝（aluminum）作为超导元件以实现高温操作，但蚀刻（etching）技术与半导体及二维材料不兼容，因此需要研究剥离技术制备的铌纳米线中超导转变的影响因素。

Method: 研究通过剥离技术（lift-off technique）制备不同宽度（W）和厚度（t）的铌器件，并测量其超导特性。采用Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）模型分析电荷输运行为，以评估纳米线的超导维度特性。

Result: 研究发现铌纳米线表现为二维超导体（two-dimensional superconductors），与宽度和厚度无关。正常态转变温度（TN）随宽度减小保持恒定，但完全超导态温度（TS）下降，导致超导转变宽度（δTC）随线宽减小而增加。这一现象归因于沉积过程中光刻胶（lithography resist）的氧扩散（oxygen diffusion）。

Conclusion: 氧扩散对铌纳米线超导转变的影响机制为优化铌基混合量子器件提供了关键知识，有助于实现2 K以上的操作温度，推动下一代量子技术的发展。

Abstract: Hybrid superconductor/semiconductor devices play a crucial role in advancing quantum science and technology by merging the properties of superconductors and semiconductors. To operate these devices at high temperature, Niobium could substitute the widespread aluminum as superconducting element. Niobium devices show the best superconducting properties when shaped by etching, but this technique is often incompatible with semiconductors and two-dimensional materials. Our work investigates the influence of oxygen diffusion on the superconducting transition of Nb nanowires fabricated by lift-off technique. To this scope, we fabricate and measure Nb devices of different width (W) and thickness (t). By using the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless (BKT) model for charge transport, we demonstrate that our nanowires behave as two-dimensional superconductors regardless of W and t. While the normal-state transition temperature (TN) remains constant with decreasing W, the temperature of the fully superconducting state (TS) decreases. Thus, the superconducting transition width (δTC) increases as W shrinks, due to oxygen diffusion from the lithography resist occurring during deposition. These insights provide essential knowledge for optimizing Nb-based hybrid quantum devices, paving the way for operating temperatures above 2 K and contributing to the development of next-generation quantum technologies.

</details>

### [134] [Dynamical magnetic breakdown and quantum oscillations from hot spot scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23605)
*Léo Mangeolle,Johannes Knolle*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究提出，即使在没有长程密度波序的情况下，量子振荡（quantum oscillations）也能产生重构的费米面（Fermi-surface）频率。通过考虑电子与涨落玻色模式耦合，发展了一种半经典理论，其中相互作用产生类似磁击穿（magnetic breakdown）的时变隧穿过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子振荡是探测费米面几何结构的成熟工具，传统上认为长程密度波序会导致费米面重构并产生新的振荡频率。本研究旨在探索在没有静态长程序的情况下，是否仍能通过玻色模式涨落产生类似的重构频率。

Method: 考虑电子与涨落玻色模式耦合，该模式在费米面的尖锐热点（hot spots）之间散射准粒子。发展了一种半经典理论，其中相互作用产生类似磁击穿的时变隧穿过程，即动态磁击穿（dynamical magnetic breakdown）。

Result: 动态磁击穿产生对应于重构费米面面积的新半经典轨道，尽管不存在静态序。由于隧穿概率依赖于玻色激发的热布居，振荡振幅表现出与标准Lifshitz-Kosevich行为的特征性偏离。

Conclusion: 该结果为探测量子临界金属中的玻色涨落提供了一种机制，并为动态磁击穿建立了一个理论框架。这表明量子振荡可以作为研究无静态序系统中涨落现象的有力探针。

Abstract: Quantum oscillations (QO) are a well-established probe of Fermi-surface (FS) geometry and in the presence of long-range density wave order can display new QO frequencies from reconstructed FS pockets. We show that such reconstructed frequencies can arise even in the absence of long-range density order. Considering electrons coupled to a fluctuating bosonic mode that scatters quasiparticles between sharp hot spots on the FS, we develop a semiclassical theory in which the interaction generates time-dependent tunneling processes analogous to magnetic breakdown. This dynamical magnetic breakdown produces new semiclassical orbits corresponding to reconstructed FS areas despite the absence of static order. Because tunneling probabilities depend on the thermal population of bosonic excitations, the resulting oscillation amplitudes exhibit characteristic deviations from standard Lifshitz-Kosevich behavior. Our results provide a mechanism to probe bosonic fluctuations in quantum critical metals and provide a framework for dynamical magnetic breakdown.

</details>


### [135] [Electronic structure of Gd-based intermetallics GdCu$_2$Ge$_2$ and GdCuAl$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23632)
*M. Pinterić,M. Dressel,M. Wenzel,P. Puphal*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过温度依赖的反射率测量，分析了GdCu₂Ge₂和GdCuAl₃两种三元金属间化合物的光学性质，揭示了两种不同散射率的巡游载流子响应，并将电子关联增强归因于费米能级靠近范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究GdCu₂Ge₂和GdCuAl₃两种三元金属间化合物的光学性质，特别是在宽光谱范围（100-18000 cm⁻¹）和低温（低至13 K）条件下的温度依赖行为，以理解其电子结构和载流子动力学。

Method: 采用温度依赖的反射率测量方法，在宽光谱范围（100-18000 cm⁻¹，相当于12 meV-2.23 eV）和低温（低至13 K）条件下对单晶样品进行研究，并结合密度泛函理论（density-functional-theory）计算进行理论支持。

Result: 在2000 cm⁻¹以下，光学谱由两种不同散射率的巡游载流子响应主导：慢载流子响应几乎无温度依赖性，而更易动的载流子响应则遵循直流电阻率行为，在GdCuAl₃中显著抑制。元素取代可描述为费米能级的刚性移动（即掺杂），而晶体对称性变化对电子结构影响较小。

Conclusion: GdCuAl₃中增强的电子关联源于费米能级靠近范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities），这解释了其较高的电阻率和载流子响应的显著抑制。密度泛函理论计算支持元素取代作为掺杂机制的观点，而晶体对称性变化对电子结构影响有限。

Abstract: We present a temperature-dependent reflectivity study of single crystals of the ternary intermetallic compounds GdCu$_2$Ge$_2$ and GdCuAl$_3$ over a broad spectral range (100-18000 cm$^{-1}$, equivalent to 12 meV-2.23 eV) down to 13 K. Below 2000 cm$^{-1}$, the optical spectra are dominated by the response of itinerant charge carriers exhibiting two distinct scattering rates. While the response of the slow charge carriers shows negligible temperature dependence, the more mobile carriers follow the dc resistivity and are significantly suppressed in GdCuAl$_3$, consistent with the higher resistivity of this compound. We attribute this behavior to enhanced electronic correlations arising from the proximity of the Fermi level to van Hove singularities. Supported by density-functional-theory calculations, we further show that elemental substitution can be described as a rigid shift of the Fermi level, i.e., doping, whereas changes in the crystalline symmetry have only minor effects on the electronic structure.

</details>


### [136] [A correlated insulator at the surface of the polar metal Ca$_3$Ru$_2$O$_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23657)
*Daniel Halliday,Izidor Benedičič,Andela Zivanovic,Masahiro Naritsuka,Brendan Edwards,Tommaso Antonelli,Naoki Kikugawa,Dmitry A. Sokolov,Craig Polley,Andrew P. Mackenzie,Georg Held Phil D. C. King,Peter Wahl*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验与理论计算相结合的方法，揭示了Ca₃Ru₂O₇相关氧化物表面存在绝缘相，与体相金属性形成鲜明对比，表明该体系接近绝缘金属态，且细微结构畸变可调控其电子相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究相关氧化物Ca₃Ru₂O₇的表面电子结构，该材料是一种低对称性钌酸盐氧化物，具有非常规极性金属相（unconventional polar-metal phase）。

Method: 采用角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）和扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy）测量相结合的方法，并结合定量低能电子衍射（quantitative low-energy electron diffraction）与电子结构计算。

Result: 研究发现表面存在绝缘相，与体相金属性截然不同；这种表面绝缘性源于表面结构弛豫（surface structure relaxation）与显著电子关联（electronic correlations）的共同作用。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明Ca₃Ru₂O₇接近绝缘金属态（insulating metallic state），并阐明细微结构畸变（subtle structural distortions）如何调控其涌现电子相（emergent electronic phases）。

Abstract: We investigate the electronic structure at the surface of the correlated oxide Ca$_3$Ru$_2$O$_7$, a low-symmetry ruthenate oxide which hosts an unconventional polar-metal phase. From a combination of angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy and scanning tunneling spectroscopy measurements, we demonstrate that the surface hosts an insulating phase, a distinct departure from metallicity within the bulk. Utilizing quantitative low-energy electron diffraction in conjunction with electronic structure calculations, we show how this results from a combined surface structure relaxation and the impact of marked electronic correlations in this system. Our findings highlight the proximity of Ca$_3$Ru$_2$O$_7$ to an insulating metallic state, and illustrate how subtle structural distortions can control its emergent electronic phases.

</details>


### [137] [Mixed-State Topological Phase: Quantized Topological Order Parameter and Lieb-Schultz-Mattis Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24031)
*Linhao Li,Yuan Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究将一维自旋系统中的纯态对称保护拓扑相（SPT）扩展到混合态体系，针对具有强U(1)和弱Z2对称性的系统，提出了短程纠缠混合态的拓扑相序参量，并推广了传统的Lieb-Schultz-Mattis定理至混合态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将纯态对称保护拓扑相（symmetry protected topological phases, SPT）的概念扩展到混合态体系，特别是在具有强U(1)和弱Z2对称性的一维自旋系统中，探索量子通道（quantum channels）框架下的拓扑相分类。

Method: 采用量子通道（quantum channels）概念研究混合态拓扑相，提出短程纠缠混合态的拓扑相序参量（topological phase order parameter），并通过具体含无序的自旋系统实现不同量化值。同时提供与模型无关的方法，通过平移和反射变换生成不同相。

Result: 所提出的拓扑相序参量具有量化特性，其不同值可通过具体含无序的自旋系统实现，并能够锐利地指示相变。这些关于短程纠缠混合态的结果进一步使传统Lieb-Schultz-Mattis定理能够推广到混合态，甚至无需依赖谱隙（spectral gaps）和晶格哈密顿量概念。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将对称保护拓扑相扩展到混合态体系，建立了短程纠缠混合态的拓扑相分类框架，并实现了对传统Lieb-Schultz-Mattis定理在混合态中的推广，为理解无序和耗散系统中的拓扑相提供了新视角。

Abstract: We investigate the extension of pure-state symmetry protected topological phases to mixed-state regime with a strong U(1) and a weak $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetries in one-dimensional spin systems by the concept of quantum channels. We propose a corresponding topological phase order parameter for short-range entangled mixed states by showing that it is quantized and its distinct values can be realized by concrete spin systems with disorders, sharply signaling phase transitions among them. We also give a model-independent way to generate two distinct phases by various types of translation and reflection transformations. These results on the short-range entangled mixed states further enable us to generalize the conventional Lieb-Schultz-Mattis theorem to mixed states, even without the concept of spectral gaps and lattice Hamiltonians.

</details>


### [138] [Reconciling strange metal transport in CeCoIn$_5$ through the difference of optical and cyclotron effective masses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23740)
*Jingyuan Wang,Zhenisbek Tagay,Liyu Shi,Jiahao Liang,Nghiep Khoan Duong,Yi Wu,P. M. T. Vianez,F. Ronning,D. G. Rickel,Darrell G. Schlom,K. M. Shen,S. A. Crooker,N. P. Armitage*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过太赫兹光谱发现CeCoIn₅奇异金属态中隐藏的费米液体行为，电流弛豫率呈现T²标度，光学质量随温度变化，解释了线性电阻率与霍尔角cotθ_H的T²依赖性的共存现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜酸盐超导体中的奇异金属行为（线性温度电阻率和异常霍尔输运）与常规费米液体理论预期不符，而重费米子金属CeCoIn₅表现出类似输运行为，其d波超导基态和强反铁磁涨落与铜酸盐相似，这促使研究者探究其奇异金属态的本质。

Method: 使用时间域太赫兹光谱（time-domain THz spectroscopy, TDTS）在宽磁场范围内测量CeCoIn₅奇异金属态的光学电导率，通过独特的高场太赫兹光谱技术分析电流弛豫率标度行为。

Result: 研究发现电流弛豫率近似按T²标度，表明在大磁场范围内存在隐藏的费米液体态；重准粒子的光学质量大致按1/T标度，而回旋运动质量不受相同的大温度依赖性重整化影响。

Conclusion: 这些发现解释了CeCoIn₅中看似矛盾的输运现象：线性温度电阻率与霍尔角余切（cotθ_H）的T²依赖性共存，实际上反映了费米液体物理，为奇异金属行为提供了新的物理解释框架。

Abstract: The strange metal behavior in cuprate superconductors - characterized by linear in temperature resistivity and anomalous Hall transport - stands in stark contrast to the expectation of conventional Fermi liquid (FL) theory. Remarkably, the similar transport behavior has also been observed in the heavy fermion metal CeCoIn$_5$, whose d-wave superconducting ground state and strong antiferromagnetic fluctuations draw parallels to the cuprates. Here we have investigated the optical conductivity of the strange metal state of CeCoIn$_5$ over a wide magnetic field range using time-domain THz spectroscopy (TDTS). Using unique high-field THz spectroscopy we have shown that the current relaxation rate scales approximately as T$^2$, giving evidence for a hidden Fermi liquid state over a large field range. This result can be reconciled with linear in T resistivity with the realization that heavy quasiparticles have an optical mass that scales roughly like 1/T. This optical mass contrasts with the mass that characterizes cyclotron motion, which does not suffer the same large temperature dependent renormalization. Although by itself anomalous, this allows one to understand a number of other phenomena in CeCoIn$_5$ that have been taken to be signatures of strange metals, including the coexistence of a conventional T$^2$ dependence of the cotangent of the Hall angle with the linear in T resistivity, which with our observation also reflects FL-like physics.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于通过Bethe ansatz方法系统分析一维超对称t-J模型的动力学谱，以理解该模型中分数化激发的特性及其在自旋和电荷通道中的表现。

Method: 采用Bethe ansatz方法，通过两组Bethe数识别分数化激发，分析单电子格林函数（single electron Green functions）谱中的集体激发边界，并考察不同磁化条件下的Bethe弦结构。

Result: 在自旋通道中发现了无能隙激发，其分数化为两个自旋子和一对正负电荷载流子，形成有限能量的多重连续谱；在粒子密度通道中观察到仅涉及电荷涨落的激发；非平庸Bethe弦（nontrivial Bethe strings）在磁化减少或守恒通道中出现，编码束缚态结构。

Abstract: Following the Bethe ansatz we determine the dynamical spectra of the one-dimensional supersymmetric t-J model. A series of fractionalized excitations are identified through two sets of Bethe numbers. Typical patterns in each set are found to yield wavefunctions containing elementary spin and charge carriers, manifested as distinct boundaries of the collective excitations in the spectra of single electron Green functions. In spin channels, gapless excitations fractionalized into two spin and a pair of postive and negative charge carriers, extending to finite energy as multiple continua. These patterns connect to the half-filling limit where only fractionalized spinons survive. In particle density channel, apart from spin-charge fractionalization, excitations involving only charge fluctuations are observed. Furthermore, nontrivial Bethe strings encoding bound state structure appear in channels of reducing or conserving magnetization, where spin and charge constituents can also be identified. These string states contribute significantly even to the low-energy sector in the limit of vanishing magnetization.

</details>


### [140] [Predicting quantum ground-state energy by data-driven Koopman analysis of variational parameter nonlinear dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23887)
*Nobuyuki Okuma*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于数据驱动Koopman分析和变分波函数框架的量子哈密顿量基态能量估计方法。该方法通过收集变分参数非线性动力学的样本点，利用扩展动态模态分解（EDMD）将基态能量计算转化为Koopman生成算子的主导本征值问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，机器学习在物理学中的应用受到广泛关注。本文旨在探索一种结合数据驱动Koopman分析和变分波函数框架的新方法，用于估计量子哈密顿量的基态能量（ground-state energy）。

Method: 该方法基于Koopman理论框架，将虚时薛定谔方程（imaginary-time Schrödinger equation）在变分波函数上的限制描述为变分参数向量的非线性时间演化。通过收集在变分流形（variational manifold）上误差较小的参数配置处的非线性动力学样本点，进行数据驱动的连续Koopman分析。基态能量被转化为Koopman生成算子（Koopman generator）的主导本征值问题，并使用扩展动态模态分解（extended dynamic mode decomposition, EDMD）进行估计。

Result: 作为具体示例，作者为四位置横场伊辛模型（four-site transverse-field Ising model）生成样本，并使用EDMD成功估计了基态能量。此外，该方法被扩展到无限链上均匀矩阵乘积态（uniform matrix product state）作为变分波函数的情况，并利用含时变分原理（time-dependent variational principle）框架下的计算技术，实现了包括误差估计在内的所有分析量的高效计算。

Conclusion: 该方法能够在真实基态位于变分流形之外时仍提供基态能量预测，因此有望补充传统的变分方法。通过结合数据驱动分析和变分原理，为量子系统的基态能量估计提供了一种新的计算框架。

Abstract: In recent years, the application of machine learning to physics has been actively explored. In this paper, we study a method for estimating the ground-state energy of quantum Hamiltonians by applying data-driven Koopman analysis within the framework of variational wave functions. Koopman theory is a framework for analyzing the nonlinear dynamics of vectors, in which the dynamics are linearized by lifting the vectors to functions defined over the original vector space. We focus on the fact that the imaginary-time Schrödinger equation, when restricted to a variational wave function, is described by a nonlinear time evolution of the variational parameter vector. We collect sample points of this nonlinear dynamics at parameter configurations where the discrepancy between the true imaginary-time dynamics and the dynamics on the variational manifold is small, and perform data-driven continuous Koopman analysis. Within our formulation, the ground-state energy is reduced to the leading eigenvalue of a differential operator known as the Koopman generator. As a concrete example, we generate samples for the four-site transverse-field Ising model and estimate the ground-state energy using extended dynamic mode decomposition (EDMD). Furthermore, as an extension of this framework, we formulate the method for the case where the variational wave function is given by a uniform matrix product state on an infinite chain. By employing computational techniques developed within the framework of the time-dependent variational principle, all the quantities required for our analysis, including error estimation, can be computed efficiently in such systems. Since our approach provides predictions for the ground-state energy even when the true ground state lies outside the variational manifold, it is expected to complement conventional variational methods.

</details>


### [141] [Excitonic order in quantum materials: fingerprints, platforms and opportunities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24211)
*Yande Que,Clara Rebanal,Liam Watson,Michael Fuhrer,Michał Papaj,Bent Weber,Iolanda Di Bernardo*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激子绝缘体作为由激子（electron-hole pairs）自发形成的平衡态多体基态，与传统的能带或莫特（Mott）绝缘体有本质区别。该概念虽在半个多世纪前提出，但近期因光谱分辨率、超快探测和材料合成技术的进步而获得新的实验关注。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，首先概述支撑激子序（exciton order）的基本理论要素，讨论维度、无序和屏蔽效应对稳定性的影响。然后系统考察激子态的实验特征，重点聚焦于区分激子序与竞争相（如电荷密度波、莫特绝缘态和杂化驱动绝缘体）的策略。

Result: 文章系统调查了快速增长的候选材料家族，包括层状硫族化合物（layered chalcogenides）、关联稀土化合物、人工激子平台以及光驱动非平衡凝聚体。特别关注了非平庸能带拓扑在其中起作用的系统。

Conclusion: 本文讨论了该领域的关键挑战和新兴机遇，识别了有望塑造未来十年研究的理论和实验前沿，为激子绝缘体研究提供了全面的现状评估和未来展望。

Abstract: The exciton insulator (EI) is a unique many-body ground state of condensed, spontaneously formed excitons (electron-hole pairs) in equilibrium, distinct from conventional band or Mott insulators. Originally proposed over half a century ago, the concept has recently gained renewed experimental traction thanks to advances in spectroscopic resolution, ultrafast probes, and materials synthesis. In this Review, we outline the essential theoretical ingredients underpinning excitonic order and discuss how dimensionality, disorder and screening affect stability. We then examine the diverse experimental fingerprints of the excitonic state, with central focus on strategies to disentangle excitonic order from competing phases such as charge density waves, Mott insulating states, and hybridization-driven insulators, particularly in systems where non-trivial band topology plays a role. We survey the rapidly expanding family of candidate materials, from layered chalcogenides and correlated rare-earth compounds to artificial excitonic platforms and optically driven non-equilibrium condensates. Finally, we discuss the key challenges and emerging opportunities in the field, identifying the theoretical and experimental frontiers that promise to shape the next decade of research.

### [142] [Hidden Unit Interpretability in RBM Quantum States:Encoding Antiferromagnetic Order in Heisenberg Spin Rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24223)
*Bharadwaj Chowdary Mummaneni,Manas Sajjan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 受限玻尔兹曼机（RBM）作为变分波函数时，其隐藏单元自发地专门化以编码一维海森堡自旋环的反铁磁序。重要隐藏单元数量随系统尺寸呈亚线性增长，量子序通过隐藏层的集体编码涌现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究受限玻尔兹曼机（Restricted Boltzmann Machines, RBMs）作为变分波函数时如何编码反铁磁序，特别关注一维海森堡自旋环（Heisenberg spin rings）在周期性边界条件下的情况。旨在理解RBM隐藏单元如何自发组织以捕捉量子多体系统的基态特性。

Method: 对N=4和N=8的自旋系统进行系统的隐藏单元分析和消融研究（ablation studies）。通过隐藏单元密度α=2到5，对N=8到20的系统进行扩展分析，每个配置使用十个独立随机种子。分析包括单个隐藏单元特性、重要性与补充性单元分类，以及移除单元对能量和相关函数的影响。

Result: 隐藏单元自发专门化以捕捉反铁磁基态的交错磁化模式，自然分为两类：对基态能量和相关结构至关重要的单元，以及提供较小修正的补充单元。移除重要单元会导致明显的能量惩罚并破坏C_{zz}(r)中的交错相关模式，而移除补充单元影响较小。重要隐藏单元比例随系统尺寸减小，符合亚线性增长m'∼N^k（k≈0.4）。

Conclusion: 量子序通过隐藏层的集体编码涌现，而非单个隐藏单元。研究结果为量子多体系统中RBM的可解释性提供了定量框架，揭示了隐藏单元组织与系统物理特性之间的定量关系。

Abstract: We investigate how Restricted Boltzmann Machines (RBMs) encode antiferromagnetic order when trained as variational ansätze for one-dimensional Heisenberg spin rings with periodic boundary conditions. Through systematic hidden unit analysis and ablation studies on $N=4$ and $N=8$ spin systems, we show that individual hidden units spontaneously specialize to capture staggered magnetization patterns characteristic of antiferromagnetic ground states. Hidden units naturally segregate into two classes: those essential for ground-state energy and correlation structure, and supplementary units providing smaller corrections. Removing important units induces clear energy penalties and disrupts the staggered correlation pattern in $C_{zz}(r)$, whereas removing supplementary units has modest effects. Single-unit analysis confirms that no individual hidden unit reproduces the full antiferromagnetic correlations, indicating that quantum order emerges through collective encoding across the hidden layer. Extending this analysis to $N=8$ through $20$ with hidden unit densities $α= 2$ to $5$ and ten independent seeds per configuration, we find that the fraction of important hidden units decreases with system size, consistent with sublinear growth $m' \sim N^k$ ($k \approx 0.4$). The energy-correlation impact relationship persists for small to moderate system sizes, though it weakens for the largest systems studied. These results provide a quantitative framework for RBM interpretability in quantum many-body systems.

### [143] [Universal Quantum Suppression in Frustrated Ising Magnets across the Quasi-1D to 2D Crossover via Quantum Annealing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24311)
*Kumar Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究利用D-Wave Advantage2量子退火机（729个自旋）解决了MNb₂O₆和BaCo₂V₂O₈家族量子磁体中的阻挫横向场伊辛模型（frustrated transverse-field Ising model）相变问题，该模型存在符号问题（sign problem）导致传统量子蒙特卡洛方法失效。研究测量了不同各向异性参数α下的量子临界点，揭示了量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）对经典铁磁稳定窗口的抑制规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MNb₂O₆和BaCo₂V₂O₈家族量子磁体实现的阻挫横向场伊辛模型存在符号问题，该问题在任意系统尺寸下对量子蒙特卡洛方法都是不可解的，导致其量子相边界无法通过数值方法获得。这阻碍了对这些量子磁体相变行为的理解。

Method: 使用D-Wave Advantage2量子退火机在L≤27（729个自旋）的系统尺寸下进行研究。通过测量不同各向异性参数α下的量子临界点g_c^{QPU}，并与经典阈值g_c^{class}(α)=2α/3进行比较。采用内Binder累积量对（inner Binder cumulant pairs）等分析方法，该量在热力学极限下收敛最快。

Result: 获得了α∈{1.0, 0.7, 0.5, 0.3}对应的量子临界点g_c^{QPU}∈{0.286, 0.210, 0.156, 0.093}。抑制比r(α)呈现明显的两区域结构：三个准一维几何（α≤0.7）与普适平台r̄=0.450一致，表明量子涨落破坏了约55%的经典铁磁稳定窗口；在经验交叉尺度α*≈0.7以上，r下降到二维极限。四参数线性拟合r(α)=0.494-0.063α总结了两个区域的行为。

Conclusion: 所有四种几何结构都显示出从铁磁体到顺磁体的直接相变、完全的量子遍历性（f_uniq=1.000）以及零价键固体序（null valence-bond solid order）。两个顺序的盲预测在测量前分别以0.2σ和0.7σ的精度得到确认，验证了交叉规律的有效性。研究成功解决了传统数值方法无法处理的量子相变问题。

Abstract: Quantum magnets in the $M\mathrm{Nb_2O_6}$ and BaCo$_2$V$_2$O$_8$ families realise frustrated transverse-field Ising models whose competing ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic couplings generate a sign problem provably intractable for quantum Monte Carlo at any system size, leaving their quantum phase boundaries numerically Inaccessible. Using a D-Wave Advantage2 quantum annealer at $L\leq27$ (729 spins), we obtain the large-$L$ critical points for this model family, measuring quantum-driven transitions at ${g_c^{\mathrm{QPU}}}\in\{0.286,\,0.210,\,0.156,\,0.093\}$ for $α\in\{1.0,\,0.7,\,0.5,\,0.3\}$, where the analytically exact classical threshold is ${g_c^{\mathrm{class}}}(α)=2α/3$. The suppression ratio $r(α)$ exhibits a sharp two-regime structure: the three quasi-1D geometries ($α\leq0.7$) are mutually consistent with a universal plateau $\bar{r}=0.450$ ($χ^2/\mathrm{dof}=1.10$, $p=0.33$), demonstrating that quantum fluctuations destroy approximately $55\%$ of the classical FM stability window independently of coupling anisotropy, while $r$ steps down to the 2D limit above the empirical crossover scale $α^*\approx0.7$. Inner Binder cumulant pairs, which converge fastest to the thermodynamic limit, resolve $r(1.0)\approx0.412$ and a step $Δr=0.038\pm0.015$ from the quasi-1D plateau. A four-point linear fit $r(α)=0.494-0.063\,α$ summarises both regimes; its $α\to0$ intercept recovers the exact 1D result of Pfeuty within 1.7 standard deviations, and its slope is a lower bound on the true crossover amplitude concentrated in $α\in[α^*,1]$. Two sequential blind predictions, confirmed at $0.2σ$ and $0.7σ$ before each measurement, validate the crossover law. All four geometries show a direct ferromagnet-to-paramagnet transition, complete quantum ergodicity ($f_{\rm uniq}=1.000$), and null valence-bond solid order.

Conclusion: 打破完美晶格平移对称性并考虑局域近藤温度分布，为所有重费米子系统在量子临界点提供了统一的理论描述框架，超越了传统基于周期性势场假设的电子结构理论。

Because the zero-point motion of the ions, however, in correlated electron systems the electronic environment experienced by an itinerant electron is neither static nor self-averaging at the single-particle level, even in perfectly stoichiometric crystals, leading to a distribution of local Kondo scales that spans two orders of magnitude in temperature. We discuss, through a comparison between uniform scenarios and one that breaks with perfect lattice translational symmetry, how incorporating this distribution yields a unified description for all heavy-fermion systems at the quantum critical point.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索在保持所有对称性的外部周期驱动场作用下，交织序场理论的相图特征，特别是比较传统朗道竞争序理论和分数化理论的行为差异。

Method: 采用大N极限（large N limit）方法，将系统与马尔可夫浴耦合，分析两种理论框架：传统朗道竞争序理论和分数化理论，其中序参数是底层多分量希格斯场（multi-component Higgs field）的不同复合物。

Result: 研究发现长时间极限下系统表现出多种行为模式：非零平均值、以驱动周期或其半周期振荡、准周期振荡（quasi-periodic oscillations）或混沌行为（chaotic behavior），揭示了周期驱动下交织序系统的丰富动力学相图。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，在对称性保持的周期驱动场作用下，交织序场理论展现出复杂的相图结构，包括周期性、准周期性和混沌动力学行为，为理解非平衡条件下竞争序系统的演化提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We obtain the phase diagrams of field theories of intertwined orders in the presence of periodic driving by an external field which preserves all symmetries. We consider both a conventional Landau theory of competing orders, and a fractionalized theory in which the order parameters are distinct composites of an underlying multi-component Higgs field. We work in the large $N$ limit and couple to a Markovian bath. The long time limits are characterized by non-zero average values, oscillations with the drive period and/or half the drive period, quasi-periodic oscillations, or chaotic behavior.

</details>

### [148] [Capacitive Pixelated CMOS Electronic Nose](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23537)
*M. A. Basyooni-M. Kabatas,Tao Shen,Kai Betlem,Chunyu Huang,Monique A. van der Veen,Frans Widdershoven,Murali K. Ghatkesar,Peter G. Steeneken*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种基于CMOS芯片的电容式电子鼻（E-nose），通过喷墨打印功能化1024个微电极阵列，利用金属有机框架（MOFs）材料实现对挥发性有机化合物（VOCs）的选择性检测，具有低功耗、低成本和高集成度特点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
