Method: 采用互补金属氧化物半导体（CMOS）芯片上的1024个电容微电极阵列，通过喷墨打印进行功能化处理。像素点涂覆UV固化油墨和金属有机框架（MOFs：ZIF-8、MIL-101(Cr)、MIL-140A）材料，形成化学多样性微域，通过吸附驱动的介电负载产生气体特异性响应模式。

Result: ZIF-8对2-丁酮（2-butanone）响应最高，而UV固化层对甲苯（toluene）响应最强；两者对水蒸气交叉敏感性低，可在潮湿条件下工作。在纯气体校准后，观察到对甲苯和2-丁酮二元混合物的可重复响应。设备功耗低，结合了大型1024像素阵列与CMOS集成。

Conclusion: 该电子鼻通过喷墨打印提供应用特定功能化，兼具低成本和多功能性。通过扩展功能化材料范围，可应用于多种气体分析，在安全监测、健康、农业和机器人等领域具有潜在应用前景。

Abstract: Although some of the human senses can nowadays be replaced by low-cost electronic sensors such as microphones and image sensors, a compact low-cost electronic nose (E-nose) remains elusive. In this work, an E-nose is presented that can capacitively detect volatile organic compounds (VOCs). The E-nose consists of an array of 1024 capacitive microelectrodes on a complementary metal-oxide-semiconductor (CMOS) chip, functionalized by inkjet printing. The pixels are coated with a UV-curable ink and metal-organic frameworks (MOFs: ZIF-8, MIL-101(Cr), MIL-140A) to create chemically diverse microdomains that generate gas-specific response patterns through adsorption-driven dielectric loading. ZIF-8 exhibits the highest response to 2-butanone, whereas the UV-curable layer responds most strongly to toluene; both show low cross-sensitivity to water vapor, enabling operation under humid conditions. After calibration in pure gases, reproducible responses to controlled binary mixtures of toluene and 2-butanone are observed. The device operates at low power, combines a large 1024-pixel array with CMOS integration, and offers application-specific functionalization by inkjet printing, providing both low cost and versatility. By further extending the range of functionalization materials, the E-nose can be applied to analyze a wide variety of gases, with potential applications in safety monitoring, health, agriculture, and robotics.

### [149] [Threshold asymptotics and decay for massive Maxwell on subextremal Reissner--Nordström](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23905)
*Bobby Eka Gunara*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文研究了亚极端Reissner-Nordström时空外部的中性有质量Maxwell（Proca）方程。通过球谐分解，分析了奇偶模态的渐近行为，建立了阈值谱理论，并推导了极化分辨的中间尾迹和普适的晚期t^{-5/6}分支切割律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究亚极端Reissner-Nordström时空外部中性有质量Maxwell（Proca）方程的动力学行为，特别关注其渐近极化分裂和晚期衰减特性。

Method: 采用球谐分解方法，将奇模态简化为标量问题，偶模态则处理为2×2耦合系统。建立了阈值谱理论，证明了截断预解式（cut-off resolvent）的亚纯延拓，并分析了分支切割跳跃（branch-cut jump）的展开。

Result: 证明了偶系统在空间无穷远处存在精确的渐近极化分裂，产生的三个通道具有有效角动量ℓ-1、ℓ、ℓ+1。推导了极化分辨的中间尾迹和普适的t^{-5/6}分支切割律，并获得了Proca场的两区渐近展开。

Conclusion: 未分裂的完整Proca场服从对数型紧致区域衰减，而辐射分支切割贡献保持显式的多项式渐近行为和明确的领先系数，为有质量矢量场在黑洞时空中的动力学提供了完整的理论描述。

Abstract: We study the neutral massive Maxwell (Proca) equation on subextremal Reissner--Nordström exteriors. After spherical-harmonic decomposition, the odd sector is scalar, while the even sector remains a genuinely coupled $2\times2$ system. Our starting point is that this even system admits an exact asymptotic polarization splitting at spatial infinity. The three resulting channels carry effective angular momenta $\ell-1$, $\ell$, and $\ell+1$, and these are precisely the indices that govern the late-time thresholds. %
For each fixed angular momentum we develop a threshold spectral theory for the cut-off resolvent. We prove meromorphic continuation across the massive branch cut, rule out upper-half-plane modes and threshold resonances, and obtain explicit small- and large-Coulomb expansions for the branch-cut jump. Inverting this jump yields polarization-resolved intermediate tails together with the universal very-late $t^{-5/6}$ branch-cut law. %
At the full-field level, high-order angular regularity allows us to sum the modewise leading terms on compact radial sets and obtain a two-regime asymptotic expansion for the radiative branch-cut component of the Proca field, with explicit coefficient fields and quantitative remainders. We also analyze the quasibound resonance branches created by stable timelike trapping, prove residue and reconstruction bounds, and derive a fully self-contained dyadic packet estimate. As a result, the unsplit full Proca field obeys logarithmic compact-region decay, while the radiative branch-cut contribution retains explicit polynomial asymptotics and explicit leading coefficients.

### [150] [Qcombo: A Python Package for Automated Commutator Calculations of Quantum Many-Body Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24399)
*L. H. Chen,Y. Li,H. Hergert,J. M. Yao*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: qcombo是一个用于符号计算量子多体算符对易子的Python包，利用广义维克定理处理正规排序算符，自动化生成代数表达式，减少人工推导错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代多体方法在核物理、量子化学等领域的开发与实现需要处理复杂冗长的解析推导，人工推导易出错，需要自动化工具来降低错误风险。

Method: qcombo基于广义维克定理（generalized Wick theorem），对正规排序形式（normal-ordered form）的量子多体算符进行符号计算，提供自动化系统化框架生成代数表达式。

Result: 该包成功应用于介质内相似重整化群（IMSRG）方法，自动生成了完整的多参考IMSRG流方程集，算符截断至正规排序三体水平。

Conclusion: qcombo为核物理、量子化学及相关领域的现代多体方法开发提供了有效的自动化工具，显著减少了复杂解析推导中的人为错误风险。

Abstract: qcombo is a Python package for the symbolic evaluation of commutators between general quantum many-body operators expressed in normal-ordered form using the generalized Wick theorem. The package provides an automated and systematic framework for generating the corresponding algebraic expressions, significantly reducing the risk of human error in lengthy and complex analytical derivations. It is designed to assist the development and implementation of modern many-body methods in nuclear physics, quantum chemistry, and related fields. The functionality and workflow of the package are demonstrated through an application to the in-medium similarity renormalization group (IMSRG) method, which has been widely used for nuclear ab initio calculations. As a representative example, qcombo is employed to automatically generate the complete set of multi-reference IMSRG flow equations with operators truncated at the normal-ordered three-body level.

### [151] [Optimal local interventions in the two-dimensional Abelian sandpile model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24459)
*Maike C. de Jongh,Richard J. Boucherie,M. N. M. van Lieshout*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文对阿贝尔沙堆模型（Abelian sandpile model）中的干预策略进行了首次严格分析，研究了通过移除选定位置沙粒来减小雪崩（avalanche）规模的方法，发现最优干预位置需要在减少最大雪崩规模与增加受控雪崩数量之间取得平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿贝尔沙堆模型作为自组织临界性（self-organized criticality）的典型示例，其雪崩现象常被视为地震或森林火灾等灾难性事件的简化表征。基于这一视角，本文旨在研究减少雪崩规模的策略，为阿贝尔沙堆模型中的干预影响提供首次严格分析。

Method: 研究考虑外部控制器可通过移除选定位置的沙粒来扰动配置。首先开发并形式化了一种扩展方法来计算源自临界顶点（critical vertices）连通分量的雪崩期望规模，然后利用该方法分析正方形分量中雪崩的结构，并明确分析在此类分量中干预的效果。

Result: 研究结果表明，最优干预位置需要在减少最大雪崩规模与增加受控雪崩数量之间取得平衡。通过分析正方形分量中雪崩的结构，明确揭示了干预措施对雪崩动态的影响机制。

Conclusion: 本文为阿贝尔沙堆模型中的干预策略提供了首个严格分析框架，揭示了最优干预位置需要在雪崩规模减小与受控事件数量增加之间权衡的规律，为理解自组织临界系统中的控制策略提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The Abelian sandpile model serves as a canonical example of self-organized criticality. This critical behavior manifests itself through large cascading events triggered by small perturbations. Such large-scale events, known as avalanches, are often regarded as stylized representations of catastrophic phenomena, such as earthquakes or forest fires. Motivated by this perspective, we study strategies to reduce avalanche sizes. We provide a first rigorous analysis of the impact of interventions in the Abelian sandpile model, considering a setting in which an external controller can perturb a configuration by removing sand grains at selected locations. We first develop and formalize an extended method to compute the expected size of an avalanche originating from a connected component of critical vertices, i.e., vertices at maximum height. Using this method, we characterize the structure of avalanches starting from square components and explicitly analyze the effect of interventions in such components. Our results show that the optimal intervention locations strike an interesting balance between reduction of largest avalanche sizes and increasing the number of mitigated avalanches.

### [152] [Geometry-tunable magnetic edge contrast in Bi2Te3 Corbino nanoplates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23693)
*Motahhare Mirhosseini,Swathi Kadaba,Allison Swyt,David L. Carroll*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了Te棒模板溶液生长方法（Te-rod-templated solution growth method），制备具有Corbino几何结构的Bi2Te3纳米片（nanoplates）。使用优化的磁力显微镜（magnetic force microscopy）技术，通过系统改变尖端高度和振荡幅度来区分真实的磁响应与静电和形貌效应。

Result: 成功制备了单晶、具有明确中心孔的少五重层（few-quintuple-layer）六角形Bi2Te3纳米片。观察到内外边缘的清晰磁对比信号，该信号强烈依赖于尖端参数。通过系统改变孔径大小，发现边缘对比随边缘间距减小而增强，表明内外边缘通道（edge channels）之间的耦合更强。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了几何可控的平台来调控Bi2Te3中的边缘局域磁行为，为探索二维拓扑绝缘体中的边缘相互作用开辟了新路径。Corbino几何结构为研究边缘通道耦合提供了有效的实验平台。

Abstract: Two-dimensional topological insulators feature helical edge states that are remarkably resistant to disorder, making them appeal for energy-efficient electronics and quantum information technologies. In this study, we develop a Te-rod-templated solution growth method to create Bi2Te3 nanoplates with a Corbino geometry. The resulting few-quintuple-layer hexagonal plates are single-crystalline and contain well-defined central pores. Using optimized magnetic force microscopy, we observe clear magnetic contrast at both the inner and outer edges. The signal depends strongly on tip height and oscillation amplitude, allowing us to distinguish genuine magnetic responses from electrostatic and topographic effects. By systematically varying the pore size, we find that edge contrast increases as the distance between edges decreases, suggesting stronger coupling between the inner and outer edge channels. These findings establish a geometry-controlled platform for tuning edge-localized magnetic behavior in Bi2Te3 and open a new path to explore edge interactions in two-dimensional topological insulators.

### [153] [Theoretical Prediction of Three-Dimensional $sp^2$-free Graphyne-Based Nanomaterials via Density Functional Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23712)
*Djardiel da S. Gomes,Alexandre F. Fonseca,Marcelo L. Pereira*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过将二维石墨炔（graphyne）片层通过垂直乙炔桥共价连接，构建了三维石墨炔衍生框架（3DGY），发现了β-和γ-3DGY两种稳定的三维碳同素异形体，具有独特的力学、电子和光学性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找具有定制维度和性质的碳基材料是材料科学的重要课题，特别是在电子学、光子学和纳米力学应用中。石墨炔（graphyne）作为一类新兴的二维碳同素异形体，为构建新型三维碳材料提供了平台。

Method: 通过将堆叠的α-、β-和γ-石墨炔片层通过垂直乙炔桥（out-of-plane acetylene bridges）共价连接，构建三维石墨炔衍生框架（3DGY）。采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算和从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics, AIMD）模拟来评估稳定性并研究其性质。

Result: α-衍生框架在该方案中未收敛到稳定构型，而β-和γ-3DGY相形成了稳定结构。力学分析显示各向异性弹性行为，电子结构计算表明β-3DGY具有约0.15 eV的间接带隙，γ-3DGY具有约1.65 eV的间接带隙。光学计算显示各向异性响应，吸收范围从红外到可见光区域。

Conclusion: β-3DGY和γ-3DGY被确认为新型三维碳同素异形体，具有独特的力学、电子和光学性质，为碳基材料在电子、光子和纳米力学应用中的发展提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: The search for carbon-based materials with tailored dimensionality and properties remains an important topic in materials science, particularly for applications in electronics, photonics, and nanomechanics. Among the emerging platforms in this context, graphyne (GY) represents a class of two-dimensional (2D) carbon allotropes composed of benzene rings connected by acetylenic linkages, yielding networks containing both $sp$- and $sp^2$-hybridized carbon atoms. By analogy with the transformation of $sp^2$ carbon networks such as graphene into $sp^3$-bonded diamond through interlayer covalent bonding, we construct three-dimensional (3D) GY-derived frameworks (3DGY) by covalently connecting stacked $α$-, $β$-, and $γ$-GY sheets via out-of-plane acetylene bridges. This approach converts the original $sp^2$ nodes into $sp^3$ centers while preserving the $sp$ character of the acetylenic segments, producing fully $sp$-$sp^3$ carbon networks. Structural relaxation shows that the $α$-derived framework does not converge to a stable configuration within this scheme, whereas the $β$- and $γ$-3DGY phases form stable architectures. Density functional theory (DFT) calculations, combined with ab initio molecular dynamics (AIMD) simulations, confirm the energetic, thermal, and dynamical stability of these two systems and are further used to investigate their structural, mechanical, electronic, and optical properties. Mechanical analysis reveals anisotropic elastic behavior, whereas electronic structure calculations show indirect band gaps of approximately 0.15 eV for $β$-3DGY and 1.65 eV for γ-3DGY. Optical calculations further reveal anisotropic responses, with absorption extending from the infrared to the visible. These results identify β-3DGY and γ-3DGY as new three-dimensional carbon allotropes with distinct mechanical, electronic, and optical properties.

</details>


### [154] [Quantum-classical dynamics of Rashba spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23758)
*Paul Bergold,Giovanni Manfredi,Cesare Tronci*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了koopmon方法以处理自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling），在一维Rashba纳米线模型中对比了完全量子模拟、Ehrenfest方法和新量子-经典混合模型的动力学表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子-经典混合模型虽能降低完全量子模拟的计算成本，但其在不同问题类别中的普适性仍待验证。本研究特别关注具有自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的系统，以探索混合模型在此类问题中的适用性。

Method: 采用基于经典力学中Koopman波函数的新量子-经典哈密顿模型，该模型保留了海森堡原理（Heisenberg principle）并能捕捉超越传统Ehrenfest方法的关联效应。扩展了koopmon粒子方案以处理自旋轨道耦合，应用于一维Rashba纳米线模型，涵盖有无谐波势（harmonic potential）以及Rashba主导（强耦合）和Zeeman主导（弱耦合）的不同参数区间。

Result: 在无外势情况下，koopmon方法在所有耦合区间都能定性复现完全量子演化的特征。虽然相比Ehrenfest模拟在自旋精度上略有损失，但后者无法捕捉轨道动力学。在存在谐波势时，koopmon方案在量子与经典部分均能以Ehrenfest模型无法达到的精度水平重现完全量子结果。研究还展示了猫态（cat-like states）形成的测试案例。

Conclusion: 扩展的koopmon方法能有效处理自旋轨道耦合系统，在轨道动力学再现方面优于传统Ehrenfest方法，为量子-经典混合模型在复杂耦合系统中的适用性提供了有力证据。

Abstract: Mixed quantum-classical models are widely used to reduce the computational cost of fully quantum simulations. However, their general applicability across different classes of problems remains an open question. Here, we address this issue for systems featuring spin-orbit coupling. In particular, we study the interaction dynamics of quantum spin-1/2 and classical orbital momentum in one-dimensional models of Rashba nanowires. We tackle this problem by resorting to a new quantum-classical Hamiltonian model that, unlike conventional approaches, retains the Heisenberg principle and captures correlation effects beyond the common Ehrenfest approach. Based on Koopman wavefunctions in classical mechanics, the new model was recently implemented numerically via a particle scheme -- the koopmon method -- which is extended here to treat spin-orbit coupling. We apply the koopmon method to study the quantum-classical dynamics of nanowire models, with and without the presence of a harmonic potential and in both Rashba-dominated (strong coupling) and Zeeman-dominated (weak coupling) regimes. Considering realistic semiconductor parameters, the results are contrasted with both fully quantum and quantum-classical Ehrenfest dynamics. In the absence of external potential, the koopmon method qualitatively reproduces the features of the fully quantum evolution for all coupling regimes. While it exhibits a slight loss in spin accuracy compared to Ehrenfest simulations, the latter fail to capture the orbital dynamics. In the presence of a harmonic potential, the koopmon scheme reproduces the full quantum results with accuracy levels that are unachievable by the Ehrenfest model in both quantum and classical sectors. We conclude by presenting a test case that exhibits the formation of cat-like states.

</details>


### [155] [Investigating spin and orbital effects via spin-torque ferromagnetic resonance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23826)
*J. L. Costa,E. Santos,A. Y. M. Tani,J. B. S. Mendes,A. Azevedo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过自旋转矩铁磁共振（ST-FMR）技术，在不同正常金属（NM）材料组成的双层系统中实验研究了自旋和轨道转矩现象。使用坡莫合金（Py）和镍（Ni）作为铁磁（FM）层分别探测自旋和轨道转矩响应，提取了阻尼型和场型转矩分量及效率，并首次实验证实了面外转矩分量的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过实验探究不同正常金属材料双层系统中的自旋和轨道转矩现象，特别是验证轨道霍尔效应（OHE）相关的轨道转矩存在，为基于轨道转矩的磁化翻转技术提供实验依据。

Method: 采用自旋转矩铁磁共振（spin-torque ferromagnetic resonance, ST-FMR）技术，在SiO₂/FM/NM双层结构系统中进行实验研究。使用坡莫合金（Py）和镍（Ni）作为铁磁层分别探测自旋和轨道转矩响应，通过施加磁场的方位角依赖性分析来支持实验解释。

Result: 实验成功提取了所有样品的阻尼型（damping-like）和场型（field-like）转矩分量及其效率，并与先前文献中的数值和实验数据进行了比较。首次实验证实了面外（out-of-plane）转矩分量的存在，该分量归因于界面机制和沿z方向的自旋轨道极化电流。研究结果为多种材料中轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect, OHE）相关的轨道转矩提供了有力证据。

Conclusion: 本研究通过ST-FMR技术系统研究了自旋和轨道转矩现象，实验证实了轨道转矩在多种材料中的存在，这拓展了基于轨道转矩驱动磁化翻转的应用前景，为自旋轨道电子学（spintronics）领域提供了重要的实验支持。

Abstract: In this work, we experimentally investigate spin and orbital torque phenomena using the spin-torque ferromagnetic resonance (ST-FMR) technique in a series of bilayer systems composed of different normal metal (NM) materials. Permalloy (Py) and Ni were employed as ferromagnetic (FM) layers to probe the spin and orbital torque responses, respectively. For the SiO$_2$/FM/NM bilayers, we extracted the damping-like and field-like torque components, as well as the damping-like torque efficiency for each sample, and compared our results with previously reported numerical and experimental data in the literature. Additionally, we experimentally demonstrate the presence of an out-of-plane torque component, which we attribute to interfacial mechanisms and associate with a spin-orbital polarized current along the $z$-direction. This interpretation is supported by the azimuthal angular dependence of the applied magnetic field. Our results provide compelling evidence of orbital torque associated with the orbital Hall effect (OHE) in several materials, thereby broadening the prospects for magnetization switching driven by orbital torque.

</details>


### [156] [Numerical analysis of the thermal relaxation of the dense gas between two parallel plates: the free energy monotonicity for the Enskog equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23839)
*Shigeru Takata,Soma Sakata,Aoto Takahashi,Masanari Hattori*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 研究两个相同温度平行板间稠密气体的热弛豫问题，通过对比原始和修正Enskog因子的Enskog方程，分析非平衡态自由能的时间演化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究由Enskog方程描述的稠密气体在两平行板间的热弛豫问题，特别关注非平衡态自由能的行为特征。

Method: 采用两种Enskog方程：一种是包含原始Enskog因子的方程，另一种是采用Takata & Takahashi (2025)近期提出的修正Enskog因子版本。通过对比分析这两种模型在相同温度平行板系统中的表现。

Result: 研究发现，修正因子版本的自由能随时间单调递减，而原始版本则不一定呈现此特性。两种模型在其他物理量的时间演化上也存在差异，最典型的是密度剖面分布。

Conclusion: 修正Enskog因子版本在描述稠密气体非平衡态热弛豫时表现出更合理的自由能单调递减行为，这为改进稠密气体动力学模型提供了重要参考。

Abstract: The thermal relaxation problem between two parallel plates with the same temperature is investigated, aiming to study the behavior of the free energy of the dense gas described by the Enskog equation. Two types of Enskog equation have been used: one is the Enskog equation with the original Enskog factor, while the other is that with a modified Enskog factor proposed recently in Takata & Takahashi, Phys. Rev. E 111, 065108 (2025). The evaluated free energy is a natural extension of the thermodynamic free energy to the non-equilibrium state. It is observed that this free energy monotonically decreases in time for the modified factor version, while it is not necessarily the case for the original version. Differences are also observed in other quantities in their time evolutions, most typically in the density profile.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 基于维度扩展方法预测了三维j波磁体。研究发现通过测量非线性自旋电流可以完全识别X波磁体类型，并预测了h波和j波奇宇称磁体中特定高阶自旋电流的存在。

Abstract: Higher-order symmetric $X$-wave magnets consist of two groups. One includes $d$-wave, $g$-wave and $i$-wave altermagnets, while the other includes $p$-wave and $f$-wave odd-parity magnets. Motivated by this development, we systematically construct an $X$-wave magnet with $\left( N_{X}+1\right) $ nodes in three dimensions from an $X$-wave magnet with $N_{X}$ nodes in two dimensions by means of a dimensional extension, where $N_X=1,2,3,4,6$ for $X=p,d,f,g,i$, respectively. Based on this method, we predict $j$-wave magnets in three dimensions. Then, we argue how to identify each of these $X$-wave magnets experimentally. We show that the $X$-wave magnet is completely identified by measuring the nonlinear spin currents. In particular, we predict that there are no spin currents other than the fourth-order ones such as $σ_{\text{spin}}^{x^{3}y;z}$ in $h$-wave odd-parity magnets in three dimensions and the sixth-order ones such as $σ_{\text{spin}}^{x^{5}y;z}$ in $j$-wave odd-parity magnets in three dimensions. They function as spin-current diodes because the spin current exhibits unidirectional flow independent of the applied electric field.

Abstract: The energy spectrum and wave functions of electrons in a single silicon quantum dot provide valuable insights into the capabilities and limitations of such a system in quantum information processing. Here we investigate the low-lying singlet and triplet configurations and spectra in a two-electron silicon quantum dot. To build toward a comprehensive understanding, we first examine the competition between Coulomb interaction and electron kinetic and confinement energy in the absence of valley-orbit coupling, as well as consequences of valley blockade in the presence of an ideal smooth interface. For realistic interfaces the variations in the magnitude and phase of valley-orbit coupling lead to inter-valley leakage, particularly when orbital splittings approach the valley splitting. In our study we particularly focus on the impact on the compositions of low-lying singlets and triplets. We find that for experimentally relevant parameter regimes the ground singlet and triplet states usually contain multiple configurations with significant weights as a result of a complicated competition among valley-orbit coupling, confinement potential, and Coulomb interaction. We further analyze the effects of an out-of-plane magnetic field on these the two-electron spectra. Our findings could have important implications for spin qubits in Si quantum dot in various contexts, such as qubit encoding and spin measurement.

### [159] [Layer-Selective Proximity Symmetry Breaking Enables Anomalous and Nonlinear Hall Responses in 1H-TMD Metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24019)
*Yusuf Wicaksono,Toshikaze Kariyado*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过层选择性磁邻近效应解锁了金属性1H-NbX₂中的线性和非线性霍尔效应，其中原生D₃h对称性原本禁止这些效应。理论计算显示面外交换作用产生可观的异常霍尔电导，而面内交换分量则产生可调谐的贝里曲率偶极子和非线性霍尔响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性霍尔响应是探测量子几何的直接电学手段，但在许多原始二维金属中因对称性限制而被禁止。研究旨在通过磁邻近效应解锁金属性1H-NbX₂（X=S, Se, Te）中的线性和非线性霍尔效应，这些材料原本的D₃h对称性使异常霍尔电导和贝里曲率偶极子（Berry-curvature dipole, BCD）为零。

Method: 采用完全相对论密度泛函理论（fully relativistic density-functional theory）结合Wannier插值方法，研究层选择性磁邻近效应。分析面外邻近交换保持C₃对称性时的情况，以及通过添加面内交换分量（或正交双面交换纹理）打破C₃对称性的情况。

Result: 面外邻近交换产生可观的片层异常霍尔电导σ⁽ˢʰᵉᵉᵗ⁾ₓᵧ ∼ 10⁻²(e²/h)，同时保持BCD为零。打破C₃对称性产生强可调谐的BCD和非线性霍尔电导，其大小与面内交换尺度近似线性相关，|D_y|达到10⁻²埃量级，在NbTe₂中达到最大值。这些幅度意味着在微米尺度霍尔棒中，毫安级交流驱动下可产生易于测量的二次谐波霍尔电压。

Conclusion: 层选择性磁邻近效应能够解锁原本对称性禁止的线性和非线性霍尔响应。研究进一步提出双界面器件概念，其中一次和二次谐波霍尔电压的符号可通过相同接触点提供两位读取输出，为量子几何探测和器件应用提供了新途径。

Abstract: Nonlinear Hall responses are a direct electrical probe of quantum geometry, but they are symmetry-forbidden in many pristine two-dimensional metals. We show that layer-selective magnetic proximity unlocks intrinsic linear and nonlinear Hall effects in metallic $1H-NbX_2$ ($X=\mathrm{S,Se,Te}$), where native $D_{3h}$ symmetry forces both the anomalous Hall conductivity and the Berry-curvature dipole (BCD) to vanish. Fully relativistic density-functional theory combined with Wannier interpolation reveals that an out-of-plane proximity exchange that preserves $C_3$ generates a sizable sheet anomalous Hall conductivity, $σ^{\mathrm{sheet}}_{xy} \sim 10^{-2}(e^2/h)$, while keeping the BCD exactly zero. Breaking $C_3$ by adding an in-plane exchange component (or an orthogonal two-sided exchange texture) produces a strongly tunable BCD and hence a nonlinear Hall conductivity that is odd and approximately linear in the in-plane exchange scale, reaching $|D_y|$ of order $10^{-2}$ angstrom and maximized in NbTe$_2$. These magnitudes imply a readily measurable second-harmonic Hall voltage in micron-scale Hall bars under mA ac drive. We further propose a dual-interface device in which the signs of the first- and second-harmonic Hall voltages provide two-bit readout using the same contacts.

*Mingxing Wu,Kouta Kondou,Taishi Chen,Satoru Nakatsuji,YoshiChika Otani*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过铁磁共振技术比较了不同晶体取向的Mn$_3$Ge/Py双层结构中自旋力矩，揭示了非共线反铁磁体中面外自旋极化的微观起源主要来自体磁自旋霍尔效应（MSHE）和界面自旋交换效应（SSW）的共同贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用铁磁共振技术（ferromagnetic resonance technique）比较了具有不同晶体取向的单晶Mn$_3$Ge/Py双层结构中的自旋力矩。通过测量自旋力矩信号的角依赖关系来区分不同机制的贡献。

Result: 测量到的自旋力矩信号具有明显的角依赖性，这为体磁自旋霍尔效应（MSHE）提供了明确证据，该效应依赖于反铁磁序。同时识别出源于界面自旋交换效应（SSW）的反铁磁序无关分量。MSHE和SSW共存且具有相当的量级，共同产生了面外自旋极化。

Conclusion: 该研究阐明了非共线反铁磁体中自旋力矩产生的起源，为它们在自旋电子学（spintronic）应用提供了有价值的见解。研究成功区分了MSHE和SSW两种机制的贡献，解决了关于面外自旋极化微观起源的争议。

Abstract: The noncollinear antiferromagnets Mn$_3$Sn/Ge emerge as promising spin-current sources with both in-plane and out-of-plane spin polarizations, thereby enabling field-free magnetization switching. However, the microscopic origin of the out-of-plane spin polarization remains under debate, specifically whether it arises from the magnetic spin Hall effect (MSHE) or the spin swapping (SSW). Here, we comparatively evaluate the spin torques in single-crystal Mn$_3$Ge/Py bilayers with different crystallographic orientations using the ferromagnetic resonance technique. The distinct angular dependences of the measured spin-torque signals provide clear evidence for the bulk MSHE, which depends on antiferromagnetic order. In addition, we identify the antiferromagnetic-order independent component originating from the interfacial SSW. The coexisting MSHE and SSW, with comparable magnitudes, give rise to the out-of-plane spin polarization. Our study disentangles the origins of spin-torque generation in noncollinear antiferromagnets, providing valuable insights for their spintronic applications.

### [161] [Electron Dynamics Reconstruction and Nontrivial Transport by Acoustic Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24102)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究者开发了一个半经典框架（semiclassical framework），将表面声波重构为准周期势来调制电子动量分布，从而描述电子动力学。该框架在双层石墨烯和MX₂（M = Mo, W; X = S, Se, Te）材料体系中进行了验证。

Conclusion: 角依赖的声电霍尔效应为贝里曲率分布提供了实验探测手段。该半经典框架为理解表面声波驱动的电子输运现象提供了理论基础，超越了传统电场简化模型。

Abstract: Surface acoustic waves (SAWs) become a popular driving source in modern condensed matter physics, but most existing theories simplify them as electric fields and ignore the non-uniform Brillouin zone folding effect. We develop a semiclassical framework and reconstruct the electron dynamics by treating SAW as a quasi-periodic potential modulating electronic momentum distribution. This framework naturally explains the experimentally observed DC drag current and predicts acousto-electric Hall effect. The theory further reveals various SAW-driven transport phenomena, emerging anomalous Hall, thermal Hall, and Nernst effects within time-reversal symmetric systems. Illustrated in bilayer graphene and $\mathrm{MX_2}$ (M = Mo, W; X = S, Se, Te), the angular-dependent acousto-electric Hall effect provides an experimental probe for Berry curvature distribution.

### [162] [Optimized control protocols for stable skyrmion creation using deep reinforcement learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24177)
*Ji Seok Song,Se Kwon Kim,Kyoung-Min Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于深度强化学习（deep reinforcement learning, DRL）的方法，用于寻找优化的动态磁场-温度路径，以在Fe3GeTe2单层中高效生成磁斯格明子（magnetic skyrmions）并增强其热稳定性。

Method: 采用深度强化学习方法，识别能够控制条纹畴不稳定性并增强热稳定性的先进动态磁场-温度路径。该方法通过最小化耗散功（dissipated work）来优化路径，确保驱动的斯格明子状态接近其平衡分布。

Result: 训练后的DRL智能体发现的优化场-温路径，在Fe3GeTe2单层中实现了比先前固定温度场扫描更高的斯格明子形成成功率。生成的斯格明子因其各向同性形状而具有更长的寿命，这倾向于抑制与斯格明子湮灭相关的内部激发模式。

Conclusion: 深度强化学习驱动的搜索简化了斯格明子生成与控制优化协议的识别过程。这些进展源于有针对性地最小化耗散功，通过上限约束Kullback-Leibler散度来确保驱动的斯格明子状态保持接近其平衡分布。

Abstract: Generating stable magnetic skyrmions is essential for the practical application of skyrmion-based spintronic devices in thermally agitating environments. Recent advancements have enabled the creation of skyrmions by controlling stripe domain instability through dynamic magnetic-field control. However, deterministic skyrmion creation and effectively managing the thermal stability of skyrmions remain challenges. Here, we present a deep reinforcement learning (DRL) approach to identify advanced dynamic magnetic-field-temperature paths that create skyrmions while controlling stripe domain instability and enhancing their thermal stability. The trained DRL agent discovers an optimized field-temperature path that achieves a higher success rate for skyrmion formation in Fe3GeTe2 monolayers compared to previous fixed-temperature field sweeps. Additionally, the generated skyrmions exhibit longer lifetimes due to their isotropic shape, which tends to suppress internal excitation modes associated with skyrmion annihilation. We demonstrate that these advancements stem from the targeted minimization of the dissipated work, which ensures that the driven skyrmion states remain close to their equilibrium distributions by upper-bounding the Kullback-Leibler divergence. Our findings suggest that a DRL-powered search streamlines the identification of optimized protocols for skyrmion creation and control.

### [163] [Dipole-exchange spin waves and mode hybridization in magnetic nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24187)
*Fedor Shuklin,Khristina Albitskaya,Sergei Solovyov,Alexander Chernov,Mihail Petrov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究分析了受限铁磁谐振器中自旋波模式在交换主导、交换-偶极和偶极相互作用区域的行为，揭示了对称性分类、简并消除和模式杂化现象，并建立了统一的耦合模式理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于深入理解受限几何形状（球形和圆柱形）铁磁谐振器中自旋波模式在不同相互作用区域（交换主导、交换-偶极和偶极相互作用）的行为特征，特别是对称性对模式分类和简并的影响。

Method: 方法基于线性化的朗道-利夫希茨-吉尔伯特方程（Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation），利用总角动量投影和镜像宇称守恒对称性对模式进行分类。通过数值分析研究偶极相互作用对交换简并的消除作用，并建立了直接基于动力学磁化强度的耦合模式理论。

Result: 结果显示非局域偶极相互作用消除了交换简并并导致模式杂化，在同一对称性扇区内产生避免交叉现象。建立的耦合模式理论将交换-偶极问题简化为有限个相互作用模式的系统，为受限磁性粒子中的自旋波谱提供了统一描述框架。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了从交换极限到偶极区域的统一理论框架，揭示了对称性在自旋波模式分类中的关键作用，以及偶极相互作用如何通过消除简并和促进模式杂化来影响受限磁性粒子的自旋波谱。

Abstract: We investigate spin-wave modes in confined ferromagnetic resonators with spherical and cylindrical geometries across the exchange-dominated, dipole-exchange, and dipolar interaction regimes. Starting from the linearized Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation, we show that the projection of the total angular momentum and mirror parity are conserved quantities in the problem of axially symmetric resonators. These symmetries provide a natural classification of spin-wave modes and explain the degeneracy of exchange modes, as well as its lifting by dipolar interactions. Numerical analysis shows that the nonlocal dipolar interaction removes the exchange degeneracy and hybridizes modes, leading to avoided crossings between modes that belong to the same symmetry sector. To describe this behavior, we develop a coupled-mode theory formulated directly in terms of dynamical magnetization, which reduces the dipole-exchange problem to a finite system of interacting modes. The resulting framework provides a unified description of spin-wave spectra in confined magnetic particles from the exchange limit to the dipolar regime.

</details>


### [164] [Topological insulator single-electron transistors for charge sensing applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24220)
*Omargeldi Atanov,Junya Feng,Jens Brede,Oliver Breunig,Yoichi Ando*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出基于拓扑绝缘体（TI）的单电子晶体管（SET）作为磁场兼容的电荷传感装置，可集成于TI-超导体混合平台。研究观测到清晰的库仑菱形（Coulomb diamonds）结构，并发现库仑共振存在约e/2的电荷偏移，该偏移受轴向磁场调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在开发磁场兼容且易于集成的电荷传感装置，用于拓扑绝缘体-超导体混合平台。建立这种电荷传感能力是实现更复杂TI基混合器件中检测和编织马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）的关键第一步。

Method: 采用拓扑绝缘体基单电子晶体管作为实验平台，通过测量电荷稳定性图（charge-stability diagrams）中的库仑菱形结构来确认电荷量子化和单电子输运。利用轴向磁场调控库仑共振偏移，并通过数值模拟复现观测结果。

Result: 实验观测到清晰的库仑菱形结构，证实了电荷量子化和单电子输运。部分器件中库仑共振出现约e/2的持续偏移，轴向磁场进一步使这些偏移向更高或更低的栅极电压移动。磁场依赖性与SET耦合的陷阱态（trap state）的塞曼位移（Zeeman shift）一致。

Conclusion: 共振偏移被确认为TI-SET器件对邻近电荷敏感性的结果。建立这种电荷传感能力是向更复杂的TI基混合器件中集成TI-SET作为电荷传感器的第一步，最终目标在于检测和编织马约拉纳零模。

Abstract: We present topological insulator (TI)-based single-electron transistors (SETs) as magnetic-field-compatible charge sensing devices that are easily integrable with TI-superconductor hybrid platforms. We observe well-resolved Coulomb diamonds in the charge-stability diagrams of our devices confirming the charge quantization and single-electron transport. In some devices, the Coulomb resonances show persistent shifts corresponding up to $\sim$ e/2 charge. An axial magnetic field further displaces these shifts to higher or lower gate voltages. We find that the axial magnetic-field dependence of the shifts is consistent with the Zeeman shift of a trap state coupled to the SET, and we reproduce the observations using numerical simulations. The resonance shifts are therefore identified as a consequence of the sensitivity of our TI-SET devices to charges in proximity. Establishing this charge sensing capability is a first step toward integrating TI-SETs as charge sensors in more complex TI-based hybrid devices, with the overarching goal of detecting and braiding Majorana zero modes.

### [165] [A material-agnostic platform to probe spin-phonon interactions using high-overtone bulk acoustic wave resonators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24230)
*Q. Greffe,A. Hugot,S. Zhang,J. Jarreau,L. Del-Rey,E. Bonet,F. Balestro,T. Chanelière,J. J. Viennot*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在毫开尔文温度和千兆赫频率下探测自旋-声子耦合的新技术，通过将高次体声波谐振器（HBARs）与任意晶体集成，实现了对钨酸钙和正硅酸钇中自旋-声子相互作用的直接表征。

Method: 引入了一种在毫开尔文温度和千兆赫频率下探测自旋-声子耦合的技术，通过粘弹性转移薄膜铌酸锂换能器将高次体声波谐振器（high-overtone bulk acoustic wave resonators, HBARs）与任意晶体集成。通过将稀薄自旋系综的拉莫尔频率调谐至与HBAR模式共振，从声学色散和耗散测量中提取自旋-声子相互作用的各向异性和强度。

Result: 在钨酸钙（CaWO₄）和正硅酸钇（Y₂SiO₅）中验证了该方法，实现了铒掺杂系综高达0.5的合作度。该方法能够以最小的制备约束研究复杂晶体材料中的自旋-声子相互作用。

Conclusion: 该技术为研究复杂晶体材料中的自旋-声子相互作用提供了新途径，将促进混合量子系统的设计和寻找具有增强自旋-声子耦合的离子-基质组合。

Abstract: Spin-phonon interactions have a dual role in emerging spin-based quantum technologies. While they can be a limitation to device performance through decoherence, they also serve as a critical resource for coherent spin control, detection, and the realization of spin-based quantum networks. However, their direct characterization remains a challenge and is usually material-dependent. Here, we introduce a technique to probe spin-phonon coupling at millikelvin temperatures and gigahertz frequencies, using high-overtone bulk acoustic wave resonators (HBARs) integrated with arbitrary crystals via visco-elastic transfer of thin-film lithium niobate transducers. By tuning the Larmor frequency of dilute spin ensembles into resonance with HBAR modes, we extract the anisotropy and strength of spin-phonon interactions from acoustic dispersion and dissipation measurements. We demonstrate this approach in calcium tungstate (CaWO4) and yttrium orthosilicate (Y2SiO5), achieving cooperativities up to 0.5 for erbium dopant ensembles. Our method enables the study of spin-phonon interactions in complex crystalline materials, with minimal fabrication constraints. These results will facilitate the design of hybrid quantum systems and the quest for ion-matrix combination with enhanced spin-phonon coupling.

### [166] [Fragile topology for six-fold rotation symmetry indicated by the concentric Wilson loop spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24412)
*Xinyang Li,Lumen Eek,Jasper van Wezel,Cristiane Morais Smith*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有p6对称性（由三角形和六边形组成的二维几何结构）晶格中Haldane模型和Kane-Mele模型的拓扑相变，探索不同对称性条件下拓扑不变量的计算方法及其有效性。

Method: 对于破坏时间反演对称性的Haldane模型，采用多带非阿贝尔Wilson loop形式计算陈数（Chern number）；对于保持时间反演对称性的Kane-Mele模型，计算Concentric Wilson Loop Spectrum（CWLS）中的π-交叉数量。

Result: Haldane模型通过独立调节三角和六边形跳跃参数产生多种拓扑相，加入次次近邻跳跃后相图更加丰富，出现高陈数区域；Kane-Mele模型中，CWLS不变量识别的拓扑性质具有脆弱性，挑战了其作为强不变量的传统认知。

Conclusion: CWLS方法适用于具有时间反演和旋转对称性但缺乏其他对称性的系统，但对于研究的6重对称性模型，该方法识别的拓扑性质是脆弱的，这对该不变量在拓扑绝缘体完整分类中作为强不变量的地位提出了质疑。

Abstract: We investigate topological phase transitions for the Haldane and Kane-Mele model in a lattice with $p6$ symmetry, which consists of triangles and hexagons arranged in a two-dimensional geometry. For the Haldane model, which breaks time-reversal symmetry, we calculate the Chern number using a multi-band non-Abelian Wilson loop formalism. By varying the hopping parameters in the triangles and hexagons independently, a large variety of topological phases emerge. In the presence of a next-next-nearest neighbor hopping, the phase diagram becomes even richer, with regions exhibiting high Chern numbers. Then, we consider the Kane-Mele model, for which time-reversal symmetry is preserved, and calculate the number of $π$-crossings in the Concentric Wilson Loop Spectrum (CWLS). This method is appropriate to determine the topological invariant for systems hosting time-reversal and rotational symmetry, but lacking all other symmetries. According to a classification based on $K$-theory, the CWLS invariant reveals topological properties even when more conventional invariants fail to detect them. The formalism was previously successfully applied to systems with 3- and 4-fold symmetry. Here, we surprisingly find that for the 6-fold-symmetry model investigated, the topology identified by this invariant is fragile, therefore questioning the claim that this should be the strong invariant missing in a complete classification of topological insulators.

### [167] [Tunable linear polarization of interface excitons at lateral heterojunctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24471)
*M. V. Durnev,D. S. Smirnov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究建立了过渡金属二硫化物单层横向异质结界面激子的偏振光致发光理论，揭示了有限波矢下光学选择规则的修正导致激子光致发光产生线性偏振，偏振度可达10%以上，且可通过面内电场调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解横向异质结界面激子的偏振光致发光特性，特别是有限波矢下光学选择规则的修正如何导致线性偏振的产生，这对于界面激子的光学性质调控具有重要意义。

Method: 采用微观变分方法（microscopic variational approach）分析界面激子的偏振光致发光，考虑电子和空穴色散的三角扭曲（trigonal warping）以及有效质量的能量依赖性两个微观机制。

Result: 研究发现线性偏振度在现实异质结构中可超过10%，偏振的大小和角度受两个微观机制的相互作用控制，且与界面晶体学取向有明确依赖关系；界面激子的大固有偶极矩使其光学响应可通过面内电场调控。

Conclusion: 该理论揭示了界面激子偏振光致发光的微观机制，证明了线性偏振的可观程度和电场可调性，为基于过渡金属二硫化物异质结的光电器件设计提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We develop a theory of polarized photoluminescence of interface excitons localized at lateral heterojunctions between transition metal dichalcogenide monolayers. We show that the circular selection rules governing interband optical transitions exactly at the band extrema are modified at finite wave vectors. The corresponding wave-vector-dependent corrections to the optical matrix elements result in a net linear polarization of excitonic photoluminescence. We identify two microscopic mechanisms responsible for linear polarization$-$trigonal warping of the electron and hole dispersions and the energy dependence of the effective masses. Their interplay controls both the magnitude and the angle of the emitted light polarization, with distinct dependences on the crystallographic orientation of the interface. Using a microscopic variational approach, we demonstrate that the degree of linear polarization can reach values exceeding 10% in realistic heterostructures. Furthermore, due to the large built-in dipole moment of interface excitons, their optical response can be tuned by an external in-plane electric field, enabling control over the strength and direction of the polarization.

### [168] [Robust valley-polarized excitonic Mott states and doublons enabled by stacking-controlled moiré geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24494)
*Hao-Tien Chu,Shou-Chien Chiu,Meng-Che Yeh,Yu-Wei Hsieh,Jia-Sian Su,Xiao-Wei Zhang,Jie-Yong Zeng,Po-Chun Huang,Si-Jie Chang,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Yunbo Ou,Seth Ariel Tongay,Ting Cao,Chaw-Keong Yong*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了通过增强相邻莫尔晶胞间的激子排斥相互作用（V_xx）来稳定单位填充激子莫特态的新途径。在H堆叠WSe2/WS2中，莫尔限域赋予层间激子面外偶极和显著的面内四极电荷分布，使V_xx至少增加两倍，从而产生长寿命（~12 ns）的谷极化激子莫特态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子级薄的莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattices）为研究相互作用玻色子提供了光学可及平台，其中强在位排斥（U_xx）抑制双占据并支持单位填充的激子莫特态（exciton Mott states）。然而，莫尔限域也增强了声子和无序辅助的弛豫，挑战了这些关联态在耗散下的鲁棒性。

Method: 采用螺旋度分辨瞬态光致发光（helicity-resolved transient photoluminescence）技术，结合基于第一性原理的建模（first-principles-informed modelling），研究H堆叠WSe2/WS2中激子的相互作用。通过分析激子的面外偶极和面内四极电荷分布（quadrupolar charge distribution）几何结构对相互作用的影响。

Result: 四极几何结构使单位填充下的V_xx相对于偶极R堆叠激子至少增加两倍。尽管U_xx略有降低，增强的V_xx产生了长寿命（~12 ns）、谷极化（valley-polarized）的激子莫特态，其寿命是R堆叠的两倍以上，且在~50 K下保持鲁棒。超过单位填充时，相同几何结构支持谷极化双激子（doublons），寿命比R堆叠长四倍。

Conclusion: 研究结果确立了莫尔几何结构对位点间相互作用（intersite interactions）的控制作为稳定激子莫特态和双激子抵抗固体中耗散的有效途径。这为通过调控激子间相互作用几何结构来增强关联量子态的鲁棒性提供了新策略。

Abstract: Atomically-thin moiré superlattices offer an optically accessible platform for interacting bosons, where strong onsite repulsion $U_{xx}$ suppresses double occupancy and supports excitonic Mott states at unit filling. However, moiré confinement also enhances phonon- and disorder-assisted relaxation, challenging the robustness of these correlated states under dissipation. Here we show that strengthening the intersite exciton repulsion $V_{xx}$ between neighboring moiré cells offers a distinct route to stabilizing unit-filling excitonic Mott states. In H-stacked WSe2/WS2, moiré confinement endows interlayer excitons with an out-of-plane dipole and a pronounced in-plane quadrupolar charge distribution. Helicity-resolved transient photoluminescence, supported by first-principles-informed modelling, reveals that this quadrupolar geometry increases $V_{xx}$ at unit filling by at least a factor of two relative to the dipolar R-stacked excitons. Despite a slight reduction in $U_{xx}$, the enhanced $V_{xx}$ yields a long-lived, valley-polarized excitonic Mott state at unit filling that persists for ~12 ns - more than twice as long as in R-stacks - and remains robust up to ~50 K. Beyond unit filling, the same geometry supports valley-polarized doublons with fourfold longer lifetimes than in R-stacks. These results establish moiré-geometric control of intersite interactions as a route to stabilizing excitonic Mott states and doublons against dissipation in solids.

While $Bi_4Te_3$ is a promising candidate due to its dual topological phases, acting as both a strong topological insulator and a topological crystalline insulator, high-quality growth remains challenging due to a narrow stoichiometric window and high sensitivity to surface kinetics. Here, we establish a reproducible molecular beam epitaxy (MBE) process to produce stoichiometric, twin-free $Bi_4Te_3$ thin films with ultra-smooth surfaces and atomically sharp van der Waals stacks. By employing selective area epitaxy (SAE), we realize laterally confined $Bi_4Te_3$ nanostructures that exhibit a feature-dependent stoichiometric deviation. This phenomenon, which we term the selective stoichiometric shift, arises from the unequal lateral diffusion of Bi and Te adatoms, revealing a direct coupling between adatom kinetics and nanoscale compositional stability. Atomic-resolution imaging further uncovers asymmetric van der Waals gaps within the stacking sequence, identifying an intrinsic structural asymmetry between the quintuple and bilayer units. These findings provide fundamental insights into the crystallization of Bi_4Te_3$ and demonstrate a scalable route for integrating functional topological materials into next-generation superconducting hybrid quantum circuits.

### [170] [Energy-gap--controlled current oscillations in graphene under periodic driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24547)
*Hasna Chnafa,Clarence Cortes,David Laroze,Ahmed Jellal*

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了诱导质量项Δ对石墨烯中约瑟夫森类电流振荡的影响，揭示了Δ作为可调参数控制电流振幅、符号和共振结构的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解诱导质量项Δ如何影响石墨烯在时空周期势U(x,t)下的电流密度，探索光-物质相互作用和量子输运的可调特性。

Method: 通过求解狄拉克方程（Dirac equation），推导准能谱（quasi-energy spectrum）和相应的本征旋量（eigenspinors），获得电流密度的显式解析表达式。

Result: Δ作为可调控制参数，调控约瑟夫森类电流振荡（Josephson-like current oscillations）的振幅、符号和共振结构。在正常入射和纯时间周期势下，能隙内的振荡随Δ增加而减弱；在时空周期势下，电流密度可正可负且随时间衰减，共振现象随Δ增大而减弱。

Conclusion: 研究强调了带隙石墨烯中光-物质相互作用和量子输运的可调性，为太赫兹（THz）纳米电子器件和光控量子开关提供了潜在应用前景。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of an induced mass term $Δ$ on the current density in graphene subjected to a space- and time-dependent periodic potential $U(x,t)$. By solving the Dirac equation and deriving both the quasi-energy spectrum and the corresponding eigenspinors, we obtain explicit analytical expressions for the current density, which exhibits a clear dependence on $Δ$. We show that $Δ$ acts as a tunable control parameter that governs the amplitude, sign, and resonance structure of Josephson-like current oscillations. For normal incidence and a purely time-periodic potential, our results reveal that the oscillations within the energy gap gradually diminish as the mass term $Δ$ increases. This suppression leads to a weakening of the Josephson-like effect typically observed in such systems. When the potential $U(x,t)$ is periodic in both space and time, the behavior becomes more complex. The current density can take either positive or negative values depending on the magnitude of the induced gap, and it generally decreases over time. As a result, the resonance phenomena--prominent at lower gap values--become progressively less significant as $Δ$ increases. These findings underscore the tunable nature of light-matter interactions and quantum transport in gapped graphene, suggesting potential applications in terahertz (THz) nanoelectronic devices and optically controlled quantum switches.

</details>


### [171] [Interlayer Coupling and Floquet-Driven Topological Phases in Bilayer Haldane Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24551)
*Imtiaz Khan,Muzamil Shah,Reza Asgari,Gao Xianlong*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了具有可调层内跳跃各向异性的AB堆叠双层Haldane晶格中的Floquet驱动拓扑相变，通过层间杂化、Haldane通量和非共振圆偏振光的组合，实现了Dirac、半Dirac和高陈数绝缘相之间的可控转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索双层几何结构如何通过层间耦合和光驱动扩展Floquet拓扑控制的范围，实现动态可调的高陈数相和谷依赖的霍尔响应。

Method: 研究方法结合了层间杂化（interlayer hybridization）、Haldane通量和非共振圆偏振光（off-resonant circularly polarized light），在具有可调层内跳跃各向异性的AB堆叠双层Haldane晶格中研究拓扑相变。

Result: 随着跳跃各向异性增加，两个不等价的Dirac点相互靠近并在布里渊区M点合并，形成半Dirac色散；本征Haldane质量与Floquet诱导质量之间的竞争驱动了一系列尖锐的拓扑相变，陈数（Chern numbers）为C=0,±1,±2；层间耦合通过诱导螺旋依赖和谷选择的能带反转，稳定了价带中的高陈数相。

Conclusion: 双层几何结构通过层间耦合和光螺旋性（light helicity）调控，扩展了Floquet拓扑控制的范围，实现了动态可调的高陈数相和谷依赖的霍尔响应；当系统接近半Dirac极限时，拓扑相空间变窄并在临界合并点消失。

Abstract: We investigate Floquet-driven topological phase transitions in an AB-stacked bilayer Haldane lattice with tunable intralayer hopping anisotropy. By combining interlayer hybridization, Haldane flux, and off-resonant circularly polarized light, we obtain controlled transitions among Dirac, semi-Dirac, and higher-Chern insulating phases. As the hopping anisotropy increases, the two inequivalent Dirac points move toward each other and merge at the Brillouin-zone $\mathbf{M}$ point, where a semi-Dirac dispersion emerges with linear and quadratic momentum dependence along orthogonal directions. In this regime, competition between the intrinsic Haldane mass and the Floquet-induced mass drives a sequence of sharp topological transitions with Chern numbers $C=0,\pm1,\pm2$. We further show that interlayer coupling qualitatively reshapes the Floquet band topology by inducing helicity-dependent and valley-selective band inversions at the K and K$'$ points, thereby stabilizing higher-Chern phases in the valence bands. These changes are accompanied by redistribution of the Berry curvature, bulk gap closings, and the collapse or sign reversal of quantized anomalous Hall plateaus. As the system approaches the semi-Dirac limit, the topological phase space narrows and disappears at the critical merger point, beyond which the system becomes topologically trivial even when it remains gapped. Overall, the bilayer geometry broadens the scope of Floquet topological control by enabling dynamically tunable higher-Chern phases and valley-dependent Hall responses governed by interlayer coupling and light helicity.

</details>

### [172] [A Theory of LLM Information Susceptibility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23626)
*Zhuo-Yang Song,Hua Xing Zhu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被部署为智能体系统中的优化模块，但此类LLM介导改进的基本限制仍未被充分理解。需要建立理论框架来阐明LLM介入何时有效、何时无效。

Method: 提出LLM信息敏感性（information susceptibility）理论，围绕核心假设构建多变量效用函数框架，将假设推广到具有多个共变预算通道的架构。通过跨越一个数量级模型规模的结构多样化领域进行实证验证。

Result: 实证验证表明，嵌套共缩放（nested, co-scaling）架构能超越敏感性边界，开启固定配置无法获得的响应通道。统计物理工具能为AI系统设计提供预测性约束。

Conclusion: 理论阐明了LLM介入何时有帮助、何时无效。如果敏感性假设普遍成立，嵌套架构可能是开放式智能体自我改进的必要结构条件。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as optimization modules in agentic systems, yet the fundamental limits of such LLM-mediated improvement remain poorly understood. Here we propose a theory of LLM information susceptibility, centred on the hypothesis that when computational resources are sufficiently large, the intervention of a fixed LLM does not increase the performance susceptibility of a strategy set with respect to budget. We develop a multi-variable utility-function framework that generalizes this hypothesis to architectures with multiple co-varying budget channels, and discuss the conditions under which co-scaling can exceed the susceptibility bound. We validate the theory empirically across structurally diverse domains and model scales spanning an order of magnitude, and show that nested, co-scaling architectures open response channels unavailable to fixed configurations. These results clarify when LLM intervention helps and when it does not, demonstrating that tools from statistical physics can provide predictive constraints for the design of AI systems. If the susceptibility hypothesis holds generally, the theory suggests that nested architectures may be a necessary structural condition for open-ended agentic self-improvement.

Abstract: We present the first joint gravitational-wave cosmological inference with LISA extreme mass-ratio inspirals at $z\lesssim1$ (galaxy redshifts) and massive black hole binaries at $z\gtrsim1$ (electromagnetic counterparts). ### [175] [Perturbative and numerical study of nonlinear relativistic effects in weak lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24179)
*Matteo Magi,Francesca Lepori,Julian Adamek*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文指出标准弱引力透镜（weak lensing）形式在二阶扰动理论中存在不完整性，通过雅可比映射（Jacobi map）形式推导了旋转场和剪切B模（shear B-modes）的角功率谱，发现Sachs基矢（Sachs basis）的平行输运会打破旋转与剪切B模的谱简并性，并首次解析推导了参考系拖曳（frame dragging）对剪切B模功率谱的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准弱引力透镜形式假设透镜映射仅依赖于偏转角，但本文证明这一描述在二阶扰动理论中是不完整的，即使在一阶仅存在标量扰动的情况下也是如此。研究旨在完善弱引力透镜的理论框架，特别是考虑相对论性高阶效应。

Method: 采用雅可比映射形式（Jacobi map formalism），在相对论性扰动理论（relativistic perturbation theory）的二阶水平上推导了旋转场、剪切B模及其角功率谱（angular power spectra）的表达式。通过数值量化修正，并首次解析推导了参考系拖曳效应的影响。

Result: 当一致考虑Sachs基矢的平行输运时，旋转与剪切B模的谱简并性被打破，在红移z_s=0.5、大角尺度ℓ∼5处发现约5%的差异。参考系拖曳效应在尺度ℓ≲10时成为剪切B模功率谱的主导贡献。虽然这些非线性相对论修正对观测星系椭圆率的影响约为1%，但相对论性弱透镜观测模拟支持了这些结果。

Conclusion: 标准弱引力透镜形式在二阶扰动理论中存在不完整性，Sachs基矢的平行输运和参考系拖曳效应显著影响大尺度剪切B模，但这些非线性相对论修正的实际探测具有挑战性。研究为弱引力透镜的完整理论描述提供了重要进展。

Abstract: The standard weak lensing formalism assumes that the lensing map relating the observed image of a source to its intrinsic shape depends only on the deflection angle. We show that this description is incomplete beyond linear perturbation theory, even when only scalar perturbations are present at first order. Using the Jacobi map formalism, we derive expressions for the rotation field, shear B-modes, and their angular power spectra at second order in relativistic perturbation theory. In the standard formalism, rotation and shear B-modes share the same spectrum, however, this degeneracy is broken once the parallel transport of the Sachs basis is consistently taken into account. We quantify this correction numerically, finding a difference of about $5\%$ on large angular scales $\ell \sim 5$ for sources at redshift $z_\mathrm{s} = 0.5$. We also investigate frame-dragging effects, which are usually neglected in weak lensing. We present the first analytical derivation of the corresponding impact on the angular power spectrum of shear B-modes and show that it becomes the dominant contribution on scales $\ell \lesssim 10$. While both Sachs-basis rotation and frame dragging significantly affect shear B-modes on large scales, their effect on the observed galaxy ellipticity is of order $1\%$, making these nonlinear relativistic corrections challenging to detect in practice. Our results are supported by relativistic simulations of weak lensing observables, including the first numerical study of frame dragging in the power spectra of the lensing convergence and cosmic shear.

</details>


### [176] [Probing Interacting Dark Sectors with upcoming Post-Reionization and Galaxy Surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24554)
*Rahul Shah,Antara Dey,Purba Mukherjee,Supratik Pal*

TL;DR: 该研究通过生成SKA-mid和Euclid未来观测的模拟数据集，预测了这些调查对相互作用暗能量（interacting dark energy）与暗物质（dark matter）之间耦合参数的约束能力。结果显示，SKA2能提供最严格的约束，特别是对相互作用强度（interaction strength）的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法基于当前观测边界获得的基准值，生成了SKA-mid的21厘米强度映射（21-cm intensity mapping）、星系成团（galaxy clustering）和宇宙剪切（cosmic shear）观测的模拟数据集，以及Euclid任务的大尺度巡天模拟数据。随后使用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov chain Monte Carlo）分析，将当前宇宙学数据与这些模拟数据集结合进行参数约束预测。

Conclusion: 结论强调了这些即将到来的巡天项目在探测暗区内部相互作用方面的潜力。SKA2在约束相互作用强度方面表现最优，而Euclid的约束能力与SKA1相当，两者都将显著提升对暗能量-暗物质相互作用参数的测量精度。

Abstract: We investigate the constraining power of future post-reionization and galaxy surveys on possible interactions between dynamical dark energy and dark matter. The analysis focuses on the interaction strength and the dark energy equation of state parameters, in addition to the six standard cosmological parameters. Using fiducial values obtained from the current observational bounds (Planck 2018 + DESI DR2 + Pantheon+), mock datasets for upcoming 21-cm intensity mapping, galaxy clustering and cosmic shear observations from the SKA-mid, and for the upcoming large-scale survey from the Euclid mission, were generated. Subsequently, Markov chain Monte Carlo analyses combining current cosmological data with these mock datasets were performed to forecast parameter constraints. The results indicate that both SKA-mid and Euclid observations can significantly improve constraints on interacting dark sector parameters. In particular, the interaction strength and dark energy equation of state parameters can be constrained considerably tighter than current combined constraints from Planck 2018, DESI DR2 and Pantheon+. Comparing different probe combinations and survey configurations, it is found that SKA2 provides the tightest projected constraints, particularly on the interaction strength, while Euclid achieves a precision broadly comparable to that of SKA1. The results highlight the potential of these upcoming surveys to probe interactions within the dark sector.

### [177] [Dynamical Systems in Cosmology: Reviewing An Alternative Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24568)
*Nandan Roy,L. Arturo Ureña-López*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 文章首先介绍了宇宙学中广泛使用的标准动力系统工具包，然后转向基于极坐标（polar）和双曲变量（hyperbolic variable）变换的替代公式。这些方法将均匀各向同性宇宙学的控制方程自然地表述为常微分方程组，使其成为动力系统分析的理想领域。

Result: 这些方法为探索广泛的标量场暗能量模型提供了强大的新途径，能够设定和约束初始条件，并分析各类势能中的追踪行为（tracking behavior）。

Conclusion: 该综述是自包含的，但始终引导读者在需要时参考更专业和深入的处理方法。动力系统方法已成为研究暗能量动力学特性的重要工具，为理解宇宙演化提供了新的分析框架。

Abstract: Dark energy is one of the deepest puzzles in modern cosmology, and mounting evidence suggests that it is not just a cosmological constant but a genuinely dynamical component. Although cosmology and dynamical systems theory emerged from different disciplines, dynamical systems methods have become essential tools to uncover the qualitative evolution of the universe. The equations governing homogeneous and isotropic cosmologies can be naturally written as systems of ordinary differential equations, making them an ideal arena for dynamical system analysis. This review begins with a sharp, streamlined introduction to the standard dynamical systems toolkit widely used in cosmology. We then move on to alternative formulations based on polar and hyperbolic variable transformations. These approaches unlock powerful new ways to probe a broad spectrum of scalar field dark energy models, to set and constrain initial conditions, and to analyze tracking behavior across wide classes of potentials. The review is self-contained, but consistently directs the reader to more specialized and in-depth treatments where needed.

### [178] [Restoring missing low scattering angle data in two-dimensional diffraction patterns of isolated molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24334)
*Yanwei Xiong,Martin Centurion*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种迭代算法，用于恢复二维衍射信号中低散射角区域的缺失数据，这对于获得实空间表示至关重要。该算法通过傅里叶变换和阿贝尔变换在动量转移域与实空间域之间转换信号，并应用实空间约束来检索缺失信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 各向异性二维衍射信号比传统各向同性信号包含更多信息，但由于使用线偏振激光激发样品会在分子上印刻空间各向异性，这些信号在典型的时间分辨衍射实验中很常见。然而，低散射角区域的缺失数据限制了获得完整实空间表示的能力。

Method: 提出了一种迭代算法，通过在动量转移域（momentum transfer domain）和实空间域（real space domain）之间通过傅里叶变换（Fourier transform）和阿贝尔变换（Abel transform）来回转换二维信号，并应用实空间约束来检索低散射角的缺失信号。该算法仅需要分子中最短和最长核间距的近似先验知识。

Result: 在模拟图案和实验测量的三氟碘甲烷分子激光诱导排列衍射图案中，成功检索到了缺失信号。这表明该算法能够有效恢复二维衍射信号中低散射角区域的缺失数据。

Conclusion: 该迭代算法为恢复二维衍射信号中低散射角区域的缺失数据提供了一种有效方法，这对于获得完整的实空间表示至关重要，特别是在使用线偏振激光激发样品的超快电子和X射线衍射实验中。

Abstract: Anisotropic two-dimensional diffraction signals contain more information than the conventional isotropic signals for both gas phase ultrafast electron and X-ray diffraction experiments and are common in typical time-resolved diffraction experiments due to the use of linearly polarized lasers to excite the sample that imprints spatial anisotropy on the molecules. We report an iterative algorithm to restore the missing data at low scattering angles in a two-dimensional diffraction signal, which is essential to obtain real-space representation. The iterative algorithm transforms two-dimensional signals back and forth between the momentum transfer domain and the real space domain through Fourier and Abel transforms and apply real space constraints to retrieve missing signal at low scattering angles. The algorithm only requires an approximate a-priori knowledge of the shortest and longest internuclear distances in the molecule. We demonstrated successful retrieval of the missing signal in simulated patterns and in experimentally measured diffraction patterns from laser-induced alignment of trifluoroiodomethane molecules.

</details>


### [179] [Collective Electronic Polarization Drives Charge Asymmetry at Oil-Water Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24142)
*Gabriele Amante,Klaudia Mrazikova,Gabriele Centi,Sylvie Roke,Ali Hassanali,Giuseppe Cassone*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过神经网络深度势能分子动力学与数据驱动信息论方法，揭示了油水界面自发负电荷产生的微观机制。研究发现扩展界面存在系统性电子不对称性，导致从水相到烃相的平均净电荷转移，产生约0.006 e⁻/nm²的表面电荷密度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 油滴在水中自发获得负电荷的现象是界面科学中长期激烈争论的问题。理解这一基本界面现象的微观机制对于界面科学和胶体化学具有重要意义。

Method: 采用基于神经网络的深度势能分子动力学（deep potential molecular dynamics）与数据驱动的信息论方法，探测扩展癸烷-水界面（decane-water interface）的真实空间电子密度。

Result: 扩展界面显示系统性电子不对称性，产生从水相到烃相的平均净电荷转移（net charge transfer），在油相产生约0.006 e⁻/nm²的表面电荷密度。这种不平衡伴随着更大的相内自极化（intra-phase self-polarization），特别是烃相内，表明集体多体极化（collective many-body polarization）主导界面电子响应。

Conclusion: 结构分析揭示了前向C-H···O与后向O-H···C基元的不对称性，为相间净电荷转移提供了微观起源。水O-H和癸烷C-H共价键的微妙收缩源于对界面电荷分离层的响应，这些特征与油水界面形成的弱非正常氢键（improper hydrogen-bonds）导致C-H模式蓝移完全一致。

Abstract: Why kinetically stable oil droplets in water spontaneously acquire a negative charge remains one of the most vigorously debated questions in interfacial science. Here, we combine neural-network based deep potential molecular dynamics with a data-driven and information theory approach to probe the real-space electron density at an extended decane-water interface. While decane-water clusters show nearly symmetric forward and backward charge transfer (CT) and thus negligible net CT, the extended interface displays a systematic electronic asymmetry, yielding a net CT from water to the hydrocarbon phase producing an average surface charge density of $\sim0.006~e^{-}\,\mathrm{nm}^{-2}$ on the oil phase. This imbalance is accompanied by much larger intra-phase self-polarization, particularly within the hydrocarbon phase, demonstrating that collective many-body polarization dominates the interfacial electronic response. Structural analysis reveals an asymmetry between forward C--H$\cdots$O and backward O--H$\cdots$C motifs, providing a microscopic origin for a net CT from one phase to the other. Curiously, both the water O--H and decane C--H covalent bonds incur subtle contractions which originate from a response to the charge-separation layers at the interface. These features are fully consistent with the weak improper hydrogen-bonds forming at the oil-water interface that results in blue-shifts of the C-H modes.

</details>


<div id='math.DS'></div>

# math.DS [[Back]](#toc)

### [180] [Spectral Rigidity and Geometric Localization of Hopf Bifurcations in Planar Predator-Prey Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24418)
*E. Chan-López,A. Martín-Ruiz,Víctor Castellanos*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 该论文识别了平面捕食者-猎物系统中Hopf和Bogdanov-Takens分岔位置的几何原理：共存平衡点的猎物坐标位于猎物零倾线（nullcline）的相邻临界点之间，这一现象源于零倾线临界点处的谱刚性（spectral rigidity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究平面捕食者-猎物系统中Hopf和Bogdanov-Takens分岔位置的几何规律，旨在揭示零倾线临界点对分岔位置的约束机制，理解谱刚性现象如何组织系统的分岔结构。

Method: 通过代数机制分析零倾线临界点对雅可比矩阵（Jacobian）的约束作用，在三个具有不同零倾线几何特征的模型族（二次型Bazykin模型、三次型Holling IV型收获模型、有理型Crowley-Martin功能反应）中建立该原理，并扩展到离散时间系统。

Result: 发现共存平衡点经历分岔时，其猎物坐标总是位于猎物零倾线的相邻临界点之间；零倾线临界点处导数消失导致雅可比矩阵约束，阻碍分岔所需谱条件的满足，形成谱刚性；该原理在连续和离散系统中均成立，呈现连续-离散对偶性。

Conclusion: 零倾线临界点作为谱屏障组织分岔结构，该定位原理适用于一般光滑猎物零倾线；研究揭示了分岔位置的几何约束机制，为理解捕食者-猎物系统的动力学行为提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We identify a geometric principle governing the location of Hopf and Bogdanov--Takens bifurcations in planar predator--prey systems. The prey coordinate of any coexistence equilibrium undergoing such a bifurcation lies between consecutive critical points of the prey nullcline. The mechanism is algebraic. At critical points of the nullcline, the vanishing of its derivative induces constraints on the Jacobian that prevent the spectral conditions required for bifurcation from being satisfied. We refer to this phenomenon as \emph{spectral rigidity}. The principle is established for three model families and one discrete counterpart with qualitatively different nullcline geometries: a quadratic case (Bazykin model), a cubic case (Holling type~IV with harvesting), and a rational case (Crowley--Martin functional response). In each case, the localization follows from explicit parametric characterizations and symbolic reduction. The analysis extends to discrete-time systems. For a map obtained by forward Euler discretization of the Crowley--Martin model, the Neimark--Sacker bifurcation occurs on the descending branch of the nullcline, providing a continuous--discrete duality governed by the same mechanism. We conjecture that this localization holds for general smooth prey nullclines, with critical points acting as spectral barriers that organise the bifurcation structure.

</details>
